manave vācaspataye śukrāya parāśarāya sa-sutāya / cāṇakyāya ca viduṣe namo 'stu naya-śāstra-kartṛbhyaḥ // 0.1	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
sakalārtha-śāstra-sāraṃ jagati samālokya viṣṇuśarmedam / tantraiḥ pañcabhir etac cakāra sumanoharaṃ śāstram // 0.2	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
ajāta-mṛta-mūrkhebhyo mṛtājātau sutau varam / yatas tau svalpa-duḥkhāya yāvaj-jīvaṃ jaḍo dahet // 0.3	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
varaṃ garbha-sravo varam ṛtuṣu naivābhigamanaṃ varaṃ jātaḥ preto varam api ca kanyaiva janitā / varaṃ bandhyā bhāryā varam api ca garbheṣu vasatir na cāvidagdhān rūpa-draviṇa-guṇa-yukto 'pi tanayaḥ // 0.4	śikhariṇī [17: ymnsBlg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
kiṃ tayā kriyate dhenvā yā na sūte na dugdhadā / ko 'rthaḥ putreṇa jātena yo na vidvān na bhaktimān // 0.5	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anantapāraṃ kila śabda-śāstraṃ svalpaṃ tathāyur bahavaś ca vighnāḥ / sāraṃ tato grāhyam apāsya phalgu haṃsair yathā kṣīram ivāmbudhyāt // 0.6	indravajrā [11: ttjgg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
adhīte ya idaṃ nityaṃ nīti-śāstraṃ śṛṇoti ca / na parābhavam āpnoti śakrād api kadācana // 0.7	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vardhamāno mahān snehaḥ siṃha-go-vṛṣayor vane / piśunenātilubdhena jambukena vināśitaḥ // 1.1	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nahi tad vidyate kiṃcid yad arthena na siddhyati / yatnena matimāṃs tasmād artham ekaṃ prasādhayet // 1.2	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasyāryas tasya mitrāṇi yasyārthās tasya bāndhavāḥ / yasyārthāḥ sa pumāṃ loke yasyārthāḥ sa ca paṇḍitaḥ // 1.3	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na sā vidyā na tad dānaṃ na tac chilpaṃ na sā kalā / na tat sthairyaṃ hi dhanināṃ yācakair yan na gīyate // 1.4	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
iha loke hi dhanināṃ paro 'pi svajanāyate / svajano 'pi daridrāṇāṃ sarvadā durjanāyate // 1.5	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthebhyo 'pi hi vṛddhebhyaḥ saṃvṛttebhya itas tataḥ / pravartante kriyāḥ sarvāḥ parvatebhya ivāpagāḥ // 1.6	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pūjyate yad apūjyo 'pi yad agamyo 'pi gamyate / vandyate yad avandyo 'pi sa prabhāvo dhanasya ca // 1.7	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aśanād indriyāṇīva syuḥ kāryāṇy akhilāny api / etasmāt kāraṇād vittaṃ sarva-sādhanam ucyate // 1.8	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthārthī jīva-loko 'yaṃ śmaśānam api sevate / tyaktvā janayitāraṃ svaṃ niḥsvaṃ yacchati dūrataḥ // 1.9	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gata-vayasām api puṃsāṃ yeṣām arthā bhavanti te taruṇāḥ / arthe tu ye hīnā vṛddhās te yauvane'pi syuḥ // 1.10	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
kṛtā bhikṣānekair vitarati nṛpo nocitam aho kṛṣiḥ kliṣṭā vidyā guru-vinaya-vṛttyātiviṣamā / kusīdād dāridryaṃ parakaragata-granthi-śamanān na manye vāṇijyāt kim api paramaṃ vartanam iha // 1.11	śikhariṇī [17: ymnsBlg]
upāyānāṃ ca sarveṣām upāyaḥ paṇya-saṃgrahaḥ / dhanārthaṃ śasyate he ekas tad-anyaḥ saṃśayātmakaḥ // 1.12	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
paṇyānāṃ gāndhikaṃ paṇyaṃ kim anyaiḥ kāñcanādibhiḥ / yatraikena ca yat krītaṃ tac chatena pradīyate // 1.13	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nikṣepe patite harmye śreṣṭhī stauti sva-devatām / nikṣepī mriyate tubhyaṃ pradāsyāmy upayācitam // 1.14	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
goṣṭhika-karma-niyuktaḥ śreṣṭhī cintayati cetasā hṛṣṭaḥ / vasudhā vasu-sampūrṇā mayādya labdhā kim anyena // 1.15	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
paricitam āgacchantaṃ grāhakam utkaṇṭhyā vilokayāsau / hṛṣyati tad-dhana-labdho yadvat putreṇa jātena // 1.16	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
anyac ca- pūrṇāpūrṇe māne paricita-jana-vañcanaṃ tathā nityam / mithyā-krayasya kathanaṃ prakṛtir iyaṃ syāt kirātānām // 1.17	ajñātasamavṛtta [6: tm] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
dviguṇaṃ triguṇaṃ vittaṃ bhāṇḍa-kraya-vicakṣaṇāḥ / prāpnuvanty udyamāl lokā dūra-deśāntaraṃ gatāḥ // 1.18	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na svalpasya kṛte bhūri nāśayen matimān naraḥ / etad evātra pāṇḍityaṃ yat svalpād bhūri-rakṣaṇam // 1.19	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arakṣitaṃ tiṣṭhati deva-rakṣitaṃ surakṣitaṃ deva-hataṃ vinaśyati / jīvaty anātho 'pi vane visarjitaḥ kṛta-prayatno 'pi gṛhe vinaśyati // 1.20	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
avyāpareṣu vyāpāraṃ yo naraḥ kartum icchati / sa eva nidhanaṃ yāti kīlotpāṭīva vānaraḥ // 1.21	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
suhṛdām upakāraṇād dviṣatām apy apakāraṇāt / nṛpa-saṃśraya iṣyate budhair jaṭharaṃ ko na bibharti kevalam // 1.22	ajñātasamavṛtta [9: ssj] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
kiṃ ca- yasmiñ jīvanti jīvanti bahavaḥ so 'tra jīvatu / vayāṃsi kiṃ na kurvanti cañcvā svodara-pūraṇam // 1.23	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yaj jīvyate kṣaṇam api prathitaṃ manuṣyair vijñāna-śaurya-vibhavārya-guṇaiḥ sametam / tan nāma jīvitam iha pravadanti taj-jñāḥ kāko 'pi jīvati cirāya baliṃ ca bhuṅkte // 1.24	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
yo nātmanā na ca pareṇa ca bandhu-varge dīne dayāṃ na kurute na ca martya-varge / kiṃ tasya jīvita-phalaṃ hi manuṣya-loke kāko 'pi jīvati cirāya baliṃ ca bhuṅkte // 1.25	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
supūrā syāt kunadikā supūro mūṣikāñjaliḥ / susaṃtuṣṭaḥ kāpuruṣaḥ svalpakenāpi tuṣyati // 1.26	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: bha-vipulā (ma-gaṇa-pūrvikā!))
kiṃ ca- kiṃ tena jātu jātena māṭur yauvana-hāriṇā / ārohati na yaḥ svasya vaṃśasyāgre dhvajo yathā // 1.27	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
parivartini saṃsāre mṛtaḥ ko vā na jāyate / jātas tu gaṇyate so 'tra yaḥ sphurec ca śriyādhikaḥ // 1.28	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ ca- jātasya nadī-tīre tasyāpi tṛṇasya janma-sāphalyam / yat salila-majjanākula-jana-hastālambanaṃ bhavati // 1.29	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tathā ca- stimitonnata-sañcārā jana-santāpa-hāriṇaḥ / jāyante viralā loke jaladā iva sajjanāḥ // 1.30	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
niratiśayaṃ garimāṇaṃ tena jananyāḥ smaranti vidvāṃsaḥ / yat kam api vahati garbhaṃ mahatām api yo gurur bhavati // 1.31	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
aprakaṭīkṛta-śaktiḥ śakto 'pi janas tiraskriyāṃ labhate / nivasann antar-dāruṇi laṅghyo vahnir na tu jvalitaḥ // 1.32	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
uktaṃ ca- apṛṣṭo 'trāpradhāno yo brūte rājñaḥ puraḥ kudhīḥ / na kevalam asaṃmānaṃ labhate ca viḍambanam // 1.33	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- vacas tatra prayoktavyaṃ yatroktaṃ labhate phalam / sthāyī bhavati cātyantaṃ rāgaḥ śukla-paṭe yathā // 1.34	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
damaka āha- mā maivaṃ vada / apradhānaḥ pradhānaḥ syāt sevate yadi pārthivam / pradhāno 'py apradhānaḥ syād yadi sevā-vivarjitaḥ // 1.35	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
āsannam eva nṛpatir bhajate manuṣyaṃ vidyā-vihīnam akulīnam asaṃskṛtaṃ vā / prāyeṇa bhūmi-patayaḥ pramadā latāś ca yat pārśvato bhavati tat pariveṣṭayanti // 1.36	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
tathā ca- kopa-prasāda-vastūni ye vicinvanti sevakāḥ / ārohanti śanaiḥ paścād dhunvantam api pārthivam // 1.37	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
vidyāvatāṃ mahecchānāṃ śilpa-vikrama-śālinām / sevā-vṛtti-vidāṃ caiva nāśrayaḥ pārthivaṃ vinā // 1.38	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ye jāty-ādi-mahotsāhān narendrān nopayānti ca / teṣām āmaraṇaṃ bhikṣā prāyaścittaṃ vinirmitam // 1.39	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ye ca prāhur durātmāno durārādhyā mahībhujaḥ / pramādālasya-jāḍyāni khyāpitāni nijāni taiḥ // 1.40	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarpān vyāghrān gajān siṃhān dṛṣṭvopāyair vaśīkṛtān / rājeti kiyatī mātrā dhīmatām apramādinām // 1.41	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rājānam eva saṃśritya vidvān yāti parāṃ gatim / vinā malayam anyatra candanaṃ na prarohati // 1.42	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dhavalāny ātapatrāṇi vājinaś ca manoramāḥ / sadā mattāś ca mātaṅgāḥ prasanne sati bhūpatau // 1.43	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
udīrito 'rthaḥ paśunāpi gṛhate hayāś ca nāgāś ca vahanti coditāḥ / anuktam apy ūhati paṇḍito janaḥ pareṅgita-jñāna-phjalā hi buddhayaḥ // 1.44	upajāti jagatī: ajñātam [12: jtjs], vaṃśastha [12: jtjr], ajñātam [12: jmjr] atha vā vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
ākārair iṅgitair gatyā ceṣṭayā bhāṣaṇena ca / netra-vaktra-vikāraiś ca lakṣyate'ntargataṃ manaḥ // 1.45	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
suvarṇa-puṣpitāṃ pṛthvīṃ vicinvanti narās trayaḥ / śūraś ca kṛta-vidyaś ca yaś ca jānāti sevitum // 1.46	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sā sevā yā prabhu-hitā grāhyā vākya-viśeṣataḥ / āśrayet pārthivaṃ vidvāṃs tad-dvāreṇaiva nānyathā // 1.47	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo na vetti guṇān yasya na taṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ / na hi tasmāt phalaṃ kiñcit sukṛṣṭād ūṣarād iva // 1.48	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dravya-kṛti-hīno 'pi sevyaḥ sevya-guṇānvitaḥ / bhavaty ājīvanaṃ tasmāt phalaṃ kālāntarād api // 1.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
api sthāṇuvad āsīnaḥ śuṣyan parigataḥ kṣudhā / na tv ajñānātma-sampannād vṛttim īhate paṇḍitaḥ // 1.50	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
sevakaḥ svāminaṃ dveṣṭi kṛpaṇaṃ paruṣākṣaram / ātmānaṃ kiṃ sa na dveṣṭi sevyāsevyaṃ na vetti yaḥ // 1.51	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasyāśritya viśrāmaṃ kṣudhārtā yānti sevakāḥ / so 'rkavan nṛpatis tyājyaḥ sadā puṣpa-phalo 'pi san // 1.52	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
rāja-mātari devyāṃ ca kumāre mukhya-mantriṇi / purohite pratīhāre sadā varteta rājavat // 1.53	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jīveti prabruvan proktaḥ kṛtyākṛtya-vicakṣaṇaḥ / karoti nirvikalpaṃ yaḥ sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.54	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prabhu-prasādajaṃ vittaṃ suprāptaṃ yo nivedayet / vastrādyaṃ ca dadhāty aṅge sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.55	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
antaḥ-pura-caraiḥ sārdhaṃ yo na mantraṃ samācaret / na kalatrair narendrasya sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.56	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dyūtaṃ yo yama-dūtābhaṃ hālāṃ hālāhalopamam / paśyed dārān vṛthākārān sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.57	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yuddha-kāle'graṇīr yaḥ syāt sadā pṛṣṭhānugaḥ pure / prabhor dvārāśrito harmye sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.58	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sammato 'haṃ vibhor nityam iti matvā vyatikramet / kṛcchreṣv api na maryādāṃ sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.59	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dveṣi-dveṣa-paro nityam iṣṭānām iṣṭa-karma-kṛt / yo naro nara-nāthasya sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.60	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
proktaḥ pratyuttaraṃ nāha viruddhaṃ prabhunā na yaḥ / na samīpe hasaty uccaiḥ sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.61	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
up raṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ tadvan manyate bhaya-varjitaḥ / pravāsaṃ sva-purāvāsaṃ sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.62	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na kuryān naranāthasya yoṣidbhiḥ saha saṃgatim / na nindāṃ na vivādaṃ ca sa bhaved rāja-vallabhaḥ // 1.63	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
damanaka āha- uttarād uttaraṃ vākyaṃ vadatāṃ samprajāyate / suvṛṣṭi-guṇa-sampannād bījād bījam ivāparam // 1.64	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
apāya-sandarśanajāṃ vipattim upāya-sandarśanajāṃ ca siddhim / medhāvino nīti-guṇa-prayuktāṃ puraḥ sphurantīm iva varṇayanti // 1.65	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
ekeṣāṃ vāci śukavad anyeṣāṃ hṛdi mūkavat / hṛdi vāci tathānyeṣāṃ valgu valgantiu sūktayaḥ // 1.66	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
aprāpta-kālaṃ vacanaṃ bṛhaspatir api bruvan / labhate bahv-avajñānam apamānaṃ ca puṣkalam // 1.67	anuṣṭubh (1,2: bha-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
karaṭaka āha- durārādhyā hi rājānaḥ parvatā iva sarvadā / vyālākīrṇāḥ suviṣamāḥ kaṭhinā duṣṭa-sevitāḥ // 1.68	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: na-vipulā)
tathā ca- bhoginaḥ kañcukāviṣṭāḥ kuṭilāḥ krūra-ceṣṭitāḥ / suduṣṭā mantra-sādhyāś ca rājānaḥ pannagā iva // 1.69	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
dvi-jihvāḥ krūra-karmāṇo 'niṣṭhāś chidrānusāriṇaḥ / dūrato 'pi hi paśyanti rājāno bhujagā iva // 1.70	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svalpam apy apakurvanti ye'bhīṣṭā hi mahīpateḥ / te vahnāv iva dahyante pataṅgāḥ pāpa-cetasaḥ // 1.71	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durārohaṃ padaṃ rājñāṃ sarva-loka-namaskṛtam / svalpenāpy apakāreṇa brāhmaṇyam iva duṣyati // 1.72	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durārādhyāḥ śriyo rājñāṃ durāpā duṣparigrahāḥ / tiṣṭhanty āpa ivādhāre ciram ātmani saṃsthitāḥ // 1.73	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya yasya hi yo bhāvas tena tena samācaret / anupraviśya medhāvī kṣipram ātma-vaśaṃ nayet // 1.74	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhartuś cittānuvartitvaṃ suvṛttaṃ cānujīvinām / rākṣasāś cāpi gṛhyante nityaṃ chandānuvartibhiḥ // 1.75	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
saruṣi nṛpe stuti-vacanaṃ tad-abhimate prema tad-dviṣi dveṣaḥ / tad-dānasya ca śaṃsā amantra-tantraṃ vaśīkaraṇam // 1.76	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
dantasya niṣkoṣaṇakena nityaṃ karṇasya kaṇḍūyanakena vāpi / tṛṇena kāryaṃ bhavatīśvarāṇāṃ kim āṅga vāggha-stavatā nareṇa // 1.77	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
sthāneṣv eva niyoktavyā bhṛtyā ābharaṇāni ca / na hi cūḍāmaṇiḥ pāde prabhavāmīti badhyate // 1.78	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yataḥ- anabhijño guṇānāṃ yo na bhṛtyair anugamyate / dhanāḍhyo 'pi kulīno 'pi kramāYāto 'pi bhūpatiḥ // 1.79	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
asamaiḥ samīyamānaḥ samaiś ca parihīyamāṇa-sat-kāraḥ / dhuri yo na yujyamānas tribhir artha-patiṃ tyajati bhṛtyaḥ // 1.80	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
kanaka-bhūṣaṇa-saṅgrahaṇocito yadi maṇis trapuṇi pratibadhyate / na sa virauti na cāpi sa śobhate bhavati yojayitur vacanīyatā // 1.81	drutavilambita [12: nBBr]
savya-dakṣiṇayor yatra viśeṣo nāsti hastayoḥ / kas tatra kṣaṇam apyāryo vidyamāna-gatir bhavet // 1.82	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāce maṇir maṇau kāco yeṣāṃ buddhir vikalpate / na teṣāṃ sannidhau bhṛtyo nāma-mātro 'pi tiṣṭhati // 1.83	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
parīkṣakā yatra na santi deśe nārghanti ratnāni samudrajāni / ābhīra-deśe kila candrakāntaṃ tribhir varāṭair vipaṇanti gopāḥ // 1.84	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
lohitākhyasya ca maṇeḥ padmarāgasya cāntaram / yatra nāsti kathaṃ tatra kriyate ratna-vikrayaḥ // 1.85	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
nirviśeṣaṃ yadā svāmī samaṃ bhṛtyeṣu vartate / tatrodyama-samarthānām utsāhaḥ parihīyate // 1.86	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na vinā pārthivo bhṛtyair na bhṛtyāḥ pārthivaṃ vinā / teṣāṃ ca vyavahāro 'yaṃ paraspara-nibandhanaḥ // 1.87	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhṛtyair vinā svayaṃ rājā lokānugraha-kāribhiḥ / mayūkhair iva dīptāṃśus tejasvy api na śobhate // 1.88	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
araiḥ sandhāryate nābhir nābhau cārāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ / svāmi-sevakayor evaṃ vṛtti-cakraṃ pravartate // 1.89	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śirasā vidhṛtā nityaṃ snehena paripālitāḥ / keśā api virajyante niḥsnehāḥ kiṃ na sevakāḥ // 1.90	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rājā tuṣṭo hi bhṛtyānām artha-mātraṃ prayacchati / te tu saṃmāna-mātreṇa prāṇair apy upakurvate // 1.91	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evaṃ jñātvā narendreṇa bhṛtyāḥ kāryā vicakṣaṇāḥ / kulīnāḥ śaurya-saṃyuktāḥ śaktā bhaktāḥ kramāgatāḥ // 1.92	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yaḥ kṛtvā sukṛtaṃ rājño duṣkaraṃ hitam uttamam / lajjayā vakti no kiñcit tena rājā sahāyavān // 1.93	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasmin kṛtyaṃ samāveśya nirviśaṅkena cetasā / āsyate sevakaḥ sa syāt kalatram iva cāparam // 1.94	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo 'nāhūtaḥ samabhyeti dvāri tiṣṭhati sarvadā / pṛṣṭhaḥ satyaṃ mitaṃ brūte sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.95	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anādiṣṭo 'pi bhūpasya dṛṣṭvā hānikaraṃ ca yaḥ / yatate tasya nāśāya sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.96	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāḍito 'pi durukto 'pi daṇḍito 'pi mahībhujā / yo na cintayate pāpaṃ sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.97	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na garvaṃ kurute māne nāpamāne ca tapyate / svākāraṃ rakṣayed yas tu sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.98	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na kṣudhā pīḍyate yas tu nidrayā na kadācana / na ca śītātapādyaiś ca sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.99	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śrutvā sāṃgrāmikīṃ vārtāṃ bhaviṣyāṃ svāminaṃ prati / prasannāsyo bhaved yas tu sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.100	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sīmā vṛddhiṃ samāyāti śukla-pakṣa ivoḍurāṭ / niyoga-saṃsthite yasmin sa bhṛtyo 'rho mahībhujām // 1.101	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sīmā saṃkocam āyāti vahnau carma ivāhitam / sthite yasmin sa tu tyājyo bhṛtyo rājyaṃ samīhatā // 1.102	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kauśeyaṃ kṛmijaṃ suvarṇam upalād durvāpi goromataḥ paṅkāt tāmarasaṃ śaśāṅka udadher indīvaraṃ gomayāt / kāṣṭhād agnir aheḥ phaṇād api maṇir go-pittato rocanā prākāśyaṃ sva-guṇodayena guṇino gacchanti kiṃ janmanā // 1.103	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
mūṣikā gṛha-jātāpi hantavyā svāpa-kāriṇī / bhakṣya-pradānair jāro hitakṛt prāpyate janaiḥ // 1.104	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
eraṇḍa-bhiṇḍārka-nalaiḥ prabhūtair api sañcitaiḥ / dāru-kṛtyaṃ yathā nāsti tathaivājñaiḥ prayojanam // 1.105	anuṣṭubh (1,2: bha-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ bhaktenāsamarthena kiṃ śakternāpakāriṇā / bhaktaṃ śaktaṃ ca māṃ rājan nāvajñātuṃ tvam arhasi // 1.106	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
so 'bravīt- api svalpataraṃ kāryaṃ yad bhavet pṛthivī-pateḥ / tan na vācyaṃ sabhā-madhye provācedaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ // 1.107	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
ṣaṭ-karṇo bhidyate mantraś catuṣkarṇaḥ sthiro bhavet / tasmāt sarva-prayatnena ṣaṭkarṇaṃ varjayet sudhīḥ // 1.108	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dariṣu kiñcit svajaneṣu kiñcid gopyaṃ vayasyeṣu suteṣu kiñcit / yuktaṃ na vā yuktam idaṃ vicintya vaded vipaścin mahato 'nurodhāt // 1.	upajāti triṣṭubh: ajñātam [11: ntjgl], upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
svāmini guṇāntarajñe guṇavati bhṛtye'nuvartini kalaye / suhṛdi nirantara-citte nivedya duḥkhaṃ sukhī bhavati // 1.	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
ambhasā bhidyate setus tathā mantro 'py arakṣitaḥ / paiśunyād bhidyate sneho bhidyate vāgbhir āturaḥ // 1.111	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atyutkaṭe ca raudre ca śatrau prāpte na hīyate / dhairyaṃ yasya mahīnātho na sa yāti parābhavam // 1.112	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
darśita-bhaye'pi dhātari dhairya-dhvaṃso bhaven na dhīrāṇām / śoṣita-sarasi nidāghe nitarām evoddhataḥ sindhuḥ // 1.113	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- yasya na vipadi viṣādaḥ sampadi harṣo raṇe na bhīrutvam / taṃ bhuvana-traya-tilakaṃ janayati jananī sutaṃ viralam // 1.114	ajñātasamavṛtta [7: jBl] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- śakti-vaikalya-namrasya niḥsāratvāl laghīyasaḥ / jannimo mānahīnasya tṛṇasya ca samā gatiḥ // 1.115	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
api ca- anya-pratāpam āsādya yo dṛḍhatvaṃ na gacchati / jatujābharaṇasyeva rūpeṇāpi hi tasya kim // 1.116	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
pūrvam eva mayā jñātaṃ pūrṇam etad dhi medasā / anupraviśya vijñātaṃ yāvac carma ca dāru ca // 1.117	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhaye vā yadi vā harṣe samprāpte yo vimarśayet / kṛtyaṃ na kurute vegān na sa santāpam āpnuyāt // 1.118	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aśvaḥ śastraṃ śāstraṃ vīṇā vāṇī naraś ca nārī ca / puruṣa-viśeṣaṃ prāptā bhavanty ayogyāś ca yogyāś ca // 1.119	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
svāmy-ādeśāt subhṛtyasya na bhoḥ sañjāyate kvacit / praviśen mukham āheyaṃ dustaraṃ vā mahārṇavam // 1.120	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- svāmy-ādiṣṭas tu yo bhṛtyaḥ samaṃ viṣamam eva ca / manyate na sa sandhāryo bhūbhujā bhūtim icchatā // 1.121	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
ye bhavanti mahīpasya sammānita-vimānitāḥ / yatante tasya nāśāya kulīnā api sarvadā // 1.122	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na badhyante hy aviśvastā balibhir durbalā api / viśvastās tv eva badhyante balavanto 'pi durbalaiḥ // 1.123	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bṛhaspater api prājño na viśvāse vrajen naraḥ / ya icched ātmano vṛddhim āyuṣyaṃ ca sukhāni ca // 1.124	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śapathaiḥ sandhitasyāpi na viśvāse vrajed ripoḥ / rājya-lābhodyato vṛtraḥ śakreṇa śapathair hataḥ // 1.125	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na viśvāsaṃ vinā śatrur devānām api siddhyati / viśvāsāt tridaśendreṇa diter garbho vidāritaḥ // 1.126	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na kaulīnyān na sauhārdān nṛpo vākye pravartate / mantriṇāṃ vāvad abhyeti vyasanaṃ śokam eva ca // 1.127	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sadaivāpadgato rājā bhogyo bhavati mantriṇām / ataeva hi vāñchanti mantriṇaḥ sāpadaṃ nṛpam // 1.128	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā necchati nīrogaḥ kadācit sucikitsakam / tathāpad rahito rājā sacivaṃ nābhivāñchati // 1.129	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api svalpam asatyaṃ yaḥ puro vadati bhūbhujām / devānāṃ ca vinaśyate sa drutaṃ sumahān api // 1.130	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
tathā ca- sarva-deva-mayo rājā manunā samprakīrtitaḥ / tasmāt taṃ devavat paśyen na vyalīkena karhicit // 1.131	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
sarva-devamayasyāpi viśeṣo nṛpater ayam / śubhāśubha-phalaṃ sadyo nṛpād devād bhavāntare // 1.132	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tṛṇāni nonmūlayati prabhañjano mrḍūni nīcaiḥ praṇatāni sarvataḥ / svabhāva evonnata-cetasām ayaṃ mahān mahatsv eva karoti vikramam // 1.133	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
gaṇḍasthaleṣu mada-vāriṣu baddha-rāga- matta-bhramad-bhramara-pāda-talāhato 'pi / kopaṃ na gacchati nitānta-balo 'pi nāgas tulye bale tu balavān parikopam eti // 1.134	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
na tac chastrair na nāgendrair na hayair na padātibhiḥ / kāryaṃ saṃsiddhim abhyeti yathā buddhyā prasādhitam // 1.135	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
paryanto labhyate bhūmeḥ samudrasya girer api / na kathañcin mahīpasya cittāntaḥ kenacit kvacit // 1.136	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
antaḥ-sārair akuṭilair acchidraiḥ suparīkṣitaiḥ / mantribhir dhāryate rājyaṃ sustambhair iva mandiram // 1.137	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- mantriṇāṃ bhinna-sandhāne bhiṣajāṃ sānnipātike / karmaṇi vyajyate prajñā svasthe ko vā na paṇḍitaḥ // 1.138	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
amṛtaṃ śiśire vahnir amṛtaṃ priya-darśanam / amṛtaṃ rāja-saṃmānam amṛtaṃ kṣīra-bhojanam // 1.139	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ākheṭakasya dharmeṇa vibhavāḥ syur vaśe nṝṇām / nṛ-prajāḥ prerayaty eko hanty anyo 'tra mṛgān iva // 1.140	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yo na pūjayate garvād uttamādhama-madhyamān / nṛpāsannān sa mānyo 'pi bhraśyate dantilo yathā // 1.141	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
narapati-hita-kartā dveṣyatāṃ yāti loke janapada-hita-kartā tyajyate pārthivendraiḥ / iti mahati virodhe vartamāne samāne nṛpati-jana-padānāṃ durlabhaḥ kārya-kartā // 1.142	mālinī [15: nnmyy]
yo hy apakartum aśaktaḥ kupyati kim asau naro 'tra nirlajjaḥ / utpatito 'pi hi caṇakaḥ śaktaḥ kiṃ bhrāṣṭrakaṃ bhaṅktum // 1.143	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
yad vāñchati divā martyo vīkṣate vā karoti vā / tat svapne'pi tad-abhyāsād brūte vātha karoti vā // 1.144	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- śubhaṃ vā yadi pāpaṃ yan nṝṇāṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam / sugūḍham api taj jñeyaṃ svapna-vākyāt tathā madāt // 1.145	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
athavā strīṇāṃ viṣaye ko 'tra sandehaḥ / jalpanti sārdham anyena paśyanty anyaṃ sa-vibhramāḥ / hṛd-gataṃ cintayanty anyaṃ priyaḥ ko nāma yoṣitām // 1.146	ajñātasamavṛtta [10: mjtl] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
anyac ca- ekena smita-pāṭalādhara-ruco jalpanty analpākṣaraṃ vīkṣante'nyam itaḥ sphuṭat-kumudinī-phullollasal-locanāḥ / dūrodāra-caritra-citra-vibhavaṃ dhyāyanti cānyaṃ dhiyā kenetthaṃ paramārthato 'rthavad iva premāsti vāma-bhruvām // 1.147	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- nāgnis tṛpyati kāṣṭhānāṃ nāpagānāṃ mahodadhiḥ / nāntakaḥ sarva-bhūtānāṃ na puṃsāṃ vāma-locanā // 1.148	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
raho nāsti kṣaṇo nāsti nāsti prārthayitā naraḥ / tena nārada nārīṇāṃ satītvam upajāyate // 1.149	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo mohān manyate mūḍho rakteyaṃ mama kāminī / sa tasyā vaśago nityaṃ bhavet krīḍā-śakuntavat // 1.150	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāsāṃ vākyāni kṛtyāni svalpāni sugurūṇy api / karoti saḥ kṛtair loke laghutvaṃ yāti sarvataḥ // 1.151	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
striyaṃ ca yaḥ prārthayate sannikarṣaṃ ca gacchati / īṣac ca kurute sevāṃ tam evecchanti yoṣitaḥ // 1.152	anuṣṭubh (1,2: bha-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
anarthitvān manuṣyāṇāṃ bhayāt parijanasya ca / maryādāyām amaryādāḥ striyas tiṣṭhanti sarvadā // 1.153	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nāsāṃ kaścid agamyo 'sti nāsāṃ ca vayasi sthitiḥ / virūpaṃ rūpavantaṃ vā pumān ity eva bhujyate // 1.154	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rakto hi jāyate bhogyo nārīṇāṃ śāṭikā yathā / ghṛṣyante yo daśālambī nitambe viniveśitaḥ // 1.155	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
alaktiko yathā rakto niṣpīḍya puruṣas tathā / abalābhir balād raktaḥ pāda-mūle nipātyate // 1.156	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ko 'rthān prāpya na garvito viṣayiṇaḥ kasyāpado 'staṃ gatāḥ strībhiḥ kasya na khaṇḍitaṃ bhuvi manaḥ ko nāmā rājñāṃ priyaḥ / kaḥ kālasya na gocarāntara-gataḥ ko 'rthī gato gauravaṃ ko vā durjana-vāgurāsu patitaḥ kṣemeṇa yātaḥ pumān // 1.157	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- kāke śaucaṃ dyūta-kāreṣu satyaṃ sarpe kṣāntiḥ strīṣu kāmopaśāntiḥ / klībe dhairyaṃ madyape tattva-cintā rājā mitraṃ kena dṛṣṭaṃ śrutaṃ vā // 1.158	śālinī [11: mttgg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
akulīno 'pi mūrkho 'pi bhūpālaṃ yo 'tra sevate / api saṃmānahīno 'pi sa sarvatra prapūjyate // 1.159	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api kāpuruṣo bhīruḥ syāc cen nṛpati-sevakaḥ / tathāpi na parābhūtiṃ janād āpnoti mānavaḥ // 1.160	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
stokenonnatim āyāti stokenāyāty adho-gatim / aho sasadṛśo ceṣṭā tulāyaṣṭeḥ khalasya ca // 1.161	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yadṛcchayāpy upanataṃ sakṛt sajjana-saṅgatam / bhavaty ajaram atyantaṃ nābhyāsa-kramam īkṣate // 1.162	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ ca- phala-hīnaṃ nṛpaṃ bhṛtyāḥ kulīnam api connatam / santy ajyāny atra gacchanti śuṣkaṃ vṛkṣam ivāṇḍajāḥ // 1.163	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- api saṃmāna-saṃyuktāḥ kulīnā bhakti-tat-parāḥ / vṛtti-bhaṅgān mahīpālaṃ tyajanty eva hi sevakāḥ // 1.164	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- kālātikramaṇaṃ vṛtteryo na kurvīta bhūpatiḥ / kadācit taṃ na muñcanti bhartsitā api sevakāḥ // 1.165	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
deśānām upari kṣmābhṛd āturāṇāṃ cikitsakāḥ / vaṇijo grāhakāṇāṃ ca mūrkhāṇām api paṇḍitāḥ // 1.166	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pramādināṃ tathā caurā bhikṣukā gṛha-medhinām / gaṇikāḥ kāmināṃ caiva sarva-lokasya śilpinaḥ // 1.167	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sāmādi-sajjitaiḥ pāśaiḥ pratīkṣante divā-niśam / upajīvanti śaktyā hi jalajā jaladān iva // 1.168	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
athavā sādhv idam ucyate- sarpāṇāṃ ca khalānāṃ ca para-dravyāpahāriṇām / abhiprāyā na sidhyanti tenedaṃ vartate jagat // 1.169	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
attuṃ vāñchati śāmbhavo gaṇapater ākhuṃ kṣudhārtaḥ phaṇī taṃ ca krauñca-ripoḥ śikhī giri-sutā-siṃho 'pi nāgāśanam / itthaṃ yatra parigrahasya ghaṭanā śambhor api syād gṛhe tatrāpy asya kathaṃ na bhāvi jagato yasmāt svarūpaṃ hi tat // 1.170	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
aśṛnvann api boddhavyo mantribhiḥ pṛthivī-patiḥ / yathā sva-doṣa-nāśāya vidureṇāmbikāsutaḥ // 1.171	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- madonmattasya bhūpasya kuñjarasya ca gacchataḥ / unmārgaṃ vācyatāṃ yānti mahāmātrāḥ samīpagāḥ // 1.172	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
jambūko huḍu-yuddhena vayaṃ cāṣāḍha-bhūtinā / dūtikā para-kāryeṇa trayo doṣāḥ svayaṃ kṛtāḥ // 1.173	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthānām arjane duḥkham arjitānāṃ ca rakṣaṇe / nāśe duḥkhaṃ vyaye duḥkhaṃ dhig arthāḥ kaṣṭa-saṃśrayāḥ // 1.174	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nispṛho nādhikārī syān nākāmī maṇḍana-priyaḥ / nāvidagdhaḥ priyaṃ brūyāt sphuṭa-vaktā na vañcakaḥ // 1.175	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pūrvaṃ vayasi yaḥ śāntaḥ sa śānta iti me matiḥ / dhātuṣu kṣīyamāṇeṣu śamaḥ kasya na jāyate // 1.176	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ādau citte tataḥ kāye satāṃ saṃjāyate jarā / asatāṃ ca punaḥ kāye naiva citte kadācana // 1.177	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śūdro vā yadi vānyo 'pi caṇḍālo 'pi jaṭādharaḥ / dīkṣitaḥ śiva-mantreṇa sa bhasmāṅgī śivo bhavet // 1.178	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ṣaḍ-akṣareṇa mantreṇa puṣpam ekam api svayam / liṅgasya mūrdhni yo dadyān na sa bhūyo 'bhijāyate // 1.179	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durmantrān nṛpatir vinaśyati yatiḥ saṅgāt suto lālasād vipro 'nadhyayanāt kulaṃ kutanayāc chīlaṃ khalopāsanāt / maitrī cāpraṇayāt samṛddhir anayāt snehaḥ pravāsāśrayāt strī garvād anavekṣaṇād api kṛṣis tyāgāt pramādād dhanam // 1.180	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
samprāpto yo 'tithiḥ sāyaṃ sūryoḍhe gṛha-medhinām / pūjayā tasya devatvaṃ prayānti gṛha-medhinaḥ // 1.181	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- tṛṇāni bhūmir udakaṃ vāk-caturthī ca sūnṛtā / satām etāni harmyeṣu nocchidyante kadācana // 1.182	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
svāgatenāgnayas tṛptā āsanena śatakratuḥ / pāda-śaucena pitaraḥ arghāc chambhus tathātitheḥ // 1.183	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
durdivase ghana-timire duḥsañcārāsu nagara-vīthīṣu / patyur videśa-gamane parama-sukhaṃ jaghana-capalāyāḥ // 1.184	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- paryaṅkeṣv āstaraṇaṃ patim anukūlaṃ manoharaṃ śayanam / tṛṇam iva laghu manyante kāminyaś caurya-rata-lubdhāḥ // 1.185	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tathā ca- keliṃ pradahati lajjā śṛṅgāro 'sthīni cāṭavaḥ kaṭavaḥ / vandha-trayāḥ paritoṣo na kiṃcid iṣṭaṃ bhavet patyau // 1.186	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
kula-patanaṃ jana-garhāṃ bandhanam api jīvitavya-sandeham / aṅgīkaroti kulaṭā satataṃ para-puruṣa-saṃsaktā // 1.187	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
vaikalyaṃ dharaṇī-pātam ayathocita-jalpanam / saṃnipātasya cihnāni madyaṃ sarvāṇi darśayet // 1.188	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kara-spando 'mbara-tyāgas tejo-hāniḥ sarāgatā / vāruṇī-saṅgajāvasthā bhānunāpy anubhūyate // 1.189	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
viṣama-stha-svādu-phala-grahaṇa-vyavasāya-niścayo yeṣām / uṣṭrāṇām iva teṣāṃ manye'haṃ śaṃsitaṃ janma // 1.190	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- sandigdhe para-loke janāpavāde ca jagati bahu-citre / svādhīne para-ramaṇe dhanyās tāruṇya-phala-bhājaḥ // 1.191	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
anyac ca- yadi bhavati deva-yogāt pumān virūpo 'pi bandhako rahasi / na tu kṛcchrād api bhadraṃ nija-kāntaṃ sā bhajaty eva // 1.192	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
āditya-candra-hari-śaṃkara-vāsavādyāḥ śaktā na jetum atiduḥkha-karāṇi yāni / tānīndriyāṇi balavanti sudurjayāni ye nirjayanti bhuvane balinas ta eke // 1.193	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
śambarasya ca yā māyā yā māyā namucer api / baleḥ kumbhīnasaś caiva sarvās tā yoṣito viduḥ // 1.194	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hasantaṃ prahasanty etā rudantaṃ prarudanty api / apriyaṃ priya-vākyaiś ca gṛhṇanti kāla-yogataḥ // 1.195	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
uśanā veda yac chāstraṃ yac ca veda bṛhaspatiḥ / strī-buddhyā na viśiṣyete tāḥ sma rakṣyāḥ kathaṃ naraiḥ // 1.196	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anṛtaṃ satyam ity āhuḥ satyaṃ cāpi tathānṛtam / iti yās tāḥ kathaṃ vīra saṃrakṣyāḥ puruṣair iha // 1.197	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nātiprasaṅgaḥ pramadāsu kāryo necched balaṃ strīṣu vivardhamānam / atiprasaktaiḥ puruṣair yatas tāḥ krīḍanti kākair iva lūna-pakṣaiḥ // 1.198	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
sumukhena vadanti vagunā praharanty eva śitena cetasā / madhu tiṣṭhati vāci yoṣitāṃ hṛdaye hālāhalaṃ mahad-viṣam // 1.199	ajñātasamavṛtta [8: ssll] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
ata eva nipīyate'dharo hṛdayaṃ muṣṭibhir eva tāḍyate / puruṣaiḥ sukha-leśa-vañcitair madhu-lubdhaiḥ kamalaṃ yathālibhiḥ // 1.200	viyoginī = [10: ssjg] 1,3 + [11: sBrlg] 2,4
api ca- āvartaḥ saṃśayānām avinaya-bhavanaṃ pattanaṃ sāhasānāṃ doṣāṇāṃ saṃnidhānaṃ kapaṭa-śata-mayaṃ kṣetram apratyayānām / svarga-dvārasya vighnaṃ naraka-pura-mukhaṃ sarva-māyā-karaṇḍaṃ strī-yantraṃ kena sṛṣṭaṃ viṣam amṛta-mayaṃ prāṇi-lokasya pāśaḥ // 1.201	sragdharā [21: mrBnyyy] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
kārkaśyaṃ stanayor dṛśos taralatālīkaṃ mukhe ślāghyate kauṭilyaṃ kaca-saṃcaye ca vacane māndyaṃ trike sthūlatā / bhīrutvaṃ hṛdaye sadaiva kathitaṃ māyā-prayogaḥ priye yāsāṃ doṣa-gaṇo guṇo mṛga-dṛśāṃ tāḥ syur narāṇāṃ priyāḥ // 1.202	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
etā hasanti ca rudanti ca kārya-hetor viśvāsayanti ca paraṃ na ca viśvasanti / tasmān nareṇa kula-śīla-samanvitena nāryaḥ śmaśāna-ghaṭikā iva varjanīyāḥ // 1.203	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
tasmān nareṇa kulaśīlavatā sadaiva nāryaḥ śmaśāna-vaṭikā iva varjanīyāḥ / vyakīrṇa-kesara-karāla-mukhā mṛgendrā nāgāś ca bhūri-mada-rāja-virājamānāḥ // 1.204	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
kurvanti tāvat prathamaṃ priyāṇi yāvan na jānanti naraṃ prasaktam / jñātvā ca taṃ manmatha-pāśa-baddhaṃ grastāmiṣaṃ mīnam ivoddharanti // 1.205	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
samudra-vīcīva cala-svabhāvāḥ sandhyābhra-rekheva muhūrta-rāgāḥ / striyaḥ kṛtārthāḥ puruṣaṃ nirarthaṃ niṣpīḍotālaktakavat tyajanti // 1.206	upajāti triṣṭubh: ajñātam [11: mtjgl], upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
anṛtaṃ sāhasaṃ māyā mūrkhatvam atilubdhatā / aśaucaṃ nirdayatvaṃ ca strīṇāṃ doṣāḥ svabhāvajāḥ // 1.207	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sammohayantimadayanti viḍambayanti nirbharstayanti ramayanti viṣādayanti / etāḥ praviśya saralaṃ hṛdayaṃ narāṇāṃ kiṃ vā na vāma-nayanā na samācaranti // 1.208	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
antar-viṣa-mayā hy etā bahiś caiva manoramāḥ / guñjā-phala-samākārā yoṣitaḥ kena nirmitāḥ // 1.209	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhinna-svara-mukha-varṇaḥ śaṅkita-dṛṣṭiḥ samutpatita-tejāḥ / bhavati hi pāpaṃ kṛtvā sva-karma-santrāsitaḥ puruṣaḥ // 1.210	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- āyāti skhalitaiḥ pādair mukha-vaivarṇya-saṃyutaḥ / lalāṭa-sveda-bhāg bhūri-gadgadaṃ bhāṣate vacaḥ // 1.211	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
adho-dṛṣṭir vadet kṛtvā pāpaṃ prāptaḥ sabhāṃ naraḥ / tasmād yatnāt parijñeyāś cihnair etair vicakṣaṇaiḥ // 1.212	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- prasanna-vadano dṛṣṭaḥ spaṣṭa-vākyaḥ saroṣa-dṛk / sabhāyāṃ vakti sāmarṣaṃ sāvaṣṭambho naraḥ śuciḥ // 1.213	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
avadhyā brāhmaṇā gāvo striyo bālāś ca jñātayaḥ / yeṣāṃ cānnāni bhuñjīta ye ca syuḥ śaraṇāgatāḥ // 1.214	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
ekaṃ hanyān na vā hanyād iṣuḥ kṣipto dhanuṣmatā / prājñena tu matiḥ kṣiptā hanyād garbha-gatān api // 1.215	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tyājyaṃ na dhairyaṃ vidhure'pi daive dhairyāt kadācit sthitm āpnuyāt saḥ / yāte samudre'pi hi pota-bhaṅge sāṃyātriko vāñchati karma eva // 1.216	indravajrā [11: ttjgg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
udyoginaṃ satatam atra sameti lakṣmīr daivaṃ hi daivam iti kāpuruṣā vadanti / daivaṃ nihatya kuru pauruṣam ātma-śaktyā yatne kṛte yadi na sidhyati ko 'tra doṣaḥ // 1.217	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
suprayuktasya dambhasya brahmāpy antaṃ na gacchati / kauliko viṣṇu-rūpeṇa rāja-kanyāṃ niṣevate // 1.218	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
auṣadhārtha-sumantrāṇāṃ buddheś caiva mahātmanām / asādhyaṃ nāsti loke'tra yad brahmāṇḍasya madhyagam // 1.219	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mattebha-kumbha-pariṇāhini kuṅkumārdre tasyāḥ payodhara-yuge rati-kheda-khinnaḥ / vakṣo nidhāya bhuja-pañjara-madhya-vartī svapsye kadā kṣaṇam avāpya tadīya-saṅgam // 1.220	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
rāgī bimbādharo 'sau stana-kalaśa-yugaṃ yauvanārūḍha-garvaṃ nīcā nābhiḥ prakṛtyā kuṭilakam alakaṃ svalpakaṃ cāpi madhyam / kurvatv etāni nāma prasabham iha manaś cintitāny āśu khedaṃ yan māṃ tasyāḥ kapolau dahata iti muhuḥ svacchakau tan na yuktam // 1.221	sragdharā [21: mrBnyyy]
putrīti jātā mahatīha cintā kasmai pradeyeti mahān vitarkaḥ / dattvā sukhaṃ prāpsyati vā na veti kanyā-pitṛtvaṃ khalu nāma kaṣṭam // 1.222	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
nadyaś ca nāryaś ca sadṛk-prabhāvās tulyāni kūlāni kulāni tāsām / toyaiś ca doṣaiś ca nipātayanti nadyo hi kūlāni kulāni nāryaḥ // 1.223	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
jananī-mano harati jātavatī parivardhate saha śucā suhṛdām / para-sātkṛtāpi kurute malinaṃ durita-kramā duhitaro vipadaḥ // 1.224	pramitākṣarā [12: sjss]
nirviṣeṇāpi sarpeṇa kartavyā mahatī phaṇā / viṣaṃ bhavatu vā mābhūt phaṇāṭopo bhayaṅkaraḥ // 1.225	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gavām arthe brāhmaṇārthe svāmy-arthe svīkṛte'thavā / sthānārthe yas tyajet prāṇāṃs tasya lokāḥ sanātanāḥ // 1.226	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ra-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
candre maṇḍala-saṃsthe vigṛhyate rāhuṇā dinādhīśaḥ / śaraṇāgatena sārdhaṃ vipad api tejasvinā ślāghyā // 1.227	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
upāyena hi yac chakyaṃ na tac chakyaṃ parākramaiḥ / kākī kanaka-sūtreṇa kṛṣṇa-sarpam aghātayat // 1.228	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya kṣetraṃ nadī-tīre bhāryā ca para-saṅgatā / sa-sarpe ca gṛhe vāsaḥ kathaṃ syāt tasya nirvṛtiḥ // 1.229	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- sarpa-yukte gṛhe vāso mṛtyur eva na saṃśayaḥ / yad grāmānte vaset sarpas tasya syāt prāṇa-saṃśayaḥ // 1.230	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
upāyena jayo yādṛg ripos tādṛṅ na hetibhiḥ / upāya-jño 'lpa-kāyo 'pi na śūraiḥ paribhūyate // 1.231	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- bhakṣayitvā bahūn matsyān uttamādhama-madhyamān / atilaulyād bakaḥ kaścin mṛtaḥ karkaṭaka-grahāt // 1.232	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yadi bhinte sūrya-suto rohiṇyāḥ śakaṭam iha loke / dvādaśa varṣāṇi tadā nahi varṣati vāsavau bhūmau // 1.233	upagīti (12, 15, 12, 15)
tathā ca- prājāpatye śakaṭe bhinne kṛtvaiva pātakaṃ vasudhā / bhasmāsthi-śakalākīrṇā kāpālikam iva vrataṃ dhatte // 1.234	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
rohiṇī-śakaṭam arka-nandanaś ced bhinnatti rudhiro 'thavā śaśī / kiṃ vadāmi tad-aniṣṭa-sāgare sarva-lokam upayāti saṅkṣayaḥ // 1.235	upajāti triṣṭubh: rathoddhatā [11: rnrlg], ajñātam [11: mnrlg]
rohiṇī-śakaṭa-madhya-saṃsthite candram asya śaraṇī-kṛtā janāḥ / kvāpi yānti śiśupācitāśanāḥ sūrya-tapta-bhidurāmbu-pāyinaḥ // 1.236	rathoddhatā [11: rnrlg]
yasya buddhir balaṃ tasya nirbuddhes tu kuto balam / vane siṃho madonmattaḥ śaśakena nipātitaḥ // 1.237	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śanaiḥ śanaiś ca yo rājyam upabhuṅkte yathā-balam / rasāyanam iva prājñaḥ sa puṣṭiṃ paramāṃ vrajet // 1.238	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vidhinā mantra-yuktena rūkṣāpi mathitāpi ca / prayacchati phalaṃ bhūmir araṇīva hutāśanam // 1.239	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prajānāṃ pālanaṃ śasyaṃ svarga-kośasya vardhanam / pīḍanaṃ dharma-nāśāya pāpāyāyaśase sthitam // 1.240	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gopālena prajādhenor vitta-dugdhaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ / pālanāt poṣaṇād grāhyaṃ nyāyyāṃ vṛttiṃ samācaret // 1.241	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ajām iva prajāṃ mohād yo hanyāt pṛthivī-patim / tasyaikā jāyate tṛptir na dvitīyā kathañcana // 1.242	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
phalārthī nṛpatir lokān pālayed yatnam āsthitaḥ / dāna-mānādi-toyena mālākāro 'ṅkurān iva // 1.243	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nṛpa-dīpo dhana-snehaṃ prajābhyaḥ saṃharann api / āntara-sthair guṇaiḥ śubhrair lakṣyate naiva kenacit // 1.244	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā gaur duhyate kāle pālyate ca tathā prajāḥ / sicyate cīyate caiva latā puṣpa-phala-pradā // 1.245	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā bījāṅkuraḥ sūkṣmaḥ prayatnenābhirakṣitaḥ / phala-prado bhavet kāle tadval lokaḥ surakṣitaḥ // 1.246	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hiraṇya-dhānya-ratnāni yānāni vividhāni ca / tathānyad api yat kiñcit prajābhyaḥ syān mahīpateḥ // 1.247	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
lokānugraha-kartāraḥ pravardhante nareśvarāḥ / lokānāṃ saṅkṣayāc caiva kṣayaṃ yānti na saṃśayaḥ // 1.248	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhūmir mitraṃ hiraṇyaṃ ca vigrahasya phala-trayam / nāsty ekam api yady eṣāṃ na taṃ kuryāt kathañcana // 1.249	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yatra na syāt phalaṃ bhūri yatra casyāt parābhavaḥ / na tatra matimān yuddhaṃ samutpādya samācaret // 1.250	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na gajānāṃ sahasreṇa na ca lakṣeṇa vājinām / yat kṛtyaṃ sidhyati rājñāṃ durgeṇaikena vigrahe // 1.251	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
śatam eko 'pi saṃdhatte prākārastho dhanurdharaḥ / tasmād durgaṃ praśaṃsanti nītiśāstravicakṣaṇāḥ // 1.252	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
purā guroḥ samādeśādd hiraṇyakaśipor bhayāt / śakreṇa vihitaṃ durgaṃ prabhāvād viśvakarmaṇaḥ // 1.253	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tenāpi ca varo datto yasya durgaṃ sa bhūpatiḥ / vijayī syāt tato bhūmau durgāṇi syuḥ sahasraśaḥ // 1.254	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
daṃṣṭrāvirahito nāgo madahīno yathā gajaḥ / sarveṣāṃ jāyate vaśyo durgahīnas tathā nṛpaḥ // 1.255	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jāta-mātraṃ na yaḥ śatruṃ rogaṃ ca praśamaṃ nayet / mahābalo 'pi tenaiva vṛddhiṃ prāpya sa hanyate // 1.256	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- uttiṣṭhamānas tu paro nopekṣyaḥ pathyam icchatā / samau hi śiṣṭair āmnātau vartsyantāv āmayaḥ sa ca // 1.257	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
api ca- upekṣitaḥ kṣīṇa-balo 'pi śatruḥ pramāda-doṣāt puruṣair madāndhaiḥ / sādhyo 'pi bhūtvā prathamaṃ tato 'sāv asādhyatāṃ vyādhir iva prayāti // 1.258	ajñātasamavṛtta [14: yjtjgg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- ātmanaḥ śaktim udvīkṣya manotsāhaṃ ca yo vrajet / bahūn hanti sa eko 'pi kṣatriyān bhārgavo yathā // 1.259	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
aviditvātmanaḥ śaktiṃ parasya ca samutsukaḥ / gacchann abhimukho vahnau nāśaṃ yāti pataṅgavat // 1.260	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo balāt pronnataṃ yāti nihantuṃ sabalo 'py arim / vimadaḥ sa nivarteta śīrṇa-danto gajo yathā // 1.261	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
priyaṃ vā yadi vā dveṣyaṃ śubhaṃ vā yadi vāśubham / apṛṣṭo 'pi hitaṃ vakṣyed yasya necchet parābhavam // 1.262	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekaṃ bhūmi-patiḥ karoti sacivaṃ rājye pramāṇaṃ yadā taṃ mohāc chrayate madaḥ sa ca madād dāsyena nirvidyate / nirviṇṇasya padaṃ karoti hṛdaye tasya svatantra-spṛhā- svātantrya-spṛhayā tataḥ sa nṛpateḥ prāṇān abhidruhyati // 1.263	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
na so 'sti puruṣo rājñāṃ yo na kāmayate śriyam / aśaktā eva sarvatra narendraṃ paryupāsate // 1.264	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aneka-doṣa-duṣṭasya kāyaḥ kasya na vallabhaḥ / kurvann api vyalīkāni yaḥ priyaḥ priya eva saḥ // 1.265	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasminn evādhikaṃ cakṣur āropayati pārthivaḥ / akulīnaḥ kulīno vā sa śriyā bhājanaṃ naraḥ // 1.266	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
piṅgalaka āha- ukto bhavati yaḥ pūrvaṃ guṇavān iti saṃsadi / tasya doṣo na vaktavyaḥ pratijñā-bhaṅga-bhīruṇā // 1.267	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
itaḥ sa daityaḥ prāpta-śrīr neta evārhati kṣayam / viṣa-vṛkṣo 'pi saṃvardhya svayaṃ chettum asāmpratam // 1.268	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
ādau na vā praṇayināṃ praṇayo vidheyo datto 'thavā pratidinaṃ paripoṣaṇīyaḥ / utkṣipya yat kṣipati tat prakaroti lajjāṃ bhūmau sthitasya patanād bhayam eva nāsti // 1.269	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
upakāriṣu yaḥ sādhuḥ sādhutve tasya ko guṇaḥ / apakāriṣu yaḥ sādhuḥ sa sādhuḥ sadbhir ucyate // 1.270	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tulyārthaṃ tulya-sāmarthyaṃ marmajñaṃ vyavasāyinam / ardha-rājya-haraṃ bhṛtyaṃ yo na hanyāt sa hanyate // 1.271	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yādṛśaiḥ sevyate bhṛtyair yādṛśāṃś copasevate / kadācin nātra sandehas tādṛg bhavati pūruṣaḥ // 1.272	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
santaptāyasi saṃsthitasya payaso nāmāpi na jñāyate mukta-kāratayā tad eva nalinī-patra-sthitaṃ rājate / svātau sāgara-śukti-kukṣi-patitaṃ taj jāyate mauktikaṃ prāyeṇādhama-madhyamottama-guṇaḥ saṃvāsato jāyate // 1.273	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- asatāṃ saṅga-doṣeṇa satī yāti matir bhramam / eka-rātri-pravāsena kāṣṭhaṃ muñje pralambitam // 1.274	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na hy avijñāta-śīlasya pradātavyaḥ pratiśrayaḥ / mat-kuṇasya ca doṣeṇa hatā manda-visarpiṇī // 1.275	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ehy āgaccha samāviśāsanam idaṃ kasmāc cirād dṛśyase kā vārteti sudurbalo 'si kuśalaṃ prīto 'smi te darśanāt / evaṃ ye samupāgatān praṇayinaḥ pratyālapanty ādarāt teṣāṃ yuktam aśaṅkitena manasā harmyāṇi gantuṃ sadā // 1.276	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
aparaṃ mayāneka-mānuṣāṇām aneka-vidhāni rudhirāṇy āsvāditāny āhāra-doṣāt kaṭu-tikta-kaṣāyāmla-rasāsvādāni na ca kadācin madhura-raktaṃ samāsvāditam / tad yadi tvaṃ prasādaṃ karoṣi tad asya nṛpater vividha-vyañjanānna-pāna-coṣya-lehya-svādv-āhāra-vaśād asya śarīre yan miṣṭaṃ raktaṃ saṃjātaṃ tad-āsvādanena saukhyaṃ sampādayāmi jihvāyā iti / uktaṃ ca- raṅkasya nṛpater vāpi jihvā-saukhyaṃ samaṃ smṛtam / tan-mātraṃ ca smṛtaṃ sāraṃ tad-arthaṃ yatate janaḥ // 1.277	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
yady eva na bhavel loke karma jihvā-pratuṣṭidam / tan na bhṛtyo bhavet kaścit kasyacid vaśago 'tha vā // 1.278	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yad asatyaṃ vaden martyo yad vāsevyaṃ ca sevate / yad gacchati videśaṃ ca tat sarvam udarārthataḥ // 1.279	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svabhāvo nopadeśena śakyate kartum anyathā / sutaptam api pānīyaṃ punar gacchati śītatām // 1.280	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yadi syāc chītalo vahniḥ śītāṃśur dahanātmakaḥ / na svabhāvo 'tra martyānāṃ śakyate kartum anyathā // 1.281	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tyaktāś cābhyantarā yena bāhyāś cābhyantarīkṛtāḥ / sa eva mṛtyum āpnoti yathā rājā kakud-drumaḥ // 1.282	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vajra-lepasya mūrkhasya nārīṇāṃ karkaṭasya ca / eko grahas tu mīnānāṃ nīlīmadyapayor yathā // 1.283	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na yasya ceṣṭitaṃ vidyān na kulaṃ na parākramam / na tasya viśvaset prājño yadīcchec chriyam ātmanaḥ // 1.284	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
te dhanyās te viveka-jñās te sabhyā iha bhūtale / āgacchanti gṛhe yeṣāṃ kāryārthaṃ suhṛdo janāḥ // 1.285	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sampattayaḥ parāyattāḥ sadā cittam anirvṛtam / sva-jīvite'py aviśvāsas teṣāṃ ye rāja-sevakāḥ // 1.286	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- sevayā dhanam icchadbhiḥ sevakaiḥ paśya yat kṛtam / svātantryaṃ yac charīrasya mūḍhais tad api hāritam // 1.287	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tāvaj janmāti-duḥkhāya tato durgatatā sadā / tatrāpi sevayā vṛttir aho duḥkha-paramparā // 1.288	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jīvanto 'pi mṛtāḥ pañca śrūyante kila bhārate / daridro vyādhito mūrkhaḥ pravāsī nitya-sevakaḥ // 1.289	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nāśnāti svacchayotsukyād vinidro na prabudhyate / na niḥśaṅkaṃ vaco brūte sevako 'py atra jīvati // 1.290	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sevā śva-vṛttir ākhyātā yais tair mithyā prajalpitam / svacchandaṃ carati svātra sevakaḥ para-śāsanāt // 1.291	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhū-śayyā brahmacaryaṃ ca kṛśatvaṃ laghu-bhojanam / sevakasya yater yadvad viśeṣaḥ pāpa-dharmajaḥ // 1.292	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śītātapādi-kaṣṭāni sahate yāni sevakaḥ / dhanāya tāni cālpāni yadi dharmān na mucyate // 1.293	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mṛdunāpi suvṛttena suśliṣṭenāpi hāriṇā / modakenāpi kiṃ tena niṣpattir yasya sevayā // 1.294	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo mantraṃ svāmino bhidyāt sācivye san-niyojitaḥ / sa hatvā nṛpa-kāryaṃ tat svayaṃ ca narakaṃ vrajet // 1.295	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yena yasya kṛto bhedaḥ sacivena mahīpateḥ / tenāśastra-vadhas tasya kṛta ity āha nāradaḥ // 1.296	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
viśrambhād yasya yo mṛtyum avāpnoti kathañcana / tasya hatyā tad-utthā sā prāhedaṃ vacanaṃ manuḥ // 1.297	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api brahma-vadhaṃ kṛtvā prāyaścittena śudhyati / tad-arthena vicīrṇena na kathañcit suhṛd-druhaḥ // 1.298	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dattvāpi kanyakāṃ vairī nihantavyo vipaścitā / anyopāyair aśakyo yo hate doṣo na vidyate // 1.299	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛtyākṛtyaṃ na manyeta kṣatriyo yudhi saṅgataḥ / prasupto droṇa-putreṇa dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ purā hataḥ // 1.300	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durjana-gamyā nāryaḥ prāyeṇāsnehavān bhavati rājā / kṛpaṇānusāri ca dhanaṃ megho giri-durga-varṣī ca // 1.301	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
ahaṃ hi saṃmato rājño ya evaṃ manyate kudhīḥ / balīvardaḥ sa vijñeyo viṣāṇa-parivarjitaḥ // 1.302	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
varaṃ vanaṃ varaṃ bhaikṣaṃ varaṃ bhāropajīvanam / varaṃ vyādhir manuṣyāṇāṃ nādhikāreṇa sampadaḥ // 1.303	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yayor eva samaṃ vittaṃ yayor eva samaṃ kulam / tayor maitrī vivāhaś ca na tu puṣṭa-vipuṣṭayoḥ // 1.304	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mṛgā mṛgaiḥ saṅgam anuvrajanti gāvaś ca gobhis turagās turagaiḥ / mūrkhāś ca mūrkhaiḥ sudhiyaḥ sudhībhiḥ samāna-śīla-vyasanena sakhyam // 1.305	upajāti triṣṭubh: ajñātam [11: ttjlg], upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
nimittam uddiśya hi yaḥ prakupyati dhruvaṃ sa tasyāpagame praśāmyati / akāraṇa-dveṣa-paro hi yo bhavet kathaṃ naras taṃ paritoṣayati // 1.306	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
bhaktānām upakāriṇāṃ para-hita-vyāpāra-yuktātmanāṃ sevā-saṃvyavahāra-tattva-viduṣāṃ droha-cyutānām api / vyāpattiḥ skhalitāntareṣu niyatā siddhir bhaved vā na vā tasmād ambupater ivāvani-pateḥ sevā sadā śaṅkinī // 1.307	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
bhāva-snigdhair upakṛtam api dveṣyatāṃ yāti loke sākṣād anyair apakṛtam api prītaye copayāti / durgrāhyatvān nṛpati-manasāṃ naika-bhāvāśrayāṇāṃ sevā-dharmaḥ parama-gahano yoginām apy agamyaḥ // 1.308	mandākrāntā [17: mBnttgg]
prabhoḥ prasādam anyasya na sahantīha sevakāḥ / sapatnya iva saṅkruddhāḥ sapatnyāḥ sukṛtair api // 1.309	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
guṇavattara-pātreṇa chādyante guṇināṃ guṇāḥ / rātrau dīpa-śikhā-kāntir na bhānāv udite sati // 1.310	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bahavaḥ paṇḍitāḥ kṣudrāḥ sarve māyopajīvinaḥ / kuryuḥ kṛtyam akṛtyaṃ vā uṣṭre kākādayo yathā // 1.311	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tac chrutvā vāyasa āha-bhoḥ svāmin ! grāmyo 'yam uṣṭra-nāmā jīva-viśeṣas tava bhojyaḥ / tad vyāpādyatām / siṃha āha-nāhaṃ gṛham āgataṃ hanmi / uktaṃ ca- gṛhaṃ śatrum api prāptaṃ viśvastam akutobhayam / yo hanyāt tasya pāpaṃ syāc chatabrāhmaṇaghātajam // 1.312	upajāti kṛti: ajñātam [20: rrBtymll], ajñātam [20: jmtmyslg], ajñātam [20: ysmrryll], ajñātam [20: mBrmrygl]
na go-pradānaṃ na mahī-pradānaṃ na cānna-dānaṃ hi tathā pradhānam / yathā vadantīha budhāḥ pradhānaṃ sarva-pradāneṣv abhaya-pradānam // 1.313	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
tac chrutvā śṛgāla āha-svāmin yady abhayapradānaṃ dattvā vadhaḥ kriyate tad eṣa doṣo bhavati / punar yadi devapādānāṃ bhaktyā sātmano jīvitavyaṃ prayacchati tan na doṣaḥ / tato yadi sa svayam evātmānaṃ vadhāya niyojayati tad vadhyo 'nyathāsmākaṃ madhyād ekatamo vadhya iti yato devapādāḥ pathyāśinaḥ kṣunnirodhād antyāṃ daśāṃ yāsyanti / tat kim etaiḥ prāṇair asmākaṃ ye svāmyarthe na yāsyanti / aparaṃ paścād apy asmābhir vahni-praveśaḥ kāryo yadi svāmi-pādānāṃ kiṃcid aniṣṭaṃ bhaviṣyati / uktaṃ ca- yasmin kule yaḥ puruṣaḥ pradhānaḥ sa sarva-yatnaiḥ parirakṣaṇīyaḥ / tasmin vinaṣṭe sva-kulaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ na nābhi-bhaṅge hy arakā vahanti // 1.314	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
āpadaṃ prāpnuyāt svāmī yasya bhṛtyasya paśyataḥ / prāṇeṣu vidyamāneṣu sa bhṛtyo narakaṃ vrajet // 1.315	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svāmy-arthe yas tyajet prāṇān bhṛtyo bhakti-samanvitaḥ / sa paraṃ padam āpnoti jarā-maraṇa-varjitam // 1.316	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāka-māṃsaṃ tathocchiṣṭaṃ stokaṃ tad api durbalam / bhakṣitenāpi kiṃ tena yena tṛptir na jāyate // 1.317	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svāmy-āyattāḥ sadā prāṇā bhṛtyānām arjitā dhanaiḥ / yatas tato na doṣo 'sti teṣāṃ grahaṇa-sambhavaḥ // 1.318	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atha tac chrutvā dvīpy āha-bhoḥ sādhūktaṃ bhavatā punar bhavān api svalpa-kāyaḥ sva-jātiś ca nakhāyudhatvād abhakṣya eva / uktaṃ ca- nābhakṣyaṃ bhakṣayet prājñaḥ prāṇaiḥ kaṇṭha-gatair api / viśeṣāt tad api stokaṃ loka-dvaya-vināśakam // 1.319	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tad darśitaṃ tvayātmanaḥ kaulīnyam / atha vā sādhu cedam ucyate- etad-arthaṃ kulīnānāṃ nṛpāḥ kurvanti saṅgraham / ādi-madhyāvasāneṣu na te gacchanti vikriyām // 1.320	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tad apasarāgrataḥ, yenāhaṃ svāminaṃ vijñāpayāmi / tathānuṣṭhite dvīpī praṇamya madotkaṭam āha-svāmin ! kriyatām adya mama prāṇaiḥ prāṇa-yātrā / dīyatām akṣayo vāsaḥ svarge / mama vistāryatāṃ kṣiti-tale prabhūtaṃ yaśaḥ / tan nātra vismayaḥ kāryaḥ / uktaṃ ca- mṛtānāṃ svāminaḥ kārye bhṛtyānām anuvartinām / bhavet svarge akṣayo vāsaḥ kīrtiś ca dharaṇī-tale // 1.321	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
manasāpi svajātyānāṃ yo 'niṣṭāni pracintayet / bhavanti tasya tāny eva iha loke paratra ca // 1.322	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na yajvāno 'pi gacchanti tāṃ gatiṃ naiva yoginaḥ / yāṃ yānti projjhita-prāṇāḥ svāmy-arthe sevakottamāḥ // 1.323	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aśuddha-prakṛtau rājñi janatā nānurajyate / yathā gṛdhra-samāsannaḥ kalahaṃsaḥ samācaret // 1.324	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- gṛdhrākāro 'pi sevyaḥ syād dhaṃsākāraiḥ sabhāsadaiḥ / haṃsākāro 'pi santyājyo gṛdhrākāraiḥ sa tair nṛpaḥ // 1.325	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mṛdunā salilena khanyamā nānyavad dhṛṣyanti girer api sthalāni / upajāpavidāṃ ca karṇa-jāpaiḥ kim u cetāṃsi mṛdūni mānavānām // 1.326	ajñātārdhasamavṛtta [ssjtl, tjrl]
karṇa-viṣeṇa ca bhagnaḥ kiṃ kiṃ na karoti bāliśo lokaḥ / kṣapaṇakatām api dhatte pibati surāṃ naraka-pālena // 1.327	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
pādāhato 'pi dṛḍha-daṇḍa-samāhato 'pi yaṃ daṃṣṭrayā spṛśati taṃ kila hanti sarpaḥ / ko 'py eṣa eva piśunogra-manuṣya-dharmaḥ karṇe paraṃ spṛśati hanti paraṃ samūlam // 1.328	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
tathā ca- aho khala-bhujaṅgasya viparīto vadha-kramaḥ / karṇe lagati cānyasya prāṇair anyo viyujyate // 1.329	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
guror apy avaliptasya kāryākāryam ajānataḥ / utpatha-pratipannasya parityāgo vidhīyate // 1.330	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mahatāṃ yo 'parādhyena dūrastho 'smīti nāśvaset / dīrghau buddhimato bāhū tābhyāṃ hiṃsati hiṃsakam // 1.331	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na tān hi tīrthais tapasā ca lokān svargaiṣiṇo dāna-śataiḥ suvṛttaiḥ / kṣaṇena yān yānti raṇeṣu dhīrāḥ prāṇān samujjhanti hi ye suśīlāḥ // 1.332	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
mṛtaiḥ samprāpyate svargo jīvadbhiḥ kīrtir uttamā / tad ubhāv api śūrāṇāṃ guṇāv etau sudurlabhau // 1.333	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
lalāṭa-deśe rudhiraṃ sravat tu śūrasya yasya praviśec ca vaktre / tat somapānena samaṃ bhavec ca saṅgrāma-yajñe vidhivat pradiṣṭam // 1.334	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
homārthair vidhivat pradāna-vidhinā sad-vipra-vṛndārcanair yajñair bhūri-sudakṣiṇaiḥ suvihitaiḥ samprāpyate yat phalam / sat-tīrthāśrama-vāsa-homa-niyamaiś cāndrāyaṇādyaiḥ kṛtaiḥ pumbhis tat-phalam āhave vinihitaiḥ samprāpyate tat-kṣaṇāt // 1.335	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
balavantaṃ ripuṃ dṛṣṭvā kilātmānaṃ pragopayet / balavadbhiś ca kartavyā śarac-candra-prakāśatā // 1.336	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- śatror vikramam ajñātvā vairam ārabhate hi yaḥ / sa parābhavam āpnoti samudraṣ ṭiṭṭibhād yathā // 1.337	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
baddhvāmbara-cara-mārgaṃ vyapagata-dhūmaṃ sadā mahad bhayadam / manda-matiḥ kaḥ praviśati hutāśanaṃ svecchayā manujaḥ // 1.338	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
mattebha-kumbha-vidalana-kṛta-śramaṃ suptam antaka-pratimam / yama-loka-darśanecchuḥ siṃhaḥ bodhayati ko nāma // 1.339	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
ko gatvā yama-sadanaṃ svayam antakam ādiśaty ajāta-bhayaḥ / prāṇān apahara matto yadi śaktiḥ kācid asti tava // 1.340	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
prāleya-leśa-miśre maruti prābhātike ca vāti jaḍe / guṇa-doṣa-jñaḥ puruṣo jalena kaḥ śītam apanayati // 1.341	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
yaḥ parābhava-santrastaḥ sva-sthānaṃ santyajen naraḥ / tena cet putriṇī mātā tad vandhyā kena kathyate // 1.342	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
utkṣipya ṭiṭṭibhaḥ pādāv āste bha gabhayād divaḥ / sva-citta-kalpito garvaḥ kasya nātrāpi vidyate // 1.343	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
suhṛdāṃ hitakāmānāṃ na karotīha yo vacaḥ / sa kūrma iva durbuddhiḥ kāṣṭhād bhraṣṭo vinaśyati // 1.344	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tyājyaṃ na dhairyaṃ vidhure'pi kāle dhairyāt kadācid gatim āpnuyāt saḥ / yathā samudre'pi ca pota-bhaṅge sāṃyātriko vāñchati tartum eva // 1.345	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
aparaṃ ca- mitrārthe bāndhavārthe ca buddhimān yatate sadā / jātāsv āpatsu yatnena jagādedaṃ vaco manuḥ // 1.346	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
anāgata-vidhātā ca pratyutpanna-matis tathā / dvāv etau sukham edhete yad-bhaviṣyo vinaśyati // 1.347	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aśaktair balinaḥ śatroḥ kartavyaṃ prapalāyanam / saṃśritavyo 'thavā durgo nānyā teṣāṃ gatir bhavet // 1.348	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vidyamānā gatir yeṣām anyatrāpi sukhāvahā / te na paśyanti vidvāṃso deha-bhaṅgaṃ kula-kṣayam // 1.349	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
para-deśa-bhayāt bhītā bahu-māyā napuṃsakāḥ / sva-deśe nidhanaṃ yānti kākāḥ kāpuruṣā mṛgāḥ // 1.350	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasyāsti sarvatra gatiḥ sa kasmāt sva-deśa-rāgeṇa hi yāti nāśam / tātasya kūpo 'yam iti bruvāṇāḥ kṣāra-jalaṃ kāpuruṣāḥ pibanti // 1.351	upajāti triṣṭubh: ajñātam [11: Btjgl], upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
arakṣitaṃ tiṣṭhati daiva-rakṣitaṃ surakṣitaṃ daiva-hataṃ vinaśyati / jīvaty anātho 'pi vane visarjitaḥ kṛta-prayatno 'pi gṛhe na jīvati // 1.352	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
puṃsām asamarthānām upadravāyātmano bhavet kopaḥ / piṭharaṃ jvalad-atimātraṃ nija-pārśvān eva dahatitarām // 1.353	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- aviditvātmanaḥ śaktiṃ parasya na samutsukaḥ / gacchann abhimukho vahnau nāśaṃ yāti pataṅgavat // 1.354	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
viśeṣāt paripūrṇasya yāti śatror amarṣaṇaḥ / ābhimukhyaṃ śaśāṅkasya yathādyāpi vidhuntudaḥ // 1.355	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- pramāṇād adhikasyāpi gaṇḍa-śyāma-mada-cyuteḥ / padaṃ mūrdhni samādhatte kesarī matta-dantinaḥ // 1.356	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- bālasyāpi raveḥ pādāḥ patanty upari bhūbhṛtām / tejasā saha jātānāṃ vayaḥ kutropayujyate // 1.357	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
hastau sthūlataraḥ sa cāṅkuśa-vaśaḥ kiṃ hasti-mātro 'ṅkuśo dīpe prajvalite praṇaśyati tamaḥ kiṃ dīpa-mātraṃ tamaḥ / vajreṇāpi hatāḥ patanti girayaḥ kiṃ vajra-mātro giris tejo yasya virājate sa balavān sthūleṣu kaḥ pratyayaḥ // 1.358	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
anirvedaḥ śriyo mūlaṃ cañcur me loha-sannibhā / aho-rātrāṇi dīrghāṇi samudraḥ kiṃ na śuṣyati // 1.359	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
duradhigamaḥ para-bhāgo yāvat puruṣeṇa pauruṣaṃ na kṛtam / jayati tulām adhirūḍho bhāsvān api jalada-paṭalāni // 1.360	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
bahūnām apy asārāṇāṃ samvāyo hi durjayaḥ / tṛṇair āveṣṭyate rajjur yathā nāgo 'pi baddhyate // 1.361	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- caṭakākāṣṭha-kūṭena makṣikā-dardurais tathā / mahājana-virodhena kuñjaraḥ pralayaṃ gataḥ // 1.362	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
naṣṭaṃ mṛtam atikrāntaṃ nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ / paṇḍitānāṃ ca mūrkhāṇāṃ viśeṣo 'yaṃ yataḥ smṛtaḥ // 1.363	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- aśocyānīha bhūtāni yo mūḍhas tāni śocati / tad-duḥkhāl labhate duḥkhaṃ dvāv anarthau niṣevate // 1.364	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
anyac ca- śleṣmāśru bāndhavair muktaṃ preto bhuṅkte yato 'vaśaḥ / tasmān na roditavyaṃ hi kriyāḥ kāryāś ca śaktitaḥ // 1.365	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
āpadi yenopakṛtaṃ yena ca hasitaṃ daśāsu viṣamāsu / upakṛtya tayor ubhayoḥ punar api jātaṃ naraṃ manye // 1.366	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
sa suhṛd-vyasane yaḥ syād anya-jāty-udbhavo 'pi san / vṛddhau sarvo 'pi mitraṃ syāt sarveṣām eva dehinām // 1.367	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sa suhṛd-vyasane yaḥ syāt sa putro yas tu bhaktimān / sa bhṛtyo yo vidheyajñaḥ sā bhāryā yatra nirvṛtiḥ // 1.368	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
punaḥ pratyupakārāya mitrāṇāṃ kriyate priyam / yat punar mitra-mitrasya kāryaṃ mitrair na kiṃ kṛtam // 1.369	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hitaiḥ sādhu-samācāraiḥ śāstrajñair mati-śālibhiḥ / kathañcin na vikalpante vidvadbhiś cintitā nayāḥ // 1.370	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
abalaḥ pronnataṃ śatruṃ yo yāti mada-mohitaḥ / yuddhārthaṃ sa nivarteta śīrṇa-danto yathā gajaḥ // 1.371	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
suhṛdi nirantara-racite guṇavati bhṛtye'nuvartini kalatre / svāmini śakti-samete nivedya duḥkhaṃ sukhī bhavati // 1.372	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
kva kasya karma saṃvīkṣya karoty anyo 'pi garhitam / gatānugatiko loko na lokaḥ pāramārthikaḥ // 1.373	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
cāṭu-taskara-durvṛttais tathā sāhasikādibhiḥ / pīḍyamānāḥ prajā rakṣyāḥ kaṭūcchadmādibhis tathā // 1.374	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prajānāṃ dharma-ṣaḍ-bhāgo rājño bhavati rakṣituḥ / adharmād api ṣaḍ-bhāgo jāyate yo na rakṣati // 1.375	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prajā-pīḍana-santāpāt samudbhūto hutāśanaḥ / rājñaḥ śriyaṃ kulaṃ prāṇān nādagdhvā vinivartate // 1.376	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rājā bandhur abandhūnāṃ rājā cakṣur acakṣuṣām / rājā pitā ca mātā ca sarveṣāṃ nyāya-vartinām // 1.377	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
phalārthī pārthivo lokān pālayed yatnam āsthitaḥ / dāna-mānādi-toyena mālākāro 'ṅkurān iva // 1.378	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā bījāṅkuraḥ sūkṣmaḥ pratnenābhirakṣitaḥ / phala-prado bhavet kāle tadval lokaḥ surakṣitaḥ // 1.379	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
hiraṇya-dhānya-ratnāni yānāni vividhāni ca / tathānyad api yat kiñcit prajābhyaḥ syān nṛpasya tat // 1.380	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo na vetti guṇān yasya na taṃ seveta paṇḍitaḥ / na hi tasmāt phalaṃ kiñcit sukṛṣṭād ūṣarād iva // 1.381	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhaktaṃ śaktaṃ kulīnaṃ ca na bhṛtyam avamānayet / putraval lālayen nityaṃ ya icchec chriyam ātmanaḥ // 1.382	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- rājā tuṣṭo 'pi bhṛtyānām artha-mātraṃ prayacchati / te tu sammānitās tasya prāṇair apy upakurvate // 1.383	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yena syāl laghutā vātha pīḍā citte prabhoḥ kvacit / prāṇa-tyāge'pi tat karma na kuryāt kula-sevakaḥ // 1.384	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhṛtyāparādhajo daṇḍaḥ svāmino jāyate yataḥ / tena lajjāpi tasyotthā na bhṛtyasya tathā punaḥ // 1.385	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tyajed ekaṃ kulasyārthe grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet / grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe svātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet // 1.386	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
āpad-arthe dhanaṃ rakṣed dārān rakṣed dhanair api / ātmānaṃ satataṃ rakṣed dārair api dhanair api // 1.387	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api putra-kalatrair vā prāṇān rakṣeta paṇḍitaḥ / vidyamānair yatas taiḥ syāt sarvaṃ bhūyo 'pi dehinām // 1.388	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yena kenāpy upāyena śubhenāpy aśubhena vā / uddhared dīnam ātmānaṃ samartho dharmam ācaret // 1.389	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yo māyāṃ kurute mūḍhaḥ prāṇa-tyāge dhanādiṣu / tasya prāṇāḥ praṇaśyanti tair naṣṭair naṣṭam eva tat // 1.390	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
parāṅmukhe'pi daive'tra kṛtyaṃ kāryaṃ vipaścitā / ātma-doṣa-vināśāya sva-citta-stambhanāya ca // 1.391	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
udyoginaṃ puruṣa-siṃham upaiti lakṣmīr daivena deyam iti kāpuruṣā vadanti / daivaṃ nihatya kuru pauruṣam ātma-śaktyā yatne kṛte yadi na sidhyati ko 'tra doṣaḥ // 1.392	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
aviruddhaṃ sukha-sthaṃ yo duḥkha-mārge niyojayet / janma-janmāntare duḥkhī sa naraḥ syād asaṃśayam // 1.393	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ghātayitum eva nīcaḥ para-kāryaṃ vetti na prasādayitum / pātayitum asti śaktir vāyor vṛkṣaṃ na connamitum // 1.394	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
jāta-mātraṃ na yaḥ śatruṃ vyādhiṃ ca praśamaṃ nayet / mahā-balo 'pi tenaiva vṛddhiṃ prāpya sa hanyate // 1.395	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pitṛ-paitāmahaṃ sthānaṃ yo yasyātra jigīṣate / sa tasya sahajaḥ śatrur ucchedyo 'pi priye sthitaḥ // 1.396	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dadyāt sādhur yadi nija-pade durjanāya praveśaṃ tan-nāśāya prabhavati tato vāñchamānaḥ svayaṃ saḥ / tasmād deyo vipula-matibhir nāvakāśo 'dhamānāṃ jārāpi syād gṛha-patir iti śrūyate vākyato 'tra // 1.397	mandākrāntā [17: mBnttgg]
nistriṃśaṃ hṛdayaṃ kṛtvā vāṇīm ikṣu-rasopāmām / vikalpo 'tra na kartavyo hanyāt tatrāpakāriṇam // 1.398	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
parasya pīḍanaṃ kurvan svārtha-siddhiṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ / mūḍha-buddhir na bhakṣeta vane caturako yathā // 1.399	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
avadhyaṃ vāthavāgamyam akṛtyaṃ nāsti kiṃcana / loke buddhimatām atra tasmāt tāṃ yojayāmy aham // 1.400	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
agamyāni pumān yāti yo 'sevyāṃś ca niṣevate / sa mṛtyum upagṛhṇāti garbham aśvatarī yathā // 1.401	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dharmārthaṃ yatatām apīha vipado devād yadi syuḥ kvacit tat tāsām upaśāntaye sumatibhiḥ kāryo viśeṣān nayaḥ / loke khyātim upāgatātra sakale lokoktir eṣā yato dagdhānāṃ kila vahninā hita-karaḥ seko 'pi tasyodbhavaḥ // 1.402	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
loke'thavā tanu-bhṛtāṃ nija-karma-pākaṃ nityaṃ samāśritavatāṃ suhita-kriyāṇām / bhāvārjitaṃ śubham athāpy aśubhaṃ nikāmaṃ yad bhāvi tad bhavati nātra vicāra-hetuḥ // 1.403	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
mahadbhiḥ spardhamānasya vipad eva garīyasī / danta-bhaṅge'pi nāgānāṃ ślāghyo giri-vidāraṇe // 1.404	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- mahato 'pi kṣayaṃ labdhvā ślāghyaṃ nīco 'pi gacchati / dānārthī madhupo yadvad gaja-karṇa-samāhataḥ // 1.405	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
antar-līna-bhujaṅgamaṃ gṛham ivāntaḥsthogra-siṃhaṃ vanaṃ grāhākīrṇam ivābhirāma-kamala-cchāyā-sanāthaṃ saraḥ / kālenārya-janāpavāda-piśunaiḥ kṣudrair anāryaiḥ śritaṃ duḥkhena pravigāhyate sa-cakitaṃ rājñāṃ manaḥ sāmayam // 1.406	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
kāryāṇy uttama-daṇḍa-sāhasa-phalāny āyāsa-sādhyāni ye prītyā saṃśamayanti nīti-kuśalāḥ sāmnaiva te mantriṇaḥ / niḥsārālpa-phalāni ye tv avidhinā vāñchanti daṇḍodyamais teṣāṃ durnaya-ceṣṭitair narapater āropyate śrīs tulām // 1.407	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
sāmādi-daṇḍa-paryanto nayaḥ proktaḥ svayambhuvā / teṣāṃ daṇḍas tu pāpīyāṃs taṃ paścād viniyojayet // 1.408	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- sāmnaiva yatra siddhir na tatra daṇḍo budhena viniyojyaḥ / pittaṃ yadi śarkarayā śāmyati ko 'rthaḥ paṭolena // 1.409	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tathā ca- ādau sāma prayoktavyaṃ puruṣeṇa vijānatā / sāma-sādhyāni kāryāṇi vikriyāṃ yānti na kvacit // 1.410	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na candreṇa na cāuṣadhyā na sūryeṇa na vahninā / sāmnaiva vilayaṃ yāti vidveṣa-prabhavaṃ tamaḥ // 1.411	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mantriṇāṃ bhinna-sandhāne bhiṣajāṃ sāṃnipātike / karmaṇi vyajyate prajñā susthe ko vā na paṇḍitaḥ // 1.412	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- ghātayitum eva nīcaḥ para-kāryaṃ vetti na prasādhayitum / pātayitum eva śaktir nākhoruddhartum anna-piṭakam // 1.413	ajñātasamavṛtta [8: tBlg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
narādhipā nīca-janānuvartino budhopadiṣṭena pathā na yānti ye / viśanty ato durgama-mārga-nirgamaṃ samasta-sambādham anartha-pañjaram // 1.414	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
guṇālayo 'py asan mantrī nṛpatir nādhigamyate / prasanna-svādu-salilo duṣṭa-grāhyo yathā hradaḥ // 1.415	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
citrāsvāda-kathair bhṛtyair anāyāsita-kārmukaiḥ / ye ramante nṛpās teṣāṃ ramante ripavaḥ śriyā // 1.416	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nānāmyaṃ namate dāru nāśmani syāt kṣura-kriyā / sūcī-mukhaṃ vijānīhi nāśiṣyāyopaśyate // 1.417	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
muhur vighnita-karmāṇaṃ dyūta-kāraṃ parājitam / nālāpayed viveka-jño yadīcchet siddhim ātmanaḥ // 1.418	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- ākheṭakaṃ vṛthākleśaṃ mūrkhaṃ vyasanasaṃsthitam / samālāpena yo yuṅkte sa gacchati parābhavam // 1.419	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
upadeśo hi mūrkhāṇāṃ prakopāya na śāntaye / payaḥ-pānaṃ bhujaṅgānāṃ kevalaṃ viṣa-vardhanam // 1.420	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- upadeśo na dātavyo yādṛśe tādṛśe nare / paśya vānaramūrkheṇa sugṛhī nirgṛhīkṛtā // 1.421	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kasmiṃścid vane śamī-vṛkṣa-śākhālambita-vasathaṃ kṛtvāraṇya-caṭaka-dampatī prativasataḥ sma / atha kadācit tayoḥ sukha-saṃsthayor hemanta-megho mandaṃ mandaṃ varṣitum ārabdhaḥ / atrāntare kaścic chākhā-mṛgo vātāsāra-samāhataḥ proddhūṣita-śarīro dantavīṇāṃ vādayan vepamānas tasyāḥ śamyā mūlam āsādyopaviṣṭaḥ / atha taṃ tādṛṣam avalokya caṭakā prāha-bho bhadra ! hasta-pāda-samopeto dṛśyase puruṣākṛtiḥ / śītena bhidyase mūḍha kathaṃ na kuruṣe gṛham // 1.422	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
sūcī-mukhi durācārā raṇḍā paṇḍita-vādinī / nāśaṅkate prajalpantī tat kim enāṃ na hanmy aham // 1.423	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evaṃ pralapya tām āha-mugdhe ! kiṃ mama cintayā tava prayojanam ? uktaṃ ca- vācyaṃ śraddhā-sametasya pṛcchateś ca viśeṣataḥ / proktaṃ śraddhā-vihīnasya araṇya-ruditopamam // 1.424	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ karoty eva pāṇḍityam asthāne viniyojitam / andhakāra-praticchanne ghaṭe dīpa ivāhitaḥ // 1.425	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jātaḥ putro 'nujātaś ca atijātas tathaiva ca / apajātaś ca loke'smin mantavyāḥ śāstra-vedibhiḥ // 1.426	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mātṛ-tulya-guṇo jātas tv anujātaḥ pituḥ samaḥ / atijāto 'dhikas tasmād apajāto 'dhamādhamaḥ // 1.427	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
apy ātmano vināśaṃ gaṇayati na khalaḥ para-vyasana-hṛṣṭaḥ / prāyo mastaka-nāśe samara-mukhe nṛtyati kabandhaḥ // 1.428	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
dharma-buddhiḥ kubuddhiś ca dvāv etau viditau mama / putreṇa vyartha-pāṇḍityāt pitā dhūmena ghātitaḥ // 1.429	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
deśāntareṣu bahu-vidha-bhāṣā-veṣādi yena na jñātam / bhramatā dharaṇī-pīṭhe tasya phalaṃ janmano vyartham // 1.430	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- vidyāṃ vittaṃ śilpaṃ tāvan nāpnoti mānavaḥ samyak / yāvad vrajati na bhūmau deśād deśāntaraṃ hṛṣṭaḥ // 1.431	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
prāpta-vidyārtha-śilpānāṃ deśāntara-nivāsinām / krośa-mātro 'pi bhū-bhāgaḥ śata-yojanavad bhavet // 1.432	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na vittaṃ darśayet prājñaḥ kasyacit svalpam apy aho / muner api yatas tasya darśanāc calate manaḥ // 1.433	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yathāmiṣaṃ jale matsyair bhakṣyate śvāpadair bhuvi / ākāśe pakṣibhiś caiva tathā sarvatra vittavān // 1.434	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mātṛvat para-dārāṇi para-dravyāṇi loṣṭavat / ātmavat sarva-bhūtāni vīkṣante dharma-buddhayaḥ // 1.435	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vivāde anviṣyate patraṃ tad-abhāve'pi sākṣiṇaḥ / sākṣy abhāvāt tato divyaṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ // 1.436	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
antyajo 'pi yadā sākṣī vivāde samprajāyate / na tatra yujyate divyaṃ kiṃ punar vana-devatāḥ // 1.437	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ādityacandrāv anilo 'nalaś ca dyaur bhūmir āpo hṛdayaṃ yamaś ca / ahaś ca rātriś ca ubhe ca sandhye dharmo hi jānāti narasya vṛttam // 1.438	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
upāyaṃ cintayet prājñas tathāpāyam api cintayet / paśyato baka-mūrkhasya nakulair bhakṣitāḥ sutāḥ // 1.439	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
navanīta-samāṃ vāṇīṃ kṛtvā cittaṃ tu nirdayam / tathā prabodhyate śatruḥ sānvayo mriyate yathā // 1.440	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yatnād api kaḥ paśyec chikhinām āhāra-niḥsaraṇa-mārgam / yadi jalada-dhvani-muditās ta eva mūḍhā na nṛtyeyuḥ // 1.441	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tulāṃ loha-sahasrasya yatra khādanti mūṣakāḥ / rājaṃs tatra harec chyeno bālakaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ // 1.442	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yatra deśe atha vā sthāne bhogān bhuktvā svavīryataḥ / tasmin vibhavahīno yo vaset sa puruṣādhamaḥ // 1.443	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yenāhaṃkārayuktena ciraṃ vilasitaṃ purā / dīnaṃ vadati tatraiva yaḥ pareṣāṃ sa ninditaḥ // 1.444	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na bhaktyā kasyacit ko 'pi priyaṃ prakurute naraḥ / muktvā bhayaṃ pralobhaṃ vā kārya-kāraṇam eva vā // 1.445	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- atyādaro bhaved yatra kārya-kāraṇa-varjitaḥ / tatra śaṅkā prakartavyā pariṇāme'sukhāvahā // 1.446	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tulāṃ loha-sahasrasya yatra khādanti mūṣikāḥ / rājaṃs tatra harec chyeno bālakaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ // 1.447	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prāyeṇātra kulānvitaṃ kukulajāḥ śrī-vallabhaṃ durbhagā dātāraṃ kṛpaṇā ṛjūn anṛjavo vitte sthitaṃ nirdhanāḥ / vairūpyopahṛtāś ca kānta-vapuṣaṃ dharmāśrayaṃ pāpino nānā-śāstra-vicakṣaṇaṃ ca puruṣaṃ nindanti mūrkhāḥ sadā // 1.448	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
tathā ca- mūrkhāṇāṃ paṇḍitā dveṣyā nirdhanānāṃ mahādhanāḥ / vratinaḥ pāpa-śīlānām asatīnāṃ kula-striyaḥ // 1.449	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
paṇḍito 'pi varaṃ śatrur na mūrkho hita-kārakaḥ / vānareṇa hato rājā viprāś cīreṇa rakṣitāḥ // 1.450	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
asatī bhavati salajjā kṣāraṃ nīraṃ ca śītalaṃ bhavati / dambhī bhavati vivekī priyavaktā bhavati dhūrtajanaḥ // 1.451	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
mṛtyor bibheṣi kiṃ bāla na sa bhītaṃ vimuñcati / adya vābda-śatānte vā mṛtyur vai prāṇināṃ dhruvaḥ // 1.452	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe ca prāṇa-tyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ / sūryasya maṇḍalaṃ bhittvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim // 1.453	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mitra-drohī kṛtaghnaś ca yaś ca viśvāsa-ghātakaḥ / te narā narakaṃ yānti yāvac candra-divākarau // 1.454	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhūmi-kṣaye rāja-vināśa eva bhṛtyasya vā buddhimato vināśe / no yuktam uktaṃ hy anayoḥ samatvaṃ naṣṭāpi bhūmiḥ sulabhā na bhṛtyāḥ // 1.455	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
ukto bhavati yaḥ pūrvaṃ guṇavān iti saṃsadi / na tasya doṣo vaktavyaḥ pratijñā-bhaṅga-bhīruṇā // 1.456	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
pitā vā yadi vā bhrātā putro bhāryāthavā suhṛt / prāṇa-drohaṃ yadā gacched dhantavyo nāsti pātakam // 1.457	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rājā ghṛṇī brāhmaṇaḥ sarva-bhakṣī strī cātrapā duṣṭamatiḥ sahāyaḥ / preṣyaḥ pratīpo 'dhikṛtaḥ prasādī tyājyā amī yaś ca kṛtaṃ na vetti // 1.458	upajāti triṣṭubh: ajñātam [11: tttgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
satyānṛtā ca paruṣā priya-vādinī ca hiṃsrā dayālur api cārtha-parā vadānyā / bhūri-vyathā pracura-vitta-samāgamā ca veśyāṅganeva nṛpa-nītir aneka-rūpā // 1.459	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
api ca- akṛtopadravaḥ kaścin mahān api na pūjyate / pūjayanti narā nāgān na tārkṣyaṃ nāga-ghātinam // 1.460	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- aśocyān anvaśocas tvaṃ prajñā-vādāṃś ca bhāṣase / gatāsūn agatāsūṃś ca nānuśocanti paṇḍitāḥ // 1.461	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
asādhanā api prājñā buddhimanot bahu-śrutāḥ / sādhayanty āśu kāryāṇi kākākhu-mṛga-kūrmavat // 2.1	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
chāyā-supta-mṛgaḥ śakunta-nivahair viṣvag-vilupta-cchadaḥ kīṭair āvṛta-koṭaraḥ kapi-kulaiḥ skandhe kṛta-praśrayaḥ / viśrabdhaṃ madhupair nipīta-kusumaḥ ślāghyaḥ sa eva drumaḥ sarvāṅgair bahu-sattva-saṅga-sukhado bhū-bhāra-bhūto 'paraḥ // 2.2	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
jihvā-laulya-prasaktānāṃ jala-madhya-nivāsinām / acintito vadho 'jñānāṃ mīnānām iva jāyate // 2.3	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
paulastyaḥ katham anya-dāra-haraṇe doṣaṃ na vijñātavān rāmeṇāpi kathaṃ na hema-hariṇasyāsambhavo lakṣitaḥ / akṣaiś cāpi yudhiṣṭhireṇa sahasā prāpto hy anarthaḥ kathaṃ pratyāsanna-vipatti-mūḍha-manasāṃ prāyo matiḥ kṣīyate // 2.4	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
tathā ca- kṛtānta-pāśa-baddhānāṃ daivopahata-cetasām / buddhayaḥ kubja-gāminyo bhavanti mahatām api // 2.5	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
vyasaneṣv eva sarveṣu yasya buddhir na hīyate / sa teṣāṃ pāram abhyeti tat-prabhāvād asaṃśayam // 2.6	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sampattau ca vipattau ca mahatām eka-rūpatā / udaye savitā rakto raktaś cāsta-maye tathā // 2.7	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tantavo 'py āyatā nityaṃ tantavo bahulāḥ samāḥ / bahūn bahutvād āyāsān sahantīty upamā satām // 2.8	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
jālam ādāya gacchanti saṃhatāḥ pakṣiṇo 'py amī / yāvac ca vivadiṣyante patiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ // 2.9	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nahi bhavati yan na bhāvyaṃ bhavati ca bhāvyaṃ vināpi yatnena / karatala-gatam api naśyati yasya hi bhavitavyatā nāsti // 2.10	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- parāṅmukhe vidhau cet syāt kathañcid draviṇodayaḥ / tat so 'nyad api saṅgṛhya yāti śaṅkha-nidhir yathā // 2.11	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
sarveṣām eva martyānāṃ vyasane samupasthite / vāṅ-mātreṇāpi sāhāyyaṃ mitrād anyo na sandadhe // 2.12	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
daṃṣṭrā-virahitaḥ sarpo mada-hīno yathā gajaḥ / sarveṣāṃ jāyate vaśyo durga-hīnas tathā nṛpaḥ // 2.13	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- na gajānāṃ sahasreṇa na ca lakṣeṇa vājinām / tat karma sidhyate rājñāṃ dureṇaikena yad raṇe // 2.14	upagīti (12, 15, 12, 15)
śatam eko 'pi sandhatte prākārastho dhanurdharaḥ / tasmād durgaṃ praśaṃsanti nīti-śāstra-vido janāḥ // 2.15	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
suhṛdaḥ sneha-sampannā locanānanda-dāyinaḥ / gṛhe gṛhavatāṃ nityaṃ nāgacchanti mahātmanām // 2.16	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ādityasyodayaṃ tāta tāmbūlaṃ bhāratī kathā / iṣṭā bhāryā sumitraṃ ca apūrvāṇi dine dine // 2.17	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
suhṛdo bhavane yasya samāgacchanti nityaśaḥ / citte ca tasya saukhyasya na kiñcit pratimaṃ sukham // 2.18	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasmāc ca yena ca yadā ca yathā ca yac ca yāvac ca yatra ca śubhāśubham ātma-karma / tasmāc ca tena ca tadā ca tathā ca tac ca tāvac ca tatra ca kṛtānta-vaśād upaiti // 2.19	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
ardhārdhād yojana-śatād āmiṣaṃ vīkṣate khagaḥ / so 'pi pārśva-sthitaṃ daivād bandhanaṃ na ca paśyati // 2.20	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
ravi-niśākarayor graha-pīḍanaṃ gaja-bhujaṅga-vihaṅgama-bandhanam / matimatāṃ ca nirīkṣya daridratā vidhir aho balavān iti me matiḥ // 2.21	drutavilambita [12: nBBr]
vyomaikānta-vicāriṇo 'pi vihagāḥ samprāpnuvanty āpadaṃ badhyante nipuṇair agādha-salilān mīnāḥ samudrād api / durnītaṃ kim ihāsti kiṃ ca sukṛtaṃ kaḥ sthāna-lābhe guṇaḥ kālaḥ sarva-janān prasārita-karo gṛhṇāti dūrād api // 2.22	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
yaḥ saṃmānaṃ sadā dhatte bhṛtyānāṃ kṣitipo 'dhikam / vittābhāve'pi taṃ dṛṣṭvā te tyajanti na karhicit // 2.23	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- viśvāsaḥ sampadāṃ mūlaṃ tena yūthapatir gajaḥ / siṃho mṛgādhipatye'pi na mṛgaiḥ parivāryate // 2.24	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
sadācāreṣu bhṛtyeṣu saṃsīdatsu ca yaḥ prabhuḥ / sukhī syān narakaṃ yāti paratreha ca sīdati // 2.25	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāruṇyaṃ saṃvibhāgaś ca yathā bhṛtyeṣu lakṣyate / cittenānena te śaṅkyā trailokyasyāpi nāthatā // 2.26	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mitravān sādhayaty arthān duḥsādhyān api vai yataḥ / tasmān mitrāṇi kurvīta samānāny eva cātmanaḥ // 2.27	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api sampūrṇatā-yuktaiḥ kartavyāḥ suhṛdo budhaiḥ / nadīśaḥ paripūrṇo 'pi candrodayam apekṣate // 2.28	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yayor eva samaṃ vittaṃ yayor eva samaṃ kulam / tayor maitrī vivāhaś ca na tu puṣṭa-vipuṣṭayoḥ // 2.29	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yo mitraṃ kurute mūḍha ātmano 'sadṛśaṃ kudhīḥ / hīnaṃ vāpy adhikaṃ vāpi hāsyatāṃ yāty asau janaḥ // 2.30	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
vairiṇā na hi sandadhyāt suśliṣṭenāpi sandhinā / sutaptam api pānīyaṃ śamayaty eva pāvakam // 2.31	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛtrimaṃ nāśam abhyeti vairaṃ drāk kṛtrimair guṇaiḥ / prāṇa-dānaṃ vinā vairaṃ sahajaṃ yāti na kṣayam // 2.32	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāraṇān mitratām eti kāraṇād yāti śatrutām / tasmān mitratvam evātra yojyaṃ vairaṃ na dhīmatā // 2.33	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sakṛd duṣṭam apīṣṭaṃ yaḥ punaḥ sandhātum icchati / sa mṛtyum upagṛhṇāti garbham aśvatarī yathā // 2.34	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
siṃho vyākaraṇasya kartur aharat prāṇān piryān pāṇiner mīmāṃsā-kṛtam unmamātha sahasā hastī muniṃ jaiminim / chando-jñāna-nidhiṃ jaghāna makaro velā-taṭe piṅgalam ajñānāvṛta-cetasām atiruṣā ko 'rthas tiraścāṃ guṇaiḥ // 2.35	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
upakārāc ca lokānāṃ nimittān mṛga-pakṣiṇām / bhayāl lobhāc ca mūrkhāṇāṃ maitrī syād darśanāt satām // 2.36	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mṛd-ghaṭa iva sukha-bhedyo duḥsandhānaś ca durjano bhavati / sujanas tu kanaka-ghaṭa iva durbhedaḥ sukara-sandhiś ca // 2.37	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
ikṣor agrāt kramaśaḥ parvaṇi parvaṇi yathā rasa-viśeṣaḥ / tadvat sajjana-maitrī-viparītānāṃ tu viparītā // 2.38	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- ārambha-gurvī kṣayiṇī krameṇa laghvī purā vṛddhimatī ca paścāt / dinasya pūrvārdha-parārdha-bhinnā chāyeva maitrī khala-sajjanānām // 2.39	indravajrā [11: ttjgg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
