śapathaiḥ sandhitasyāpi na viśvāsaṃ vrajed ripoḥ / śrūyate śapathaṃ kṛtvā vṛtraḥ śakreṇa sūditaḥ // 2.40	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na viśvāsaṃ vinā śatrur devānām api sidhyati / viśvāsāt tridaśendreṇa diter garbho vidāritaḥ // 2.41	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- bṛhaspater api prājñas tasmān naivātra viśvaset / ya icched ātmano buddhim āyuṣyaṃ ca sukhāni ca // 2.42	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- susūkṣmeṇāpi randhreṇa praviśyābhyantaraṃ ripuḥ / nāśayec ca śanaiḥ paścāt plavaṃ salila-pūravat // 2.43	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na viśvased aviśvaste viśvaste'pi na viśvaset / viśvāsād bhayam utpannaṃ mūlāny api nikṛntati // 2.44	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na badhyate hy aviśvasto durbalo 'pi balotkaṭaiḥ / viśvastāś cāśu badhyante balavanto 'pi durbalaiḥ // 2.45	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sukṛtyaṃ viṣṇu-guptasya mitrāptir bhārgavasya ca / bṛhaspater aviśvāso nītir-sandhis tridhā sthitaḥ // 2.46	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- mahatāpy artha-sāreṇa yo viśvasiti śatruṣu / bhāryāsu suviraktāsu tad-antaṃ tasya jīvitam // 2.47	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
satāṃ sāptapadaṃ maitram ity āhur vibudhā janāḥ / tasmāt tvaṃ mitratāṃ prāpto vacanaṃ mama tac chṛṇu // 2.48	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhīta-bhītaiḥ purā śatrur mandaṃ mandaṃ visarpati / bhūmau prahelayā paścāj jāra-hasto 'ṅganāsv iva // 2.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dadāti pratigṛhṇāti guhyam ākhyāti pṛcchati / bhuṅkte bhojāyate caiva ṣaḍ-vidhaṃ prīti-lakṣaṇam // 2.50	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nopakāraṃ vinā prītiḥ kathañcit kasyacid bhavet / upayācita-dānena yato devā abhīṣṭadāḥ // 2.51	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāvat prītir bhavel loke yāvad dānaṃ pradīyate / vatsaḥ kṣīra-kṣayaṃ dṛṣṭvā parityajati mātaram // 2.52	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
paśya dānasya māhātmyaṃ sadyaḥ pratyaya-kārakam / yat-prabhāvād api dveṣo mitratāṃ yāti tat-kṣaṇāt // 2.53	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
putrād api priyataraṃ khalu tena dānaṃ manye paśor api viveka-vivarjitasya / datte khale tu nikhilaṃ khalu yena dugdhaṃ nityaṃ dadāti mahiṣī sasutāpi paśya // 2.54	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
kiṃ bahunā- prītiṃ nirantarāṃ kṛtvā durbhedyāṃ nakha-māṃsavat / mūṣako vāyasaś caiva gatau kṛtrima-mitratām // 2.55	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
anāvṛṣṭi-hate deśe sasye ca pralayaṃ gate / dhanyās tāta na paśyanti deśa-bhaṅgaṃ kula-kṣayam // 2.56	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ko 'tibhāraḥ samarthānāṃ kiṃ dūraṃ vyavasāyinām / ko videśaḥ savidyānāṃ kaḥ paraḥ priya-vādinām // 2.57	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vidvattvaṃ ca nṛpatvaṃ ca naiva tulyaṃ kadācana / sva-deśe pūjyate rājā vidvān sarvatra pūjyate // 2.58	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sa āha- sampātaṃ vipra-pātaṃ ca mahā-pātaṃ nipātanam / vakraṃ tiryak tathā cordhvam aṣṭamaṃ laghu-saṃjñakam // 2.59	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ candanaiḥ sa-karpūrais tuhinaiḥ kiṃ ca śītalaiḥ / sarve te mitra-gātrasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm // 2.60	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- kenāmṛtam idaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ mitram ity akṣara-dvayam / āpadāṃ ca paritrāṇaṃ śoka-santāpa-bheṣajam // 2.61	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya na jñāyate vīryaṃ na kulaṃ na viceṣṭitam / na tena saṅgatiṃ kuryād ity uvāca bṛhaspatiḥ // 2.62	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
amṛtasya pravāhaiḥ kiṃ kāya-kṣālana-sambhavaiḥ / cirān mitra-pariṣvaṅgo yo 'sau mūlya-vivarjitaḥ // 2.63	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
parjanyasya yathā dhārā yathā ca divi tārakāḥ / sikatā-reṇavo yadvat saṅkhyayā parivarjitā // 2.64	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
guṇāḥ saṅkhyā-parityaktās tadvad asya mahātmanaḥ / paraṃ nirvedam āpannaḥ samprāpto 'yaṃ tavāntikam // 2.65	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ehy āgaccha samāviśāsanam idaṃ kasmāc cirād dṛśyase kā vārteti sudurbalo 'si kuśalaṃ prīto 'smi te darśanāt / evaṃ ye samupāgatān praṇayinaḥ pratyālapanty ādarāt teṣāṃ yuktam aśaṅkitena manasā harmyāṇi gantuṃ sadā // 2.66	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
gṛhī yatrāgataṃ dṛṣṭvā diśo vīkṣeta vāpy adhaḥ / tatra ye sadane yānti te śṛṅga-rahitā vṛṣāḥ // 2.67	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sābhyutthāna-kriyā yatra nālāpā madhurākṣarāḥ / guṇa-doṣa-kathā naiva tatra harmyaṃ na gamyate // 2.68	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
narakāya matis te cet paurohityaṃ samācāra / varṣaṃ yāvat kim anyena maṭha-cintāṃ dina-trayam // 2.69	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
ūṣmāpi vittajo vṛddhiṃ tejo nayati dehinām / kiṃ punas tasya sambhogas tyāga-dharma-samanvitaḥ // 2.70	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- nākasmāc chāṇḍilī mātar vikrīṇāti tilais tilān / luñcitān itarair yena hetur atra bhaviṣyati // 2.71	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
grāsād api tad ardhaṃ ca kasmān no dīyate'rthiṣu / icchānurūpo vibhavaḥ kadā kasya bhaviṣyati // 2.72	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: bha-vipulā)
īśvarā bhūri-dānena yal labhante phalaṃ kila / daridras tac ca kākiṇyā prāpnuyād iti na śrutiḥ // 2.73	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dātā laghur api sevyo bhavati na kṛpaṇo mahān api samṛddhyā / kūpo 'ntaḥ-svādu-jalaḥ prītyai lokasya na samudraḥ // 2.74	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- akṛta-tyāga-mahimnāṃ mithyā kiṃ rāja-rāja-śabdena / goptāraṃ na nidhīnāṃ mahayanti maheśvaraṃ vibudhāḥ // 2.75	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
api ca- sadā dāna-parikṣīṇaḥ śasta eva karīśvaraḥ / adānaḥ pīna-gātro 'pi nindya eva hi gardabhaḥ // 2.76	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
suśīlo 'pi suvṛtto 'pi yāty adānād adho ghaṭaḥ / punaḥ kubjāpi kāṇāpi dānād upari karkaṭī // 2.77	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yacchan jalam api jalado vallabhatām eti sakala-lokasya / nityaṃ prasārita-karo mitro 'pi na vīkṣituṃ śakyaḥ // 2.78	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
sat-pātraṃ mahatī śraddhā deśe kāle yathocite / yad dīyate viveka-jñais tad anantāya kalpate // 2.79	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- atitṛṣṇā na kartavyā tṛṣṇāṃ naiva parityajet / atitṛṣṇābhibhūtasya śikhā bhavati mastake // 2.80	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
akṛte'py udyame puṃsām anya-janma-kṛtaṃ phalam / śubhāśubhaṃ samabhyeti vidhinā saṃniyojitam // 2.81	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yasmin deśe ca kāle ca vayasā yādṛśena ca / kṛtaṃ śubhāśubhaṃ karma tat tathā tena bhujyate // 2.82	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
śanaiḥ śanaiś ca bhoktavyaṃ svayaṃ vittam upārjitam / rasāyanam iva prājñair helayā na kadācana // 2.83	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
āyuḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca vidyā nidhanam eva ca / pañcaitāni hi sṛjyante garbhasthasyaiva dehinaḥ // 2.84	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sakṛd api dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ vibudhā jānanti sāratāṃ tasya / hasta-tulayāpi nipuṇāḥ pala-pramāṇā vijānanti // 2.85	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
vāñchaiva sūcayati pūrvataraṃ bhaviṣyaṃ puṃsāṃ yad anya-tanujaṃ tv aśubhaṃ śubhaṃ vā / vijñāyate śiśur ajāta-kalāpa-cihnaḥ pratyudgatair apasaran saralaḥ kalāpī // 2.86	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
chittvā pāśam apāsya kūṭa-racanāṃ bhaṅktvā balād vāgurāṃ paryantāgni-śikhā-kalāpa-jaṭilān nirgatya dūraṃ vanāt / vyādhānāṃ śara-gocarād api javenotpatya dhāvan mṛgaḥ kūpāntaḥ-patitaḥ karotu vidhure kiṃ vā vidhau pauruṣam // 2.87	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
yad utsāhī sadā martyaḥ parābhavati yaj janān / yad uddhataṃ vaded vākyaṃ tat sarvaṃ vittajaṃ balam // 2.88	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthena balavān sarvo 'py artha-yuktaḥ sa paṇḍitaḥ / paśyainaṃ mūṣakaṃ vyarthaṃ sajāteḥ samatāṃ matam // 2.89	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
daṃṣṭrā-virahitaḥ sarpo mada-hīno yathā gajaḥ / tathārthena vihīno 'tra puruṣo nāma-dhārakaḥ // 2.90	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthena ca vihīnasya puruṣasyālpa-medhasaḥ / vyucchidyante kriyāḥ sarvā grīṣme kusarito yathā // 2.91	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā kāka-yavāḥ proktā yathāraṇya-bhavās tilāḥ / nāma-mātrā na siddhau hi dhana-hīnās tathā narāḥ // 2.92	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
santo 'pi na hi rājante daridrasyetare guṇāḥ / āditya iva bhūtānāṃ śrīr guṇānāṃ prakāśinī // 2.93	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na tathā bādhyate loke prakṛtyā nirdhano janaḥ / yathā dravyāṇi samprāpya tair vihīno 'sukhe sthitaḥ // 2.94	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śuṣkasya kīṭa-khātasya vahni-dagdhasya sarvataḥ / taror apy ūṣarasthasya varaṃ janma na cārthinaḥ // 2.95	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śaṅkanīyā hi sarvatra niṣpratāpā daridratā / upakartum api hi prāptaṃ niḥsvaṃ santyajya gacchati // 2.96	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
unnamyonnamya tatraiva daridrāṇāṃ manorathāḥ / patanti hṛdaye vyarthā vidhavāstrīstanā iva // 2.97	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vyakte'pi vāsare nityaṃ daurgatya-tamasāvṛtaḥ / agrato 'pi sthito yatnān na kenāpīha dṛśyate // 2.98	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yat-sakāśān na lābhāḥ syāt kevalāḥ syur vipattayaḥ / sa svāmī dūratas tyājyo viśeṣād anujīvibhiḥ // 2.99	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mṛto daridraḥ puruṣo mṛtaṃ maithunam aprajam / mṛtam aśrotriyaṃ śrāddhaṃ mṛto yajñas tv adakṣiṇam // 2.100	anuṣṭubh (1,2: bha-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
vyathayanti paraṃ ceto manoratha-śatair janāḥ / nānuṣṭhānair dhanair hīnāḥ kulajāḥ vidhavā iva // 2.101	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
daurgatyaṃ dehināṃ duḥkham apamāna-karaṃ param / yena svair api manyante jīvanto 'pi mṛtā iva // 2.102	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dainyasya pātratām eti parābhṛteḥ paraṃ padam / vipadām āśrayaḥ śaśvad daurgatya-kaluṣī-kṛtaḥ // 2.103	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
lajjante bāndhavās tena sambandhaṃ gopayanti ca / mitrāṇy amitratāṃ yānti yasya na syuḥ kapardakāḥ // 2.104	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mūrtaṃ lāghavam evaitad apāyānām idaṃ gṛham / paryāyo maraṇasyāyaṃ nirdhanatvaṃ śarīriṇām // 2.105	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ajā-dhūlir iva trastair mārjanī-reṇuvaj janaiḥ / dīpa-khaṭvottha-cchāyeva tyajyate nirdhano janaḥ // 2.106	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
śaucāvaśiṣṭayāpy asti kiñcit kāryaṃ kvacin mṛdā / nirdhanena janenaiva na tu kiñcit prayojanam // 2.107	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
adhano dātu-kāmo 'pi samprāpto dhanināṃ gṛham / manyate yācako 'yaṃ dhig dāridryaṃ khalu dehinām // 2.108	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sva-vitta-haraṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā yo hi rakṣaty asūn naraḥ / pitaro 'pi na gṛhṇanti tad-dattaṃ saliāñjalim // 2.109	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- gavārthe brāhmaṇārthe ca strī-vitta-haraṇe tathā / prāṇāṃs tyajati yo yuddhe tasya lokāḥ sanātanāḥ // 2.110	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
prāptavyam arthaṃ labhate manuṣyo devo 'pi taṃ laṅghayituṃ na śaktaḥ / tasmān na śocāmi na vismayo me yad asmadīyaṃ na hi tat pareṣām // 2.111	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
prāptavyam arthaṃ labhate manuṣyo devo 'pi taṃ laṅghayituṃ na śaktaḥ / tasmān na śocāmi na vismayo me yad asmadīyaṃ na hi tat pareṣām // 2.111	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
guroḥ sutāṃ mitra-bhāryāṃ svāmi-sevaka-gehinīm / yo gacchati pumāṃl loke tam āhur brahma-ghātinam // 2.112	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ra-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
aparaṃ ca- ayaśaḥ prāpyate yena yena cādho-gatir bhavet / svārthāc ca bhraśyate yena tat karma na samācaret // 2.113	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
vikāraṃ yāti no cittaṃ vitte yasya kadācana / mitraṃ syāt sarva-kāle ca kārayen mitram uttamam // 2.114	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vidvadbhiḥ suhṛdām atra cihnair etair asaṃśayam / parīkṣā-karaṇaṃ proktaṃ homāgner iva paṇḍitaiḥ // 2.115	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- āpat-kāle tu samprāpte yan mitraṃ mitram eva tat / vṛddhi-kāle tu samprāpte durjano 'pi suhṛd bhavet // 2.116	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mitraṃ ko 'pi na kasyāpi nitāntaṃ na ca vaira-kṛt / dṛśyate mitra-vidhvastāt kāryād vairī parīkṣitaḥ // 2.117	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
abhrac-chāyā khala-prītiḥ samudrānte ca medinī / alpenaiva vinaśyanti yauvanāni dhanāni ca // 2.118	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
susañcitair jīvanavat surakṣitair nije'pi dehe na viyojitaiḥ kvacit / puṃso yamāntaṃ vrajato 'pi niṣṭhurair etair dhanaiḥ pañcapadī na dīyate // 2.119	upajāti jagatī: indravaṃśā [12: ttjr], vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] atha vā vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
anyac ca- yathāmiṣaṃ jale matsyair bhakṣyate śvāpadair bhuvi / ākāśe pakṣibhiś caiva tathā sarvatra vittavān // 2.120	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
nirdoṣam api vittāḍhya doṣair yojayate nṛpaḥ / nidhanaḥ prāpta-doṣo 'pi sarvatra nirupadravaḥ // 2.121	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthānām arjanaṃ kāryaṃ vardhanaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ tathā / bhakṣyamāṇo nirādāyaḥ sumerurapi hīyate // 2.122	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arthārthī yāni kaṣṭāni mūḍho 'yaṃ sahate janaḥ / śatāṃśenāpi mokṣārthī tāni cen mokṣam āpnuyāt // 2.123	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ko dhīrasya manasvinaḥ sva-viṣayaḥ ko vā videśaḥ smṛto yaṃ deśaṃ śrayate tam eva kurute bāhu-pratāpārjitam / yad daṃṣṭrānakhalāṅgula-praharaṇaiḥ siṃho vanaṃ gāhate tasmin eva hata-dvipendra-rudhirais tṛṣṇāṃ chinatty ātmanaḥ // 2.124	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
ko 'tibhāraḥ samarthānāṃ kiṃ dūraṃ vyavasāyinām / ko videśaḥ suvdyānāṃ kaḥ paraḥ priya-vādinām // 2.125	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
utsāha-sampannam adīrgha-sūtraṃ kriyā-vidhijñaṃ vyasaneṣv asaktam / śūraṃ kṛtajñaṃ dṛḍha-sauhṛdaṃ ca- lakṣmīḥ svayaṃ vāñchati vāsa-hetoḥ // 2.126	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
arthasyopārjanaṃ kṛtvā naivābhāgyaḥ samaśnute / araṇyaṃ mahadāsādya mūḍhaḥ somilako yathā // 2.127	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
utpatanti yad ākāśe nipatanti mahītale / pakṣiṇāṃ tad api prāptyā nādattam upatiṣṭhati // 2.128	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na hi bhavati yan na bhāvyaṃ bhavati ca bhāvyaṃ vināpi yatnena / kara-tala-gatam api naśyati yasya tu bhavitavyatā nāsti // 2.129	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
yathā dhenu-sahasreṣu vatso vindati mātaraṃ / tathā pūrva-kṛtaṃ karma kartāram anugacchati // 2.130	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śete saha śayānena gacchantam anugacchati / narāṇāṃ prāktanaṃ karma tiṣṭhati tu sahātmanā // 2.131	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
yathā chāyā-tapau nityaṃ susambaddhau parasparaṃ / evaṃ karma ca kartā ca saṃśliṣṭāv itaretaram // 2.132	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathaikena na hastena tālikā saṃprapadyate / tathodyama-parityaktaṃ na phalaṃ karmaṇaḥ smṛtam // 2.133	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
paśya karma-vaśāt prāptaṃ bhojyakāle'pi bhojanam / hastodyamaṃ vinā vaktre praviśen na kathañcana // 2.134	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
udyoginaṃ puruṣa-siṃham upaiti lakṣmīr daivena deyam iti kāpuruṣā vadanti / daivaṃ nihatya kuru pauruṣam ātma-śaktyā yatne kṛte yadi na sidhyati ko 'tra doṣaḥ // 2.135	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
tathā ca- udyamena hi sidhyanti kāryāṇi na manorathaiḥ / na hi suptasya siṃhasya viśanti vadane mṛgāḥ // 2.136	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
udyamena vinā rājan na sidhyanti manorathāḥ / kātarā iti jalpanti yad bhāvyaṃ tad bhaviṣyati // 2.137	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sva-śaktyā kurvataḥ karma na cet siddhiṃ prayacchati / nopālabhyaḥ pumāṃs tatra daivāntarita-pauruṣaḥ // 2.138	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sa āha-bhoḥ ! kiṃ kariṣyasi bhoga-rahitena dhanena yatas tava bhojanācchādanābhyadhikā prāptir api nāsti ? uktaṃ ca- kiṃ tayā kriyate lakṣmyā yā vadhūr iva kevalā / yā na veśyeva sāmānyā pathikair upabhujyate // 2.139	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
kṛpaṇo 'py akulīno 'pi sadā saṃśrita-mānuṣaiḥ / sevyate sa naro loke yasya syād vitta-sañcayaḥ // 2.140	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- śithilau ca subaddhau ca patataḥ patato na vā / nirīkṣitau mayā bhadre daśa varṣāṇi pañca ca // 2.141	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yo dhruvāṇi parityajyādhruvāṇi niṣevate / dhruvāṇi tasya naśyanti adhruvaṃ naṣṭam eva ca // 2.142	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
supūrā syāt kunadikā supūro mūṣikāñjaliḥ / susantuṣṭaḥ kāpuruṣaḥ svalpakenāpi tuṣyati // 2.143	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: bha-vipulā (ma-gaṇa-pūrvikā!))
yatrotsāha-samārambho yatrālasya-vinigrahaḥ / naya-vikrama-saṃyogas tatra śrīr acalā dhruvaṃ // 2.144	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tad daivam iti sañcintya tyajen nodyogam ātmanaḥ / anuyogaṃ vinā tailaṃ tilānāṃ nopajāyate // 2.145	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- yaḥ stokenāpi santoṣaṃ kurute mandadhīr janaḥ / tasya bhāgya-vihīnasya dattā śrīr api mārjyate // 2.146	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛta-niścayino vandyās tuṅgimā nopabhujyate / cātakaḥ ko varāko 'yaṃ yasyendro vārivāhakaḥ // 2.147	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāvat syāt sarva-kṛtyeṣu puruṣo 'tra svayaṃ prabhuḥ / strī-vākyāṅkuśa-vikṣuṇṇo yāvan no dhriyate balāt // 2.148	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
akṛtyaṃ manyate kṛtyaṃ agamyaṃ manyate sugam / abhakṣyaṃ manyate bhakṣyaṃ strī-vākya-prerito naraḥ // 2.149	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
agnihotra-phalā vedāḥ śīla-vṛtta-phalaṃ śrutam / rati-putra-phalā dārā datta-bhukta-phalaṃ dhanam // 2.150	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gṛha-madhya-nikhātena dhanena dhanino yadi / bhavāmaḥ kiṃ na tenaiva dhanena dhanino vayaṃ // 2.151	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
upārjitānām arthānāṃ tyāga eva hi rakṣaṇam / taḍāgodara-saṃsthānāṃ parīvāha ivāmbhasām // 2.152	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- upārjitānām arthānāṃ tyāga eva hi rakṣaṇam / taḍāgodara-saṃsthānāṃ parivāha ivāmbhasām // 2.153	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- dānaṃ bhogo nāśas tisro gatayo bhavanti vittasya / yo na dadāti na bhuṅkte tasya tṛtīyā gatir bhavati // 2.154	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
dhanādikeṣu vidyante ye'tra mūrkhāḥ sukhāśayāḥ / tapta-grīṣmeṇa sevante śaityārthaṃ te hutāśanam // 2.155	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarpāḥ pibanti pavanaṃ na ca durbalās te śuṣkais tṛṇair vana-gajā balino bhavanti / kandaiḥ phalair muni-varā gamayanti kālaṃ santoṣa eva puruṣasya paraṃ nidhānam // 2.156	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
santoṣāmṛta-tṛptānāṃ yat sukhaṃ śānta-cetasām / kutas tad-dhana-lubdhānām itaś cetaś ca dhāvatām // 2.157	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pīyūṣam iva saṃtoṣaṃ pibatāṃ nirvṛtiḥ parā / duḥkhaṃ nirantaraṃ puṃsām asaṃtoṣavatāṃ punaḥ // 2.158	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nirodhāc cetaso 'kṣāṇi niruddhāny akhilāny api / ācchādite ravau meghaiḥ sañchannāḥ syur gabhastayaḥ // 2.159	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vāñchā-vicchedanaṃ prāhuḥ svāsthyaṃ śāntā maha-rṣayaḥ / vāñchā nivartate nārthaiḥ pipāsevāgni-sevanaiḥ // 2.160	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anindyam api nindanti stuvanty astutyam uccakaiḥ / svāpateya-kṛte martyāḥ kiṃ kiṃ nāma na kurvate // 2.161	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dharmārthaṃ yasya vittehā tasyāpi na śubhāvahā / prakṣālanādd hi paṅkasya dūrād asparśanaṃ varam // 2.162	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dānena tulyo nidhir asti nānyo lobhāc ca nānyo 'sti paraḥ pṛthivyām / vibhūṣaṇaṃ śīla-samaṃ na cānyat santoṣa-tulyaṃ dhanam asti nānyat // 2.163	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
dāridryasya parā mūrtir yan māna-draviṇālpatā / jarad-gava-dhanaḥ śarvas tathāpi parameśvaraḥ // 2.164	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sulabhāḥ puruṣā rājan satataṃ priya-vādinaḥ / apriyasya ca pathyasya vaktā śrotā ca durlabhaḥ // 2.166	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
apriyāṇy api pathyāni ye vadanti nṛṇām iha / ta eva suhṛdaḥ proktā anye syur nāma-dhārakāḥ // 2.167	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhaya-trasto naraḥ śvāsaṃ prabhūtaṃ kurute muhuḥ / diśo 'valokayaty eva na svāsthyaṃ vrajati kvacit // 2.168	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dvāv upāyāv iha proktau vimuktau śatru-darśane / hastayoś cālanād eko dvitīyaḥ pāda-vega-jaḥ // 2.169	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
subhāṣita-rasāsvāda-baddha-romāñca-kañcukaṃ / vināpi saṃgamaṃ strīṇāṃ kavīnāṃ sukham edhate // 2.170	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
subhāṣita-maya-dravya-saṅgrahaṃ na karoti yaḥ / sa tu prastāva-yajñeṣu kāṃ pradāsyati dakṣiṇām // 2.171	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- sakṛd uktaṃ na gṛhṇāti svayaṃ vā na karoti yaḥ / yasya saṃpuṭikā nāsti kutas tasya subhāṣitam // 2.172	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
sva-gṛhodyāna-gate'pi snigdhaiḥ pāpaṃ viśaṅkyate mohāt / kim u dṛṣṭa-bahv-apāya-pratibhaya-kāntāra-madhya-sthe // 2.173	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
api mandatvam āpanno naṣṭo vāpīṣṭa-darśanāt / prāyeṇa prāṇināṃ bhūyo duḥkhāvego 'dhiko bhavet // 2.174	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prāṇātyaye samutpanne yadi syān mitra-darśanaṃ / tad dvābhyāṃ sukha-daṃ paścāj jīvato 'pi mṛtasya ca // 2.175	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ajñānāj jñānato vāpi duruktaṃ yad udāhṛtam / mayā tat kṣamyatām adya dvābhyām api prasādataḥ // 2.176	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
sampadi yasya na harṣo vipadi viṣādo raṇe na bhīrutvaṃ / taṃ bhuvana-traya-tilakaṃ janayati jananī sutaṃ viralaṃ // 2.177	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
āpan-nāśāya vibudhaiḥ kartavyāḥ suhṛdo 'malāḥ / na taraty āpadaṃ kaścid yo 'tra mitra-vivarjitaḥ // 2.178	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛtānta-pāśa-baddhānāṃ daivopahata-cetasāṃ / buddhayaḥ kubja-gāminyo bhavanti mahatām api // 2.179	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vidhātrā racitā yā sā lalāṭe'kṣara-mālikā / na tāṃ mārjayituṃ śaktāḥ sva-śaktyāpy atipaṇḍitāḥ // 2.180	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dayita-jana-viprayogo vitta-viyogaś ca sahyāḥ syuḥ / yadi sumahauṣadha-kalpo vayasya-jana-saṃgamo na syāt // 2.181	upagīti (12, 15, 12, 15)
varaṃ prāṇa-parityāgo na viyogo bhavādṛśaiḥ / prāṇā janmāntare bhūyo na bhavanti bhavad-vidhāḥ // 2.182	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekasya duḥkhasya na yāvad antaṃ gacchāmy ahaṃ pāram ivārṇavasya / tāvad dvitīyaṃ samupasthitaṃ me chidreṣv anarthā bahulī-bhavanti // 2.183	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
tāvad askhalitaṃ yāvat sukhaṃ yāti same pathi / skhalite ca samutpanne viṣame ca pade pade // 2.184	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yan namraṃ saralaṃ cāpi yac cāpatsu na sīdati / dhanur mitraṃ kalatraṃ ca durlabhaṃ śuddha-vaṃśajam // 2.185	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na mātari na dāreṣu na sodarye na cātmaje / viśrambhas tādṛśaḥ puṃsāṃ yādṛṅ mitre nirantare // 2.186	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
asampattau paro lābho guhyasya kathanaṃ tathā / āpad-vimokṣaṇaṃ caiva mitrasyaitat phala-trayam // 2.187	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāyaḥ saṃnihitāpāyaḥ sampadaḥ padam āpadām / samāgamāḥ sāpagamāḥ sarvam utpādi bhaṅguram // 2.188	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: bha-vipulā)
kṣate prahārā nipatanty abhīkṣṇaṃ dhana-kṣaye vardhati jāṭharāgniḥ / āpatsu vairāṇi samudbhavanti cchidreṣv anarthā bahulī-bhavanti // 2.189	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
prāpte bhaye paritrāṇaṃ prīti-viśrambha-bhājanaṃ / kena ratnam idaṃ sṛṣṭaṃ mitram ity akṣara-dvayaṃ // 2.190	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vyasanaṃ prāpya yo mohāt kevalaṃ paridevayet / krandanaṃ vardhayaty eva tasyāntaṃ nādhigacchati // 2.191	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kevalaṃ vyasanasyoktaṃ bheṣajaṃ naya-paṇḍitaiḥ / tasyoccheda-samārambho viṣāda-parivarjanaṃ // 2.192	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atīta-lābhasya surakṣaṇārthaṃ bhaviṣya-lābhasya ca saṅgamārtham / āpat-prapannasya ca mokṣaṇārthaṃ yan mantryate'sau paramo hi mantraḥ // 2.193	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
siddhiṃ vā yadi vāsiddhiṃ cittotsāho nivedayet / prathamaṃ sarva-jantūnāṃ prājño vetti na cetaraḥ // 2.194	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
prāpto bandhanam apy ayaṃ guru-mṛgas tāvat tvayā me hṛtaḥ samprāptaḥ kamaṭhaḥ sa cāpi niyataṃ naṣṭas tavādeśataḥ / kṣut-kṣāmo 'tra vane bhramāmi śiśukais tyaktaḥ samaṃ bhāryayā yac cānyan na kṛtaṃ kṛtānta kurute tac cāpi sahyaṃ mayā // 2.195	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
yo mitrāṇi karoty atra na kauṭilyena vartate / taiḥ samaṃ na parābhūtiṃ samprāpnoti kathañcana // 2.196	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na viśvaset pūrva-virodhitasya śatroś ca mitratvam upāgatasya / dagdhāṃ guhāṃ paśya ulūka-pūrṇāṃ kāka-praṇītena hutāśanena // 3.1	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
ya upekṣeta śatruṃ svaṃ prasarantaṃ yadṛcchayā / rogaṃ cālasya-saṃyuktaḥ sa śanais tena hanyate // 3.2	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- jāta-mātraṃ na yaḥ śatruṃ vyādhiṃ ca praśamaṃ nayet / mahābalo 'pi tenaiva vṛddhiṃ prāpya sa hanyate // 3.3	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
apṛṣṭenāpi vaktavyaṃ sacivenātra kiṃcana / pṛṣṭena tu viśeṣeṇa vācyaṃ pathyaṃ mahīpateḥ // 3.4	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo na pṛṣṭo hitaṃ brūte pariṇāme sukhāvaham / mantro na priya-vaktā ca kevalaṃ sa ripuḥ smṛtam // 3.5	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmād ekāntam āsādya kāryo mantro mahīpate / yena tasya vayaṃ kurmo niyamaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā // 3.6	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ ca- balīyasi praṇamatāṃ kāle praharatām api / sampado nāvagacchanti pratīpam iva nimnagāḥ // 3.7	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
satyāḍhyo dhārmikaś cāryo bhrātṛ-saṅghātavān balī / aneka-vijayī caiva sandheyaḥ sa ripur bhavet // 3.8	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sandhiḥ kāryo 'py anāryeṇa vijñāya prāṇa-saṃśayam / prāṇaiḥ saṃrakṣitaiḥ sarvaṃ yato bhavati rakṣitam // 3.9	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aneka-yuddha-vijayī sandhānaṃ yasya gacchati / tat-prabhāveṇa tasyāśu vaśaṃ gacchanty arātayaḥ // 3.10	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
sandhim icchet samenāpi sandigdho vijayī yudhi / na hi sāṃśayikaṃ kuryād ity uvāca bṛhaspatiḥ // 3.11	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sandigdho vijayo yuddhe janānām iha yuddhyatām / upāya-tritayād ūrdhvaṃ tasmād yuddhaṃ samācaret // 3.12	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
asandadhāno mānāndhaḥ samenāpi hato bhṛśam / āmakumbham ivābhittvā nāvatiṣṭheta śaktimān // 3.13	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
samaṃ śaktimatā yuddham aśaktasya hi mṛtyave / vṛṣatkumbhaṃ yathā bhittvā tāvat tiṣṭhati śaktimān // 3.14	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- bhūmir mitraṃ hiraṇyaṃ vā vigrahasya phala-trayam / nāsty ekam api yady eṣāṃ vigrahaṃ na samācaret // 3.15	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
khanann ākhu-bilaṃ siṃhaḥ pāṣāṇa-śakalākulam / prāpnoti nakha-bhaṅgaṃ hi phalaṃ vā mūṣako bhavet // 3.16	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmān na syāt phalaṃ yatra puṣṭaṃ yuddhaṃ tu kevalam / na hi tat svayam utpādyaṃ kartavyaṃ na kathañcana // 3.17	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
balīyasā samākrānto vaitasīṃ vṛttim āśrayet / vāñchann abhraṃśinīṃ lakṣmīṃ na bhaujaṅgī kadācana // 3.18	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kurvan hi vaitasīṃ vṛttiṃ prāpnoti mahatīṃ śriyam / bhujaṅga-vṛttim āpanno vadham arhati kevalam // 3.19	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kaurmaṃ saṅkocam āsthāya prahārān api marṣayet / kāle kāle ca matimān uttiṣṭhet kṛṣṇa-sarpavat // 3.20	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
āgataṃ vigrahaṃ vidvān upāyaiḥ praśamaṃ nayet / vijayasya hy anityatvād rabhasena na sampatet // 3.21	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
balinā saha yoddhavyam iti nāsti nidarśanam / prativātaṃ na hi ghanaḥ kadācid upasarpati // 3.22	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
śatruṇā na hi sandadhyāt suśliṣṭenāpi sandhinā / sutaptam api pānīyaṃ śamayaty eva pāvakam // 3.23	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ ca- satya-dharma-vihīnena na sandadhyāt kathañcana / sugandhito 'py asādhutvād acirād yāti vikriyām // 3.24	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
krūro lubdho 'laso 'satyaḥ pramādī bhīrur asthiraḥ / mūḍho yodhāvamantā ca sukhocchedyo bhaved ripuḥ // 3.25	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
caturthopāya-sādhye tu ripau sāntvam apakriyā / svedyam āma-jvaraṃ prājñaḥ ko 'mbhasā pariṣiñcati // 3.26	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sāmavādāḥ sakopasya śatroḥ pratyuta dīpikāḥ / prataptasyeva sahasā sarpiṣas toya-bindavaḥ // 3.27	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
pramāṇābhyadhikasyāpi mahat-sattvam adhiṣṭhitaḥ / padaṃ mūrdhni samādhatte kesarī matta-dantinaḥ // 3.28	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
utsāha-śakti-sampanno hanyāc chatruṃ laghur gurum / yathā kaṇṭhīravo nāgaṃ bhāradvājaḥ pracakṣate // 3.29	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
māyayā śatravo vadhyā avadhyāḥ syur balena ye / yathā strī-rūpam āsthāya hato bhīmena kīcakaḥ // 3.30	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- mṛtyor ivogra-daṇḍasya rājño yānti vaśaṃ dviṣaḥ / sarvaṃsahaṃ tu manyante tṛṇāya ripavaś ca tam // 3.31	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na jātu śamanaṃ yasya tejas tejasvi-tejasām / vṛthā jātena kiṃ tena mātur yauvana-hāriṇā // 3.32	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yā lakṣmīr nānuliptāṅgī vair-śoṇita-kuṅkumaiḥ / kāntāpi manasaḥ prītiṃ na sā dhatte manasvinām // 3.33	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
ripu-raktena saṃsiktā tat-strī-netrāmbubhis tathā / na bhūmir yasya bhūpasya kā ślāghā tasya jīvite // 3.34	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
balotkaṭena duṣṭena maryādā-rahitena ca / na sandhi-vigrahau naiva vinā yānaṃ praśasyate // 3.35	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dvidhākāraṃ bhaved yānaṃ bhavet prāṇārtha-rakṣaṇam / ekam anyaj jigīṣoś ca yātrālakṣaṇam ucyate // 3.36	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kārttike vātha caitre vā vijigīṣoḥ praśasyate / yānam utkṛṣṭa-vīryasya śatru-deśe na cānyadā // 3.37	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
avaskanda-pradānasya sarve kālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ / vyasane vartamānasya śatrocchidrānvitasya ca // 3.38	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svasthānaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā śūraiś cātair mahābalaiḥ / para-deśaṃ tato gacchet praṇidhi-vyāptam agrataḥ // 3.39	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ajñātavī-vadhāsāra-toya-śasyo vrajet tu yaḥ / para-rāṣṭraṃ na bhūyaḥ sa sva-rāṣṭram adhigacchati // 3.40	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tan na yuktaṃ prabho kartuṃ dvitīyaṃ yānam eva ca / na vigraho na sandhānaṃ balinā tena pāpinā // 3.41	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yad apasarati meṣaḥ kāraṇaṃ tat prahartuṃ mṛga-patir api kopāt saṅkucaty utpatiṣṇuḥ / hṛdaya-nihita-bhāvā gūḍha-mantra-pracārāḥ kim api vigaṇayanto buddhimantaḥ sahante // 3.42	mālinī [15: nnmyy]
anyac ca- balavantaṃ ripuṃ dṛṣṭvā deśa-tyāgaṃ karoti yaḥ / yudhiṣṭhira ivāpnoti punar jīvan sa medinīm // 3.43	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yudhyate'haṅkṛtiṃ kṛtvā durbalo yo balīyasā / sa tasya vāñchitaṃ kuryād ātmanaś ca kula-kṣayam // 3.44	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nakraḥ sva-sthānam āsādya gajendram api karṣati / sa eva pracyutaḥ sthānāc chunāpi paribhūyate // 3.45	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā- abhiyukto balavatā tiṣṭhan durge prayatnavān / tatrasthaḥ suhṛdāhvānaṃ kurvītātma-vimuktaye // 3.46	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yo ripor āgamaṃ śrutvā bhaya-santrasta-mānasaḥ / sva-sthānaṃ hi tyajet tatra na tu bhūyo viśec ca saḥ // 3.47	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
daṃṣṭrā-virahitaḥ sarpo mada-hīno yathā gajaḥ / sthāna-hīnas tathā rājā gamyaḥ syāt sarva-jantuṣu // 3.48	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nija-sthāna-sthito 'py ekaḥ śataṃ yoddhuṃ sahen naraḥ / śaktānām api śatrūṇāṃ tasmāt sthānaṃ na santyajet // 3.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmād durgaṃ dṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā subhaṭāsāra-saṃyutam / prākāra-parikhā-yuktaṃ śastrādibhir alaṅkṛtam // 3.50	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tiṣṭhen madhya-gato nityaṃ yuddhāya kṛta-niścayaḥ / jīvan samprāptsyati rājyaṃ mṛto vā svargam eṣyati // 3.51	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
anyac ca- balināpi na bādhyante laghavo 'py eka-saṃśrayāḥ / vipakṣeṇāpi marutā yathaika-sthāna-vīrudhāḥ // 3.52	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: na-vipulā)
mahān apy ekajo vṛkṣaḥ balavān supratiṣṭhitaḥ / prasahya iva vātena śakyo dharṣayituṃ yataḥ // 3.53	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atha ye saṃhatā vṛkṣā sarvataḥ supratiṣṭhitāḥ / te na raudrānilenāpi hanyante hy eka-saṃśrayāt // 3.54	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evaṃ manuṣyam apy ekaṃ śauryeṇāpi samanvitam / śakyaṃ dviṣanto manyante hiṃsanti ca tataḥ param // 3.55	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
asahāyaḥ samartho 'pi tejasvī kiṃ kariṣyati / nirvāte jvalito vahniḥ svayam eva praśāmyati // 3.56	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
saṅgatiḥ śreyasī puṃsāṃ sva-pakṣe ca viśeṣataḥ / tuṣair api paribhraṣṭā na prarohanti taṇḍulāḥ // 3.57	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vanāni dahato vahneḥ sakhī bhavati mārutaḥ / sa eva dīpa-nāśāya kṛśe kasyāsti sauhṛdam // 3.58	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
saṅghātavān yathā veṇur niviḍair veṇubhir vṛtaḥ / na śakyeta samucchettuṃ durbalo 'pi yathā nṛpaḥ // 3.59	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mahājanasya samparkaḥ kasya nonnati-kārakaḥ / padma-patra-sthitaṃ toyaṃ dhatte muktā-phala-śriyam // 3.60	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aviśvāsaṃ sadā tiṣṭhet sandhinā vigraheṇa ca / dvaidhī-bhāvaṃ samāśritya pāpe śatrau balīyasi // 3.61	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ucchedyam api vidvāṃso vardhayanty arim ekadā / guḍena vardhitaḥ śleṣmā yato niḥśeṣatāṃ vrajet // 3.62	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- strīṇāṃ śatroḥ kumitrasya paṇya-strīṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ / yo bhaved eka-bhāvo 'tra na sa jīvati mānavaḥ // 3.63	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛtyaṃ deva-dvijātīnām ātmanaś ca guros tathā / eka-bhāvena kartavyaṃ śeṣaṃ dvaidha-samāśritam // 3.64	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
eko bhāvaḥ sadā śasto yatīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām / śrī-lubdhānāṃ na lokānāṃ viśeṣeṇa mahī-bhujām // 3.65	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gāvo gandhena paśyanti vedaiḥ paśyanti vai dvijāḥ / cārai paśyanti rājānaś cakṣurbhyām itare janāḥ // 3.66	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ cātra viṣaye- yas tīrthāni nije pakṣe para-pakṣe viśeṣataḥ / guptaiś cārair nṛpo vetti na sa durgatim āpnuyāt // 3.67	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kaccid aṣṭadaśāny eṣu sva-pakṣe daśa pañca ca / tribhis tribhir avijñātair vetsi tīrthāni cārakaiḥ // 3.68	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vaidya-sāṃvatsarācāryāḥ sva-pakṣe'dhikṛtāś carāḥ / tathāhi-tuṇḍikonmattāḥ sarvaṃ jānanti śatruṣu // 3.69	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- kṛtvā kṛtya-vidas tīrtheṣv antaḥ praṇidhayaḥ padam / vidāṅkurvantu mahatas talaṃ vidviṣad-ambhasaḥ // 3.70	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: na-vipulā)
yo na rakṣati vitrastān pīḍyamānān paraiḥ sadā / jantūn pārthiva-rūpeṇa sa kṛtānto na saṃśayaḥ // 3.71	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yadi na syān narapatiḥ samyaṅ netāḥ tataḥ prajāḥ / akarṇadhārā jaladhau viplaveteha naur iva // 3.72	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: bha-vipulā)
ṣaḍ imān puruṣo jahyād bhinnāṃ nāvam ivārṇave / apravaktāram ācāryam anadhīyānam ṛtvijam // 3.73	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
arakṣitāraṃ rājānaṃ bhāryāṃ cāpirya-vādinīm / grāma-kāmaṃ ca gopālaṃ vana-kāmaṃ ca nāpitam // 3.74	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
narāṇāṃ nāpito dhūrtaḥ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva vāyasaḥ / daṃṣṭriṇāṃ ca śṛgālas tu śvebhikṣus tapasvinām // 3.75	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
bahudhā bahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ cintitāḥ sunirūpitāḥ / kathañcin na vilīyante vidvadbhiś cintitā nayāḥ // 3.76	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vakra-nāsaṃ sujihmākṣaṃ krūram apriya-darśanam / akruddhasyedṛśaṃ vaktraṃ bhavet kruddhasya kīdṛśam // 3.77	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svabhāva-raudram atyugraṃ krūram apriya-vādinam / ulūkaṃ nṛpatiṃ kṛtvā kā naḥ siddhir bhaviṣyati // 3.78	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
eka eva hitārthāya tejasvī pārthivo bhuvaḥ / yugānta iva bhāsvanto bahavo 'tra vipattaye // 3.79	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gurūṇāṃ nāma-mātre'pi gṛhīte svāmi-sambhave / duṣṭānāṃ purataḥ kṣemaṃ tat-kṣaṇād eva jāyate // 3.80	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- vyapadeśena mahatāṃ siddiḥ sañjāyate parā / śaśino vyapadeśena vasanti śaśakāḥ sukham // 3.81	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
spṛśann api gajo hanti jighrann api bhujaṅgamaḥ / hasann api nṛpo hanti mānayann api durjanaḥ // 3.82	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tyajed ekaṃ kulasyārthe grāmasyārthe kulaṃ tyajet / grāmaṃ janapadasyārthe ātmārthe pṛthivīṃ tyajet // 3.83	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṣemyāṃ śasya-pradāṃ nityaṃ paśu-vṛddhi-karīm api / parityajen nṛpo bhūmim ātmārtham avicārayan // 3.84	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
āpad-arthe dhanaṃ rakṣed dārān rakṣed dhanair api / ātmānaṃ satataṃ rakṣed dārair api dhanair api // 3.85	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nirviṣeṇāpi sarpeṇa kartavyā mahatī phaṭā / viṣaṃ bhavatu mā vāstu phaṭāṭopo bhayaṅkaraḥ // 3.86	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sākāro niḥspṛho vāgmī nānā-śāstra-vicakṣaṇaḥ / para-cittāvagantā ca rājño dūtaḥ sa iṣyate // 3.87	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- yo mūrkhaṃ laulya-sampannaṃ rāja-dvārikam ācaret / mithyā-vādaṃ viśeṣeṇa tasya kāryaṃ na sidhyati // 3.88	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
udyateṣv api śastreṣu bandhu-varga-vadheṣv api / puruṣāṇy api jalpanto vadhyā dūtā na bhūbhujā // 3.89	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṣudram alasaṃ kāpuruṣaṃ vyasaninam akṛtajñaṃ jīvita-kāmaḥ / pṛṣṭha-pralapana-śīlaṃ svāmitve nābhiyojayet // 3.90	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
tathā ca- kṣudram arthapatiṃ prāpya nyāyānveṣaṇa-tat-parau / ubhāv api kṣayaṃ prāptau purā śaśaka-piñjalau // 3.91	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na tādṛg jāyate saukhyam api svarge śarīriṇām / dāridrye'pi hi yādṛk syāt sva-deśe sva-pure gṛhe // 3.92	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vāpī-kūpa-taḍāgānāṃ devālaya-kujanmanām / utsargāt parataḥ svāmyam api kartuṃ na śakyate // 3.93	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- pratyakṣaṃ yasya yad bhuktaṃ kṣetrādyaṃ daśa vatsarān / tatra bhuktiḥ pramāṇaṃ syād na sākṣī nākṣarāṇi vā // 3.94	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mānuṣāṇām ayaṃ nyāyo munibhiḥ parikīrtitaḥ / tiraścāṃ ca vihaṅgānāṃ yāvad eva samāśrayaḥ // 3.95	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anityāni śarīrāṇi vibhavo naiva śāśvataḥ / nityaṃ saṃnihito mṛtyuḥ kartavyo dharma-saṃgrahaḥ // 3.96	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya dharma-vihīnāni dināny āyānti yānti ca / sa lohakāra-bhastreva śvasann api na jīvati // 3.97	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nācchādayati kaupīnaṃ na daṃśa-maśakāpaham / śunaḥ-puccham iva vyarthaṃ pāṇḍityaṃ dharma-varjitam // 3.98	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- pulākā iva dhānyeṣu pūtikā iv pakṣiṣu / maśakā iva martyeṣu yeṣāṃ dharmo na kāraṇam // 3.99	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
śreyaḥ puṣpa-phalaṃ vṛkṣād dadhnaḥ śreyo ghṛtaṃ smṛtam / śreyas tailaṃ ca puṇyākāc chreyān dharmas tu mānuṣāt // 3.100	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sṛṣṭā mūtra-purīṣārtham āhārāya ca kevalam / dharma-hīnāḥ parārthāya puruṣāḥ paśavo yathā // 3.101	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sthairyaṃ sarveṣu kṛtyeṣu śaṃsanti naya-paṇḍitāḥ / bahv-antarāya-yuktasya dharmasya tvaritā gatiḥ // 3.102	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
saṅkṣepāt kathyate dharmo janāḥ kiṃ vistareṇa vaḥ / paropakāraḥ puṇyāya pāpāya para-pīḍanam // 3.103	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
śrūyatāṃ dharma-sarvasvaṃ śrutvā caivāvadhāryatām / ātmanaḥ pratikūlāni pareṣāṃ na samācaret // 3.104	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ahiṃsā-pūrvako dharmo yasmāt sarva-hite rataḥ / yūkā-mat-kuṇa-daṃśādīṃs tasmāt tān api rakṣayet // 3.105	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hiṃsakāny api bhūtāni yo hiṃsati sa nirghṛṇaḥ / sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ kiṃ punar yaḥ śubhāni ca // 3.106	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vṛkṣāṃś chittvā paśūn hatvā kṛtvā rudhira-kardamam / yady evaṃ gamyate svargaṃ narakaṃ kena gamyate // 3.107	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mānād vā yadi vā lobhāt krodhād vā yadi vā bhayāt / yo nyāyam anyathā brūte sa yāti narakaṃ naraḥ // 3.108	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pañca paśv-anṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte / śataṃ kanyānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte // 3.109	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
upaviṣṭaḥ sabhā-madhye yo na vakti sphuṭaṃ vacaḥ / tasmād dūreṇa sa tyājyo na yo vā kīrtayed ṛtam // 3.110	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rohate sāyakair viddhaṃ chinnaṃ rohati cāsinā / vaco duruktaṃ bībhatsaṃ na prarohati vāk-kṣatam // 3.111	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
adeśa-kālajñam anāyati-kṣamaṃ yad apriyaṃ lāghava-kāri cātmanaḥ / yo 'trābravīt kāraṇa-varjitaṃ vaco na tad vacaḥ syād viṣam eva tad bhavet // 3.112	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
balopapanno 'pi hi buddhimān naraḥ pare nayen na svayam eva vairitām / bhiṣaṅ mamāstīti vicintya bhakṣayed akāraṇāt ko hi vicakṣaṇo viṣam // 3.113	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
parivādaḥ pariṣadi na kathañcit paṇḍitena vaktavyaḥ / satyam api tan na vācyaṃ yad uktam asukhāvahaṃ bhavati // 3.114	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
suhṛdbhir āptair asakṛd-vicāritaṃ svayaṃ hi buddhyā pravicāritāśrayam / karoti kāryaṃ khalu yaḥ sa buddhimān sa eva lakṣmyā yaśasāṃ ca bhājanam // 3.115	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
bahu-buddhi-samāyuktāḥ suvijñānā balotkaṭān / śaktā vañcayituṃ dhūrtā brāhmaṇaṃ chāgalad iva // 3.116	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
śvāna-kukkuṭa-cāṇḍālāḥ sama-sparśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ / rāsabhoṣṭrau viśeṣeṇa tasmāt tān naiva saṃspṛśet // 3.117	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tiryañcaṃ mānuṣaṃ vāpi yo mṛtaṃ saṃspṛśet kudhīḥ / pañca-gavyena śuddhiḥ syāt tasya cāndrāyaṇena vā // 3.118	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yaḥ spṛśed rāsabhaṃ martyo jñānād ajñānato 'pi vā / sa-cailaṃ snānam uddiṣṭaṃ tasya pāpa-praśāntaye // 3.119	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
abhinava-sevaka-vinayaiḥ prāghuṇakoktair vilāsinīr uditaiḥ / dhūrta-jana-vacana-nikarair iha kaścid avañcito nāsti // 3.120	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
bahavo na viroddhavyā durjayā hi mahājanāḥ / sphurantam api nāgendraṃ bhakṣayanti pipīlikāḥ // 3.121	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
apasāra-samāyuktaṃ na yajñair durgam ucyate / apasāra-parityaktaṃ durga-vyājena bandhanam // 3.122	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
api prāṇa-samān iṣṭān pālitān lālitān api / bhṛtyān yuddhe samutpanne paśyec chuṣkam ivendhanam // 3.123	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- prāṇavad rakṣayed bhṛtyān svakāyam iva poṣayet / sadaika-divasasyārthe yatra syād ripu-saṅgamaḥ // 3.124	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
śatroḥ pracalane chidram ekam anyaṃ ca saṃśrayam / kurvāṇo jāyate vaśyo vyagratve rāja-sevinām // 3.125	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vṛttim apy āśritaḥ śatrur avadhyaḥ syāj jigīṣuṇā / kiṃ punaḥ saṃśrito durgaṃ sāmagryā parayā yutam // 3.126	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anārambho hi kāryāṇāṃ prathamaṃ buddhi-lakṣaṇam / ārabdhasyānta-gamanaṃ dvitīyaṃ buddhi-lakṣaṇam // 3.127	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
balīyasā hīna-balo virodhaṃ na bhūti-kāmo manasāpi vāñchet / na vadhyate vetasa-vṛttir atra vyaktaṃ praṇāśo 'sti pataṅga-vṛtteḥ // 3.128	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
balavantaṃ ripuṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvasvam api buddhimān / dattvā hi rakṣayet prāṇān rakṣitais tair dhanaṃ punaḥ // 3.129	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hīnaḥ śatrur nihantavyo yāvan na balavān bhavet / prāpta-sva-pauruṣa-balaḥ paścād bhavati durjayaḥ // 3.130	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
kālo hi sakṛd abhyeti yan naraṃ kāla-kāṅkṣiṇam / durlabhaḥ sa punas tena kāla-karmācikīrṣatā // 3.131	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kaścit kṣudra-samācāraḥ prāṇināṃ kāla-sannibhaḥ / vicacāra mahāraṇye ghoraḥ śuni-lubdhakaḥ // 3.132	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
bhūtān yo nānugṛhṇāti hy ātmanaḥ śaraṇāgatān / bhūtārthās tasya naśyanti haṃsāḥ padma-vane yathā // 3.133	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śrūyate hi kapotena śatruḥ śaraṇam āgataḥ / pūjitaś ca yathā-nyāyaṃ svaiś ca māṃsair nimantritaḥ // 3.134	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kaścid kṣudra-samācāraḥ prāṇināṃ kāla-sannibhaḥ / vicacāra mahāraṇye ghoraḥ śakuni-lubdhakaḥ // 3.135	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
naiva kaścit suhṛt tasya na sambandhī na bāndhavaḥ / sa taiḥ sarvaiḥ parityaktas tena raudreṇa karmaṇā // 3.136	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
athavā- ye nṛśaṃsā durātmanaḥ prāṇināṃ prāṇa-nāśakāḥ / udvejanīyā bhūtānāṃ vyālā iva bhavanti te // 3.137	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
sa pañjarakam ādāya pāśaṃ ca laguḍaṃ tathā / nityam eva vanaṃ yāti sarva-prāṇi-vihiṃsakaḥ // 3.138	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyedyur bhramatas tasya vane kāpi kapotikā / jātā hasta-gatā tāṃ sa prākṣipat pañjcarāntare // 3.139	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atha kṛṣṇā diśaḥ sarvā vanasthasyābhavan ghanaiḥ vāta-vṛṣṭiś ca mahato kṣaya-kāla ivābhavat // 3.140	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
tataḥ sa trasta-hṛdayaḥ kampamāno muhur muhuḥ / anveṣayan paritrāṇam āsasāda vanaspatim // 3.141	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
muhūrtaṃ paśyate yāvad viyad vimala-tārakam / prāpya vṛkṣaṃ vadaty evaṃ yo 'tra tiṣṭhati kaścana // 3.142	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasyāhaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāptaḥ sa paritrātu mām iti / śītena bhidyamānaṃ ca kṣudhayā gata-cetanam // 3.143	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atha tasya taroḥ skandhe kapotaḥ suciroṣitaḥ / bhāryā-virahitas tiṣṭhan vilalāpa suduḥkhitaḥ // 3.144	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vāta-varṣo mahān āsīn na cāgacchati me priyā / tayā virahitaṃ hy etac chūnyam adya gṛhaṃ mama // 3.145	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pativratā pati-prāṇā patyuḥ priya-hite ratā / yasya syād īdṛśī bhāryā dhanyaḥ sa puruṣo bhuvi // 3.146	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na gṛhaṃ gṛham ity āhur gṛhiṇī gṛham ucyate / gṛhaṃ tu gṛhiṇī-hīnam araṇya-sadṛśaṃ matam // 3.147	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pañjara-sthā tataḥ śrutvā bhartur duḥkhānvitaṃ vacaḥ / kapotikā susantuṣṭā vākyaṃ cedam athāha sā // 3.148	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na sā strīty abhimantavyā yasyāṃ bhartā na tuṣyati / tuṣṭe bhartari nārīṇāṃ tuṣṭāḥ syuḥ sarva-devatāḥ // 3.149	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dāvāgninā vidagdheva sa-puṣpa-stavakā latā / bhasmībhavatu sā nārī yasyāṃ bhartā na tuṣyati // 3.150	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mitaṃ dadāti hi pitā mitaṃ bhrātā mitaṃ sutaḥ / amitasya hi dātāraṃ bhartāraṃ kā na pūjayet // 3.151	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
punaś cābravīt- śṛṇuṣvāvahitaḥ kānta yat te vakṣyāmy ahaṃ hitam / prāṇair api tvayā nityaṃ saṃrakṣyaḥ śaraṇāgataḥ // 3.152	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
eṣa śākunikaḥ śete tavāvāsaṃ samāśritaḥ / śītārtaś ca kṣudhārtaś ca pūjām asmai samācara // 3.153	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śrūyate ca- yaḥ sāyam atithiṃ prāptaṃ yathā-śakti na pūjayet / tasyāsau duṣkṛtaṃ dattvā sukṛtaṃ cāpakarṣati // 3.154	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mā cāsmai tvaṃ kṛthā dvaiṣaṃ baddhāneneti mat-priyā / sva-kṛtair eva baddhāhaṃ prāktanaiḥ karma-bandhanaiḥ // 3.155	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dāridrya-roga-duḥkhāni bandhana-vyasanāni ca / ātmāparādha-vṛkṣasya phalāny etāni dehinām // 3.156	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmāt tvaṃ dveṣam utsṛjya mad-bandhana-samudbhavam / dharme manaḥ samādhāya pūjayainaṃ yathā-vidhi // 3.157	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasyās tad-vacanaṃ śrutvā dharma-yukti-samanvitam / upagamya tato 'dhṛṣṭaḥ kapotaḥ prāha lubdhakam // 3.158	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhadra susvāgataṃ te'stu brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te / santāpaś ca na kartavyaḥ sva-gṛhe vartate bhavān // 3.159	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasya tad-vacanaṃ śrutvā pratyuvāca vihaṅgamam / kapota khalu śītaṃ me hima-trāṇaṃ vidhīyatām // 3.160	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sa gatvāṅgārakaṃ nītvā pātayāmāsa pāvakam / tataḥ śuṣkeṣu parṇeṣu tam āśu samadīpayat // 3.161	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
susandīptaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tam āha śaraṇāgatam / pratāpayasva viśrabdhaṃ sva-gātrāṇy atra nirbhayaḥ // 3.162	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
udgatena ca jīvāmo vayaṃ sarve vanaukasaḥ / na cāsti vibhavaḥ kaścin nāśaye yena te kṣudham // 3.163	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sahasraṃ bharate kaścic chatamanyo daśāparaḥ / mama tv akṛta-puṇyasya kṣudrasyātmāpi durbharaḥ // 3.164	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekasyāpy atither annaṃ yaḥ pradātuṃ na śaktimān / tasyāneka-parikleśe gṛhe kiṃ vasataḥ phalam // 3.165	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tat tathā sādhayāmy etac charīraṃ duḥkha-jīvitam / yathā bhūyo na vakṣyāmi nāstīty arthi-samāgame // 3.166	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sa ninindi kilātmānaṃ na tu taṃ lubdhakaṃ punaḥ / uvāca tarpayiṣye tvāṃ muhūrtaṃ pratipālaya // 3.167	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evam uktvā sa dharmātmā prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā / tam agniṃ samparikramya praviveśa sva-veśmavat // 3.168	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tatas taṃ lubdhako dṛṣṭvā kṛpayā pīḍito bhṛśam / kapotam agnau patitaṃ vākyam etad abhāṣata // 3.169	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: bha-vipulā)
yaḥ karoti naraḥ pāpaṃ na tasyātmā dhruvaṃ priyaḥ / ātmanā hi kṛtaṃ pāpam ātmanaiva hi bhujyate // 3.170	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
so 'haṃ pāpa-matiś caiva pāpa-karma-rataḥ sadā / patiṣyāmi mahā-ghore narake nātra saṃśayaḥ // 3.171	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nūnaṃ mama nṛśaṃsasya pratyādarśaḥ sudarśitaḥ / prayacchatā sva-māṃsāni kapotena mahātmanā // 3.172	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
adya-prabhṛti dehaṃ svaṃ sarva-bhoga-vivarjitam / toyaṃ svalpaṃ yathā grīṣmaḥ śoṣayiṣyāmy ahaṃ punaḥ // 3.173	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śīta-vātātapa-sahaḥ kṛśāṅgo malinas tathā / upavāsair bahuvidhaiś cariṣye dharmam uttamam // 3.174	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: na-vipulā)
tato yaṣṭiṃ śalākāṃ ca jālakaṃ pañjaraṃ tathā / babhañja lubdhako dīnāṃ kāpotīṃ ca mumoca tām // 3.175	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
lubdhakena tato muktā dṛṣṭvāgnau patitaṃ patim / kapotī vilalāpārtā śoka-santapta-mānasā // 3.176	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na kāryam adya me nātha jīvitena tvayā vinā / dīnāyāḥ pati-hīnāyāḥ kiṃ nāryā jīvite phalam // 3.177	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
māno darpas tv ahaṅkāraḥ kulaṃ pūjā ca bandhuṣu / dāsa-bhṛtya-janeṣv ājñā vaidhavyena praṇaśyati // 3.178	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evaṃ vilapya bahuśaḥ kṛpaṇaṃ bhṛśa-duḥkhitā / pativratā susandīptaṃ tam evāgniṃ viveśa sā // 3.179	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
tato divyāmbara-dharā divyābharaṇa-bhūṣitā / bhartāraṃ sā vimānasthaṃ dadarśa svaṃ kapotikā // 3.180	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
so 'pi divya-tanur bhūtvā yathārtham idam abravīt / aho mām anugacchantyā kṛtaṃ sādhu śubhe tvayā // 3.181	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tisraḥ koṭyo 'rdha-koṭī ca yāni romāṇi mānuṣe / tāvat kālaṃ vaset svarge bhartāraṃ yānugacchati // 3.182	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kapota-dehaḥ sūryāste pratyahaṃ sukham anvabhūt / kapota-dehavatsāsīt prāk puṇya-prabhavaṃ hitam // 3.183	anuṣṭubh (1,2: ma-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
harṣāviṣṭas tato vyādho viveśa ca vanaṃ dhanam / prāṇi-hiṃsāṃ parityajya bahu-nirvedavān bhṛśam // 3.184	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tatra dāvānalaṃ dṛṣṭvā viveśa viratāśayaḥ / nirdagdha-kalmaṣo bhūtvā svarga-saukhyam avāptavān // 3.185	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yā mamodvijate nityaṃ sā mamādyāvagūhate / priya-kāraka bhadraṃ te yan mamāsti harasva tat // 3.186	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hartavyaṃ te na paśyāmi hartavyaṃ ced bhaviṣyati / punar apy āgamiṣyāmi yadīyaṃ nāvagūhate // 3.187	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śvetaṃ padaṃ śirasi yat tu śiroruhāṇāṃ sthānaṃ paraṃ paribhavasya tad eva puṃsām / āropitāsthi-śakalaṃ parihṛtya yānti cāṇḍāla-kūpam iva dūrataraṃ taruṇyaḥ // 3.188	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
gātraṃ saṅkucitaṃ gatir vigalitā dantāś ca nāśaṅgatā dṛṣṭir bhrāmyati rūpam apy upahataṃ vaktraṃ ca lālāyate / vākyaṃ naiva karoti bāndhava-janaḥ patnī na śuśrūṣate dhik kaṣṭaṃ jarayābhibhūta-pūruṣaṃ putro 'py avajñāyate // 3.189	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
śatravo 'pi hitārthaiva vivadantaḥ parasparam / caureṇa jīvitaṃ dattaṃ rākṣasena tu go-yugam // 3.190	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
parasparasya marmāṇi ye na rakṣanti jantavaḥ / ta eva nidhanaṃ yānti valmīkodara-sarpavat // 3.191	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
apūjyā yatra pūjyante pūjyānāṃ tu vimānanā / trīṇi tatra pravartante durbhikṣaṃ maraṇaṃ bhayam // 3.192	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- pratyakṣe'pi kṛte pāpe mūrkhaḥ sāmnā praśāmyati / ratha-kāraḥ svakāṃ bhāryāṃ sajārāṃ śirasāvahat // 3.193	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yadi syāt pāvakaḥ śītaḥ proṣṇī vā śaśa-lāñchanaḥ / strīṇāṃ tadā satītvaṃ syād yadi syād durjano hitaḥ // 3.194	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yac ca vedeṣu śāstreṣu na dṛṣṭaṃ na ca saṃśrutam / tat sarvaṃ vetti loko 'yaṃ yat syād brahmāṇḍa-madhyagam // 3.195	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durdivase ghana-timire varṣati jalade mahāṭavī-prabhṛtau / patyur videśa-gamane parama-sukhaṃ jaghana-capalāyāḥ // 3.196	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
mitra-rūpā hi ripavaḥ sambhāvyante vicakṣaṇaiḥ / ye hitaṃ vākyam utsṛjya viparītopasevinaḥ // 3.197	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- santo 'py arthā vinaśyanti deśa-kāla-virodhinaḥ / aprājñān mantriṇaḥ prāpya tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā // 3.198	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
sūryaṃ bhartāram utsṛjya parjanyaṃ mārutaṃ girim / sva-jātiṃ mūṣikā prāptā svajātir duratikramā // 3.199	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yady asya vihitaṃ bhojyaṃ na tat tasya praduṣyati / abhakṣye bahu-doṣaḥ syāt tasmāt kāryo na vyatyayaḥ // 3.200	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
bhakṣyaṃ yathā dvijātīnāṃ madyapānāṃ yathā haviḥ / abhakṣyaṃ bhakṣyatām eti tathānyeṣām api dvija // 3.201	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhakṣyaṃ bhakṣyatāṃ śreya abhakṣyaṃ tu mahad agham / tat kathaṃ māṃ vṛthācāra tvaṃ daṇḍayitum arhasi // 3.202	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca sama-loṣṭāśma-kāñcanaḥ / suhṛn-mitre hy udāsīno madhyastho dveṣya-bandhuṣu / sādhuṣv api ca pāpeṣu sama-buddhir viśiṣyate // 3.203	upajāti jagatī: ajñātam [12: jrtm], ajñātam [12: mrsB], ajñātam [12: yntr], ajñātam [12: yrBy]
sādhūnāṃ niravadyānāṃ sadācāra-vicāriṇām / yogī yuñjīta satataṃ satatam ātmānaṃ rahasi sthitaḥ // 3.204	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
muñca muñca pataty eko mā muñceti dvitīyakaḥ / ubhayoḥ patanaṃ dṛṣṭvā maunaṃ sarvārtha-sādhanam // 3.205	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sañcarantīha pāpāni yugeṣv anyeṣu dehinām / kalau tu pāpa-saṃyukte yaḥ karoti sa lipyate // 3.206	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ ca- āsanāc chayanād yānāt saṃgateś cāpi bhojanāt / kṛte sañcarate pāpaṃ taila-bindur ivāmbhasi // 3.207	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
janitā copanetā ca yas tu vidyāṃ prayacchati / anna-dātā bhaya-trātā pañcaite pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ // 3.208	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anūḍhā mandire yasya rajaḥ prāpnoti kanyakā / patanti pitaras tasya svarga-sthā api tair guṇaiḥ // 3.209	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
varaṃ varayate kanyā mātā vittaṃ pitā śrutam / bāndhavāḥ kulam icchanti miṣṭānnam itare janāḥ // 3.210	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yāvan na lajjate kanyā yāvat krīḍati pāṃsunā / yāvat tiṣṭhati go-mārge tāvat kanyāṃ vivāhayet // 3.211	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
mātā caiva pitā caiva jyeṣṭha-bhrātā tathaiva ca / trayas te narakaṃ yānti dṛṣṭvā kanyāṃ rajasvalām // 3.212	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kulaṃ ca śīlaṃ ca sanāthatāṃ ca vidyāṃ ca vittaṃ ca vapur vayaś ca / etān guṇān saptān sapta parīkṣya deyā kanyā budhaiḥ śeṣam acintanīyam // 3.213	indravajrā [11: ttjgg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
