hanyatām iti yenoktaṃ svāmino hita-vādinā / sa evaiko 'tra sarveṣāṃ nīti-śāstrārtha-tattva-vit // 3.215	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pūrvaṃ tāvad ahaṃ mūrkho dvitīyaḥ paśu-bandhakaḥ / tato rājā ca mantrī ca sarvaṃ vai mūrkha-maṇḍalam // 3.216	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anāgataṃ yaḥ kurute sa śobhate sa śocate yo na karoty anāgatam / vane vasann eva jarām upāgato bilasya vācā na kadāpi hi śrutā // 3.217	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
bhaya-santrasta-manasāṃ hasta-pādādikāḥ kriyāḥ / pravartante na vāṇī ca vepathuś cādhiko bhavet // 3.218	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
na dīrgha-darśino yasya mantriṇaḥ syur mahīpateḥ / kramāyātā dhruvaṃ tasya na cirāt syāt parikṣayaḥ // 3.219	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mantri-rūpā hi ripavaḥ sambhāvyās te vicakṣaṇaiḥ / ye santaṃ nayam utsṛjya sevante pratilomataḥ // 3.220	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
amitraṃ kurute mitraṃ mitraṃ dveṣṭi hinasti ca / śubhaṃ vetty aśubhaṃ pāpaṃ bhadraṃ daiva-hato naraḥ // 3.221	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śīghra-kṛtyeṣu kāryeṣu vilambayati yo naraḥ / tat kṛtyaṃ devatās tasya kopād vighnanty asaṃśayam // 3.222	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yasya yasya hi kāryasya phalitasya viśeṣataḥ / kṣipram akriyamāṇasya kālaḥ pibati tat-phalam // 3.223	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
vara-magnau pradīpte tu prapātaḥ puṇya-karmaṇām / na cārijana-saṃsargo muhūrtam api sevitaḥ // 3.224	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāryasyāpekṣayā bhuktaṃ viṣam apy amṛtāyate / sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ yatra nātra kāryā vicāraṇā // 3.225	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
upanata-bhaye yo yo mārgo hitārtha-karo bhavet- sa sa nipuṇayā buddhyā sevyo mahān kṛpaṇo 'pi vā / karikara-nibhau jyāghātā kau mahāstra-viśāradau valaya-racitau strīvad bāhū kṛtau na kirīṭinā // 3.226	hariṇī [17: nsmrslg]
śaktenāpi satā janena viduṣā kālāntarāpekṣiṇā vastavyaṃ khalu vākya-vajra-viṣame kṣudre'pi pāpe jane / darvī-vyagra-kareṇa dhūma-malinenāyāsa-yukte ca bhīmenātibalena matsya-bhavane kiṃ noṣitaṃ sūdavat // 3.227	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
yad vā tad vā viṣama-patitaḥ sādhu vā garhitaṃ vā kālāpekṣī hṛdaya-nihitaṃ buddhimān karma kuryāt / kiṃ gāṇḍīva-sphurad-uru-guṇāsphālana-krūra-pāṇir nāsīl līlā-naṭana-vilasan mekhalī savyasācī // 3.228	mandākrāntā [17: mBnttgg]
siddhiṃ prārthayatā janena viduṣā tejo nigṛhya svakaṃ sattvotsāhavatāpi daiva-vidhiṣu sthairyaṃ prakārya kramāt / devendra-draviṇeśvarāntaka-samair apy anvito bhrātṛbhiḥ kiṃ kliṣṭaḥ suciraṃ virāṭa-bhavane śrīmān na dharmātmajaḥ // 3.229	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
rūpābhijana-sampanno mādrī-putrau balānvitau / gokarma-rakṣā-vyāpāre virāṭa-preṣyatāṃ gatau // 3.230	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
rūpeṇāpratimena yauvana-guṇaiḥ śreṣṭhe kule janmanā kāntyā śrīr iva yātra sāpi vidaśāṃ kāla-kramād āgatā / sairandhrīti sa-garvitaṃ yuvatibhiḥ sākṣepam ākhyātayā draupadyā nanu matsya-rāja-bhavane dhṛṣṭaṃ na kiṃ candanam // 3.231	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
arito 'bhyāgato bhṛtyo duṣṭas tat-saṅga-tat-paraḥ / apasarpa-sadharmatvān nityodvegī ca dūṣitaḥ // 3.232	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
āsane śayane yāne pāna-bhojana-vastuṣu / dṛṣṭvāntaraṃ pramatteṣu praharanty arayo 'riṣu // 3.233	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena trivarga-nilayaṃ budhaḥ / ātmānam ādṛto rakṣet pramādād dhi vinaśyati // 3.234	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
santāpayanti kam apathya-bhujaṃ na rogā durmantriṇaṃ kam upayānti na nīti-doṣāḥ / kaṃ śrīr na darpayati kaṃ na nihanti mṛtyuḥ kaṃ svīkṛtā na viṣayā paripīḍayanti // 3.235	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
lubdhasya naśyati yaśaḥ piśunasya maitrī naṣṭa-kriyasya kula artha-parasya dharmaḥ / vidyā-phalaṃ vyasaninaḥ kṛpaṇasya saukhyaṃ rājyaṃ pramatta-sacivasya narādhipasya // 3.236	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
apamānaṃ puraskṛtya mānaṃ kṛtvā tu pṛṣṭhataḥ / svārtham abhyuddharet prājñaḥ kārya-dhvaṃso hi mūrkhatā // 3.237	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
skandhenāpi vahec chatruṃ kālam āsādya buddhimān / mahatā kṛṣṇa-sarpeṇa maṇḍūkā bahavo hatāḥ // 3.238	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na tathā kariṇā yānaṃ turageṇa rathena vā / nara-yānena vā yānaṃ yathā mandaviṣeṇa me // 3.239	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
maṇḍūkā vividhā hy ete chala-pūrvopasādhitāḥ / kiyantaṃ kālam akṣīṇā bhaveyuḥ khāditā mama // 3.240	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarvam etad vijānāmi yathā vāhyo 'smi darduraiḥ / kiñcit kālaṃ pratīkṣe'haṃ ghṛtāndho brāhmaṇo yathā // 3.241	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vane prajvalito vahnir dahan mūlāni rakṣati / samūlonmūlanaṃ kuryād vāyur yo mṛdu-śītalaḥ // 3.242	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mahattvam etan mahatāṃ nayālaṅkāra-dhāriṇām / na muñcanti yad ārabdhaṃ kṛcchre'pi vyasanodaye // 3.243	anuṣṭubh (1,2: bha-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
prārabhyate na khalu vighna-bhayena nīcaiḥ prārabhya vighna-vihatā viramanti madhyāḥ / vighnaiḥ sahasra-guṇitair api hanyamānāḥ prārabdham uttama-guṇā na parityajanti // 3.244	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
ṛṇa-śeṣaṃ cāgni-śeṣaṃ ca śatru-śeṣaṃ tathaiva ca / vyādhi-śeṣaṃ ca niḥśeṣaṃ kṛtvā prājño na sīdati // 3.245	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
śastrair hatā na hi hatā ripavo bhavanti prajñā-hatās tu ripavaḥ suhatā bhavanti / śastaṃ nihanti puruṣasya śarīram ekaṃ prajñā kulaṃ ca vibhavaś ca yaśaś ca hanti // 3.246	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
prasarati matiḥ kāryārambhe dṛḍhībhavati smṛtiḥ svayam upanayann arthān mantro na gacchati viplavam / sphurati saphalas tarkaś cittaṃ samunnatim aśnute bhavati ca ratiḥ ślāghye kṛtye narasya bhaviṣyataḥ // 3.247	hariṇī [17: nsmrslg]
tyāgini śūre viduṣi ca saṃsarga-rucir jano guṇī bhavati / guṇavati dhanaṃ dhanāc chrīḥ śrīmaty ājñā tato rājyam // 3.248	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tīkṣṇopāya-prāpti-gamyo 'pi yo 'rthas tasyāpy ādau saṃśrayaḥ sādhu yuktaḥ / uttuṅgāgraḥ sāra-bhūto vanānāṃ mānyābhyarcya cchidyate pādapendraḥ // 3.249	śālinī [11: mttgg]
aniścitair adhyavasāya-bhīrubhir yatheṣṭa-saṃlāpa-rati-prayojanaiḥ / phale visaṃvādam upāgatā giraḥ prayānti loke parihāsa-vastutām // 3.250	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
śakṣyāmi kartum idam alpam ayatna-sādhyam anādaraḥ ka iti kṛtyam upekṣamāṇāḥ / kecit pramatta-manasaḥ paritāpa-duḥkham āpat-prasaṅga-sulabhaṃ puruṣā prayānti // 3.251	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg] (? 3 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
niḥsarpe baddha-sarpe vā bhavane suṣyate sukham / sadā dṛṣṭa-bhujaṅge tu nidrā duḥkhena labhyate // 3.252	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vistīrṇa-vyavasāya-sādhya-mahatāṃ snighdopayuktāśiṣāṃ kāryāṇāṃ naya-sāhasonnati-matām icchāpad-ārohiṇām / mānotseka-parākrama-vyasaninaḥ pāraṃ na yāvad-gatāḥ sāmarṣe hṛdaye'vakāśa-viṣayā tāvat kathaṃ nirvṛtiḥ // 3.253	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
prajā na rañjayed yas tu rājā rakṣādibhir guṇaiḥ / ajāgala-stanasyeva tasya rājyaṃ nirarthakam // 3.254	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
guṇeṣu rāgo vyasaneṣv anādaro ratiḥ subhṛtyeṣu ca yasya bhūpateḥ / ciraṃ sa bhuṅkte cala-cāmarāṃśukāṃ sitātapatrābharaṇāṃ nṛpa-śriyam // 3.255	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
yadaiva rājye kriyate'bhiṣekas tadaiva buddhir vyasaneṣu yojyā / ghaṭā hi rājñām abhiṣeka-kāle sahāmbhasaivāpadam udgiranti // 3.256	upendravajrā [11: jtjgg]
rāmasya vrajanaṃ vane nivasanaṃ pāṇḍoḥ sutānāṃ vane vṛṣṇīnāṃ nidhanaṃ nalasya nṛpate rājyāt paribhraṃśanam / nāṭyācāryakam arjunasya patanaṃ sañcintya laṅkeśvare sarve kāla-vaśāj jano 'tra sahate kaḥ kaṃ paritrāyate // 3.257	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
kva sa daśarathaḥ svarge bhūtvā mahendra-suhṛd gataḥ kva sa jalanidher velāṃ baddhvā nṛpaḥ sagaras tathā / kva sa karatalāj jāto vainyaḥ kva sūrya-tanur manuḥ nanu balavatā kālenaite prabodhya nimīlitāḥ // 3.258	hariṇī [17: nsmrslg]
māndhātā kva gatas triloka-vijayī rājā kva satyavrataḥ devānāṃ nṛpatir gataḥ kva nahuṣaḥ sac-chāstravān keśavaḥ / manyante sarathāḥ sa-kuñjara-varāḥ śakrāsanādhyāsinaḥ kālenaiva mahātmanā tv anukṛtāḥ kālena nirvāsitāḥ // 3.259	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
api ca- sa ca nṛpatis te sacivās tāḥ pramadās tāni kānana-vanāni / sa ca te ca tāś ca tāni ca kṛtānta-dṛṣṭāni naṣṭāni // 3.260	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
samutpanneṣu kāryeṣu buddhir yasya na hīyate / sa eva durgaṃ tarati jalastho vānaro yathā // 4.1	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: bha-vipulā)
priyo vā yadi vā dveṣyo mūrkho vā yadi paṇḍitaḥ / vaiśvadevāntam āpannaḥ so 'tithiḥ svarga-saṅkramaḥ // 4.2	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na pṛcchec caraṇaṃ gotraṃ na ca vidyāṃ kulaṃ na ca / atithiṃ vaiśvadevānte śrāddhe ca manur abravīt // 4.3	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
dūra-mārga-śrama-śrāntaṃ vaiśvadevāntam āgatam / atithiṃ pūjayed yas tu sa yāti paramāṃ gatim // 4.4	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
apūjito 'tithir yasya gṛhād yāti viniḥśvasan / gacchanti pitaras tasya vimukhāḥ saha daivataiḥ // 4.5	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekaṃ prasūyate mātā dvitīyaṃ vāk prasūyate / vāg-jātam adhikaṃ procuḥ sodaryād api bāndhavāt // 4.6	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sāhlādaṃ vacanaṃ prayacchati na me no vāñchitaṃ kiñcana prāyaḥ procchvasiṣi drutaṃ hutavaha-jvālā samaṃ rātriṣu / kaṇṭhāśleṣa-parigrahe śithilatā yan nādarāc cumbase tat te dhūrta hṛdi sthitā priyatamā kācin mamevāparā // 4.7	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
mayi te pāda-patite kiṅkaratvam upāgate / tvaṃ prāṇa-vallabhe kasmāt kopane kopam eṣyasi // 4.8	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
sārdhaṃ manoratha-śatais tava dhūrta kāntā saiva sthitā manasi kṛtrima-bhāva-ramyā / asmākam asti na kathañcid ihāvakāśaṃ tasmāt kṛtaṃ caraṇa-pāta-viḍambanābhiḥ // 4.9	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
vajra-lepasya mūrkhasya nārīṇāṃ karkaṭasya ca / eko grahas tu mīnānāṃ nīlī-madya-payos tathā // 4.10	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
brahmaghne ca surāpe ca caure bhagna-vrate śaṭhe / niṣkṛtir vihitā sadbhiḥ kṛtaghne nāsti niṣkṛtiḥ // 4.11	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
varjayet kaulikākāraṃ mitraṃ prājñataro naraḥ / ātmanaḥ sammukhaṃ nityaṃ ya ākarṣati lolupaḥ // 4.12	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- dadāti pratigṛhṇāti guhyam ākhyāti pṛcchati / bhuṅkte bhojayate caiva ṣaḍ-vidhaṃ prīti-lakṣaṇam // 4.13	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na viśvased aviśvaste viśvaste'pi na viśvaset / viśvāsād bhayam utpannaṃ mūlāny api nikṛntati // 4.14	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sakṛd duṣṭaṃ ca yo mitraṃ punaḥ sandhātum icchati / sa mṛtyum upagṛhṇāti garbham aśvatarī yathā // 4.15	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bubhukṣitaḥ kiṃ na karoti pāpaṃ kṣīṇā janā niṣkaruṇā bhavanti / ākhyāhi bhadre priya-darśanasya na gaṅgadattaḥ punar eti kūpam // 4.16	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
āpadi yenāpakṛtaṃ yena ca hasitaṃ daśāsu viṣamāsu / apakṛtya tayor ubhayoḥ punar api jātaṃ naraṃ manye // 4.17	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
śatrubhir yojayec chatruṃ balinā balavattaram / sva-kāryāya yato na syāt kācit pīḍātra tat-kṣaye // 4.18	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- śatrum unmūlayet prājñas tīkṣṇaṃ tīkṣṇena śatruṇā / vyathā-karaṃ sukhārthāya kaṇṭakenaiva kaṇṭakam // 4.19	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya na jāyate śīlaṃ na kulaṃ na ca saṃśrayaḥ / na tena saṅgatiṃ kuryād ity uvāca bṛhaspatiḥ // 4.20	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yo yasya jāyate vadhyaḥ sa svapne'pi kathañcana / na tat-samīpam abhyeti tat kim evaṃ prajalpasi // 4.21	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarva-nāśe ca sañjāte prāṇānām api saṃśaye / api śatruṃ praṇamyāpi rakṣet prāṇāndhanāni ca // 4.22	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yac chakyaṃ grasituṃ yasya grastaṃ pariṇamec ca yat / hitaṃ ca pariṇāme yat tad ādyaṃ bhūtim icchatā // 4.23	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo hi prāṇa-parikṣīṇaḥ sahāya-parivarjitaḥ / sa hi sarva-sukhopāyāṃ vṛttim āracayed budhaḥ // 4.24	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo 'mitraṃ kurute mitraṃ vīryābhyadhikam ātmanaḥ / sa karoti na sandehaḥ svayaṃ hi viṣa-bhakṣaṇam // 4.25	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarvasva-haraṇe yuktaṃ śatruṃ buddhi-yutā narāḥ / toṣayanty alpa-dānena bāḍavaṃ sāgaro yathā // 4.26	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo durbalo 'ṇūn api yācyamāno balīyasā yacchati naiva sāmnā / prayacchate naiva ca darśyamānaṃ khārīṃ sa cūrṇasya punar dadāti // 4.27	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
tathā ca- sarva-nāśe samutpanne ardhaṃ tyajati paṇḍitaḥ / ardhena kurute kāryaṃ sarva-nāśo hi dustaraḥ // 4.28	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na svalpasya kṛte bhūri nāśayen matimān naraḥ / etad eva hi pāṇḍityaṃ yat svalpād bhūri-rakṣaṇam // 4.29	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yathā hi malinair vastrair yatra tatropaviśyate / evaṃ calita-vittas tu vitta-śeṣaṃ na rakṣati // 4.30	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ krandasi durākranda sva-pakṣa-kṣaya-kāraka / sva-pakṣasya kṣaye jāte ko nas trātā bhaviṣyati // 4.31	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bubhukṣitaḥ kiṃ na karoti pāpaṃ kṣīṇā narā niṣkaruṇā bhavanti / ākhyāhi bhadre priya-darśanasya na gaṅgadattaḥ punar eti kūpam // 4.32	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
āgataś ca gataś caiva gatvā yaḥ punar āgataḥ / akarṇa-hṛdayo mūrkhas tatraiva nidhanaṃ gataḥ // 4.33	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nāmṛtaṃ na viṣaṃ kiñcid ekāṃ muktvā nitambinīm / yasyāḥ saṅgena jīvyeta mriyate ca viyogataḥ // 4.34	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- yāsāṃ nāmnāpi kāmaḥ syāt saṅgamaṃ darśanaṃ vinā / tāsāṃ dṛk-saṅgamaṃ prāpya yan na dravati kautukam // 4.35	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
strī-mudrāṃ makaradhvajasya jayinīṃ sarvārdha-sampat-karīṃ te mūḍhāḥ pravihāya yānti kudhiyo mithyā-phalānveṣiṇaḥ / te tenaiva nihatya nirdayataraṃ nagnīkṛtā muṇḍitāḥ kecid rakta-paṭīkṛtāś ca jaṭilāḥ kāpālikāś cāpare // 4.36	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
jānann api naro daivāt prakaroti vigarhitam / karma kiṃ kasyacil loke garhitaṃ rocate katham // 4.37	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
svārtham utsṛjya yo dambhī satyaṃ brūte sumanda-dhīḥ / sa svārthād bhraśyate nūnaṃ yudhiṣṭhira ivāparaḥ // 4.38	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śūdraś ca kṛta-vighnaś ca darśanīyo 'si putraka / yasmin kule tvam utpanno gajas tatra na hanyate // 4.39	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
strī-vipraliṅgi-bāleṣu prahartavyaṃ na karhicit / prāṇa-tyāge'pi sañjāte viśvasteṣu viśeṣataḥ // 4.40	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
akṛtyaṃ naiva kartavyaṃ prāṇa-tyāge'py upasthite / na ca kṛtyaṃ parityājyam eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ // 4.41	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekenāpi sudhīreṇa sotsāhena raṇaṃ prati / sotsāhaṃ jāyate sainyaṃ bhagne bhaṅgam avāpnuyāt // 4.42	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- ata eva vāñchanti bhūpā yodhān mahābalān / śūrān vīrān kṛtotsāhān varjayanti ca kātarān // 4.43	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yad-arthe sva-kulaṃ tyaktaṃ jīvitārdhaṃ ca hāritam / sā māṃ tyajati niḥsnehā kaḥ strīṇāṃ viśvasen naraḥ // 4.44	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
na kiṃ dadyān na kiṃ kuryāt strībhir abhyarthito naraḥ / anaśvā yatra hreṣante śiraḥ parvaṇi muṇḍitam // 4.45	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
ātmano mukha-doṣeṇa badhyante śuka-sārikāḥ / bakās tatra na badhyante maunaṃ sarvārtha-sādhanam // 4.46	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- suguptaṃ rakṣyamāṇo 'pi darśayan dāruṇaṃ vapuḥ / vyāghra-carma-praticchanno vāk-kṛte rāsabho hataḥ // 4.47	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
gargo hi pāda-śaucāl laghv-āsana-dānato gataḥ somaḥ / dattaḥ kadaśana-bhojyāc chyāmalakaś cārdha-candreṇa // 4.48	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
pratyakṣe'pi kṛte pāpe mūrkhaḥ sāmnā praśāmyati / rathakāraḥ svakāṃ bhāryāṃ sajārāṃ śirasāvahat // 4.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nadīnāṃ ca kulānāṃ ca munīnāṃ ca mahātmanām / parīkṣā na prakartavyā strīṇāṃ duścaritasya ca // 4.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vasor vīryotpannām abhajata munir matsya-tanayāṃ tathā jāto vyāso śata-guṇa-nivāsaḥ kim aparam / svayaṃ vedān vyasyan śamita-kuru-vaṃśa-prasavitā sa evābhā̆c chrīmān ahaha viṣamā karma-gatayaḥ // 4.50	śikhariṇī [17: ymnsBlg]
yadi syāt pāvakaḥ śītaḥ proṣṇo vā śaśa-lāñchanaḥ / strīṇāṃ tadā satītvaṃ syād yadi syād durjano hitaḥ // 4.51	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yan na vedeṣu śāstreṣu na dṛṣṭaṃ na ca saṃśrutam / tat sarvaṃ vetti loko 'yaṃ yat syād brahmāṇḍa-madhyagam // 4.52	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durdivase ghana-timire duḥkha-cārāsu nagara-vīthīṣu / patyau videśa-yāte parama-sukhaṃ jaghana-capalāyāḥ // 4.53	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
sadbhiḥ sambodhyamāno 'pi durātmā pāpa-pauruṣaḥ / ghṛṣyamāṇa ivāṅgāro nirmalatvaṃ na gacchati // 4.54	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yā mamodvijate nityaṃ sādya mām avagūhate / priya-kāraka bhadraṃ te yan mamāsti harasva tat // 4.55	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śvetaṃ padaṃ śirasi yat tu śiroruhāṇāṃ sthānaṃ paraṃ paribhavasya tad eva puṃsām / āropitāsthi-śakalaṃ parihṛtya yānti cāṇḍāla-kūpam iva dūrataraṃ taruṇyaḥ // 4.56	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
gātraṃ saṅkucitaṃ gati-vigalitā dantāś ca nāśaṃ gatāh dṛṣṭir bhrāmyati rūpam eva hrasate vaktraṃ ca lālāyate / vākyaṃ naiva karoti bāndhava-janaḥ patnī na śuśrūṣate hā kaṣṭaṃ jarayābhibhūta-puruṣaḥ putrair avajñāyate // 4.57	upajāti atidhṛti: ajñātam [19: msnsttg], ajñātam [19: msysttg], śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] atha vā śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
na gṛhaṃ gṛham ity āhur gṛhiṇī gṛham ucyate / gṛhaṃ tu gṛhiṇī-hīnaṃ kāntārān nātiricyate // 4.58	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- vṛkṣa-mūle'pi dayitā yatra tiṣṭhati tad gṛham / prāsādo 'pi tayā hīno 'raṇya-sadṛśaḥ smṛtaḥ // 4.59	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
mātā yasya gṛhe nāsti bhāryā ca priya-vādinī / araṇyaṃ tena gantavyaṃ yathāraṇyaṃ tathā gṛham // 4.60	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yā bhāryā duṣṭa-caritrā satataṃ kalaha-priyā / bhāryā-rūpeṇa sā jñeyā vidagdhair dāruṇā jarā // 4.61	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmāt sarva-prayatnena nāmāpi parivarjayet / strīṇām iha hi sarvāsāṃ ya icchet sukham ātmanaḥ // 4.62	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yad-antas tan na jihvāyāṃ yaj jihvāyāṃ na tad-bahiḥ / yad-bahis tan na kurvanti vicitra-caritāḥ striyaḥ // 4.63	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ke nāma na vinaśyanti mithyā-jñānān nitambinīm / ramyāṃ te upasarpanti dīpābhāṃ śalabhā yathā // 4.64	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
antar-viṣa-mayā hy etā bahiś caiva manoramāḥ / guñjā-phala-samākārā yoṣitaḥ kena nirmitāḥ // 4.65	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāḍitā api daṇḍena śastrair api vikhaṇḍitāḥ / na vaśaṃ yoṣito yānti na dānair na ca saṃstavaiḥ // 4.66	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
āstāṃ tāvat kim anyena daurātmyeneha yoṣitām / vidhṛtaṃ svodareṇāpi ghnanti putram api svakam // 4.67	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rūkṣāyāṃ sneha-sad-bhāvaṃ kaṭhorāyāṃ sumārdavam / nīrasāyāṃ rasaṃ bālo bālikāyāṃ vikalpayet // 4.68	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yādṛśaṃ mama pāṇḍityaṃ tādṛśaṃ dviguṇaṃ tava / nābhūj jāro na bhartā ca kiṃ nirīkṣasi nagnike // 4.69	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
gṛdhreṇāpahṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ matsyo 'pi salilaṃ gataḥ / matsya-māṃsa-paribhraṣṭe kiṃ nirīkṣyasi jambuke // 4.70	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mitraṃ hy amitratāṃ yātam aparaṃ me priyā mitrā / gṛham anyena ca vyāptaṃ kim adyāpi bhaviṣyati // 4.71	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
athavā yuktam idam ucyate- kṣate prahārā nipatanty abhīkṣṇam anna-kṣaye vardhati jāṭharāgniḥ / āpatsu vairāṇi samudbhavanti vāme vidhau sarvam idaṃ narāṇām // 4.72	indravajrā [11: ttjgg] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
yaḥ pṛṣṭvā kurute kāryaṃ praṣṭavyān sva-hitān gurūn / na tasya jāyate vighnaḥ kasmiṃścid api karmaṇi // 4.73	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
satāṃ vacanam ādiṣṭaṃ madena na karoti yaḥ / sa vināśam avāpnoti ghaṇṭoṣṭra iva satvaram // 4.74	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
upadeśa-pradātṝṇāṃ narāṇāṃ hitam icchatām / parasminn iha loke ca vyasanaṃ nopapadyate // 4.75	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
upakāriṣu yaḥ sādhuḥ sādhutve tasya ko guṇaḥ / apakāriṣu yaḥ sādhuḥ sa sādhuḥ sadbhir ucyate // 4.76	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
hatas tvaṃ prāpsyasi svargaṃ jīvan gṛham atho yaśaḥ / yudhyamānasya te bhāvi guṇa-dvayam anuttamam // 4.77	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uttamaṃ praṇipātena śūraṃ bhedena yojayet / nīcam alpa-pradānena sama-śaktiṃ parākramaiḥ // 4.78	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
antyāvastho 'pi mahān svāmi-guṇān na jahāti śuddhatayā / na śveta-bhāvam ujjhati śaṅkhaḥ śikhi-bhukta-mukto 'pi // 4.79	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
na yatra śakyate kartuṃ sāma dānam athāpi vā / bhedas tatra prayoktavyo yataḥ sa vaśa-kārakaḥ // 4.80	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
antaḥ-sthenāviruddhena suvṛttenāticāruṇā / antar-bhinnena samprāptaṃ mauktikenāpi bandhanam // 4.81	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sambhāvyaṃ goṣu sampannaṃ sambhāvyaṃ brāhmaṇe tapaḥ / sambhāvyaṃ strīṣu cāpalyaṃ sambhāvyaṃ jātito bhayam // 4.82	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- subhikṣāṇi vicitrāṇi śithilāḥ paura-yoṣitaḥ / eko doṣo videśasya svajātir yad virudhyate // 4.83	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
akṛtvā pauruṣaṃ yā śrīḥ kiṃ tayālasa-bhāgyayā / kuraṅgo 'pi samaśnāti daivād upanataṃ tṛṇam // 4.84	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kudṛṣṭaṃ kuparijñātaṃ kuśrutaṃ kuparīkṣitam / tan nareṇa na kartavyaṃ nāpitenātra yat kṛtam // 5.1	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śīlaṃ śaucaṃ kṣāntir dākṣiṇyaṃ madhuratā kule janma / na virājanti hi sarve vitta-vihīnasya pusuṣasya // 5.2	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
māno vā darpo vā vijñānaṃ vibhramaḥ subuddhir vā / sarvaṃ praṇaśyati samaṃ vitta-vihīno yadā puruṣaḥ // 5.3	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
pratidivasaṃ yāti layaṃ vasanta-vātāhateva śiśira-śrīḥ / buddhir buddhimatām api kuṭumba-bhara-cintayā satatam // 5.4	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
naśyati vipulamater api buddhiḥ puruṣasya manda-vibhavasya / ghṛta-lavaṇa-taila-taṇḍula-vastrendhana-cintayā satatam // 5.5	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
gaṇanam iva naṣṭa-tārakaṃ suṣkam iva saraḥ śmaśānam iva raudram / priya-darśanam api rūkṣaṃ bhavati gṛhaṃ dhana-vihīnasya // 5.6	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
na vibhāvyante laghavo vitta-vihīnāḥ puro 'pi nivasantaḥ / satataṃ jāta-vinaṣṭāḥ payasām iva budbudāḥ payasi // 5.7	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
sukulaṃ kuśalaṃ sujanaṃ vihāya kula-kuśala-śīla-vikale'pi / āḍhye kalpa-tarāv iva nityaṃ rajyanti jana-nivahāḥ // 5.8	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
viphalam iha pūrva-sukṛtaṃ vidyāvanto 'pi kula-samudbhūtāḥ / yasya yadā vibhavaḥ syāt tasya tadā dāsatāṃ yānti // 5.9	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
laghur ayam āha na lokaḥ kāmaṃ garjantam api patiṃ payasām / sarvam alajjākaram iha yad yat kurvanti paripūrṇāḥ // 5.10	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
vyādhitena sa-śokena cintā-grastena jantunā / kāmārtenātha mattena dṛṣṭaḥ svapno nirarthakaḥ // 5.11	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jayanti te jinā yeṣāṃ kevala-jñāna-śālinām / ā janmanaḥ smarotpattau mānasenoṣarāyitam // 5.12	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anyac ca- sā jihvā yā jinaṃ stauti tac-cittaṃ yaj jine ratam / tau eva tu karau ślāghyau yau tat-pūjā-karau karau // 5.13	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
dhyāna-vyājam upetya cintayasi kām unmīlya cakṣuḥ kṣaṇaṃ paśyānaṅga-śarāturaṃ janam imaṃ trātāpi no rakṣasi / mithyā-kāruṇiko 'si nirghṛṇataras tvattaḥ kuto 'nyaḥ pumān serṣyaṃ māra-vadhūbhir ity abhihito bauddho jinaḥ pātu vaḥ // 5.14	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
ekākī gṛha-santyaktaḥ pāṇi-pātro digambaraḥ / so 'pi sambādhyate loke tṛṣṇayā paśya kautukam // 5.15	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
jīryante jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ / cakṣuḥ śrotre ca jīryete tṛṣṇaikā taruṇāyate // 5.16	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kukkuṭaṃ kuparijñātaṃ kuśrutaṃ kuparīkṣitam / tan nareṇa na kartavyaṃ nāpitenātra yat kṛtam // 5.16	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
aparīkṣya na kartavyaṃ kartavyaṃ suparīkṣitam / paścād bhavati santāpo brāhmaṇī nakulaṃ yathā // 5.17	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kuputro 'pi bhavet puṃsāṃ hṛdayānanda-kārakaḥ / durvinītaḥ kurūpo 'pi mūrkho 'pi vyasanī khalaḥ // 5.18	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
evaṃ ca bhāṣate lokaś candanaṃ kila śītalam / putra-gātrasya saṃsparśaś candanād atiricyate // 5.19	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sauhṛdasya na vāñchanti janakasya hitasya ca / lokāḥ prapālakasyāpi yathā putrasya bandhanam // 5.20	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
atilobho na kartavyaḥ kartavyas tu pramāṇataḥ / atilobhaja-doṣeṇa jambuko nidhanaṃ gataḥ // 5.21	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
varaṃ vanaṃ vyāghra-gajādi-sevitaṃ janena hīnaṃ bahu-kaṇṭakāvṛtam / tṛṇāni śayyā paridhāna-valkalaḥ na bandhu-madhye dhana-hīna-jīvitam // 5.22	vaṃśastha [12: jtjr]
svāmī dveṣṭi susevito 'pi sahasā projjhanti sad-bāndhavāḥ rājante na guṇās tyajanti tanujāḥ sphārībhavanty āpadaḥ / bhāryā sādhu suvaṃśajāpi bhajate no yānti mitrāṇi ca nyāyāropita-vikramāṇy api nṛṇāṃ yeṣāṃ na hi syād dhanam // 5.23	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
śūraḥ surūpaḥ subhagaś ca vāgmī śastrāṇi śāstrāṇi vidāṃkarotu / arthaṃ vinā naiva yaśaś ca mānaṃ prāpnoti martyo 'tra manuṣya-loke // 5.24	indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
tānīndriyāṇy avikalāni tad eva nāma sā buddhir apratihatā vacanaṃ tad eva / arthoṣmaṇā virahitaḥ puruṣaḥ sa eva bāhyaḥ kṣaṇena bhavatīti vicitram etat // 5.25	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
satyaṃ parityajati muñcati bandhu-vargaṃ śīghraṃ vihāya jananīm api janma-bhūmim / santyajya gacchati videśam abhīṣṭa-lokaṃ cintākulīkṛta-matiḥ puruṣo 'tra loke // 5.26	vasantatilakā [14: tBjjgg]
duṣprāpyāṇi bahūni ca labhyante vāñchitāni draviṇāni / avasara-tulitābhir alaṃ tanubhiḥ sāhasika-puruṣāṇām // 5.27	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tathā ca- patati kadācin nabhasaḥ khāte pātālato 'pi jalam eti / daivam acintyaṃ balavad balavān nanu puruṣakāro 'pi // 5.28	ajñātasamavṛtta [10: jnyl] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
abhimata-siddhir aśeṣā bhavati hi puruṣasya puruṣakāreṇa / daivam iti yadapi kathayasi puruṣa-guṇaḥ so 'py adṛṣṭākhyaḥ // 5.29	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
bhayam atulaṃ guru-lokāt tṛṇam iva tulayanti sādhu sāhasikāḥ / prāṇān adbhutam etac cārtiṃ caritaṃ hy udārāṇām // 5.30	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
kleśasyāṅgam adattvā sukham eva sukhāni neha labhyante / madhubhin mathanāyas tair āśliṣyati bāhubhir lakṣmīm // 5.31	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
tasya kathaṃ na calā syāt patnī viṣṇor nṛsiṃhakasyāpi māsāṃś caturo nidrāṃ yaḥ sevati jala-gataḥ satatam // 5.32	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
duradhigamaḥ para-bhāgo yāvat puruṣeṇa sāhasaṃ na kṛtam / jayati tulām adhirūḍho bhāsvān iha jalada-paṭalāni // 5.33	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
mahānta eva mahatām arthaṃ sādhayituṃ kṣamāḥ / ṛte samudrād anyaḥ ko bibharti baḍavānalam // 5.34	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
varaṃ buddhir na sā vidyā vidyāyā buddhir uttamā / buddhi-hīno vinaśyanti yathā te siṃha-kārakāḥ // 5.35	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kiṃ tayā kriyate lakṣmyā yā vadhūr iva kevalā / yā na veśyeva sāmānyā pathikair upabhujyate // 5.36	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- ayaṃ nijaḥ paro veti gaṇanā laghu-cetasām / udāra-caritānāṃ tu vasudhaiva kuṭumbakam // 5.37	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
api śāstreṣu kuśalā lokācāra-vivarjitāḥ / sarve te hāsyatāṃ yānti yathā te mūrkha-paṇḍitāḥ // 5.38	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
utsave vyasane prāpte durbhikṣe śatru-saṅkaṭe / rāja-dvāre śmaśāne ca yas tiṣṭhati sa bāndhavaḥ // 5.39	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sarva-nāśe samutpanne ardhaṃ tyajati paṇḍitaḥ / ardhena kurute kāryaṃ sarva-nāśo hi duḥsahaḥ // 5.40	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
subuddhayo vinaśyanti duṣṭa-daivena nāśitāḥ / svalpa-dhīr api tasmiṃs tu kule nandati santatam // 5.41	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
uktaṃ ca- arakṣitaṃ tiṣṭhati daiva-rakṣitaṃ surakṣitaṃ daiva-hataṃ vinaśyati / jīvaty anātho 'pi vane visarjitaḥ kṛta-prayatno 'pi gṛhe na jīvati // 5.42	ajñātasamavṛtta [15: rjtjB] (? 2 eva pādāḥ yuktāḥ)
tathā ca- śatabuddhiḥ śirastho 'yaṃ lambate ca sahasra-dhīḥ / eka-buddhir ahaṃ bhadre krīḍāmi vimale jale // 5.43	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
sarpāṇāṃ ca khalānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ duṣṭa-cetasām / abhiprāyā na sidhyanti tenedaṃ vartate jagat // 5.44	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
buddher buddhimatāṃ loke nāsty agamyaṃ hi kiñcana / buddhyā yato hatā nandāś cāṇakyenāsi-pāṇayaḥ // 5.45	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā- na yatrāsti gatir vāyo raśmīnāṃ ca vivasvataḥ / tatrāpi praviśaty āśu buddhir buddhimatāṃ sadā // 5.46	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
na yat svarge'pi saukhyaṃ syād divya-sparśena śobhane / kusthāne'pi bhavet puṃsāṃ janmano yatra sambhavaḥ // 5.47	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
śatabuddhiḥ śiraḥstho 'yaṃ lambate ca sahasradhīḥ / ekabuddhir ahaṃ bhadre krīḍāmi vimale jale // 5.48	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sādhu mātula gītena mayā prokto 'pi na sthitaḥ / apūrvo 'yaṃ maṇir baddhaḥ samprāptaṃ gīta-lakṣaṇam // 5.49	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kāṃsī vivarjayec cauryaṃ nidrāluś cet sa puṃścalīm / jihvā-laulyaṃ ca rujākrānto jīvitaṃ yo 'tra vāñchati // 5.50	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
śaraj-jyotsnāhate dūraṃ tamasi priya-sannidhau / dhanyānāṃ viśati śrotre gīta-jhaṅkāra-jā sudhā // 5.51	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rāsabha āha-dhig dhiṅ mūrkha ! kim ahaṃ na jānāsi gītam ? tad yathā tasya bhedān śṛṇu- sapta svarās trayo grāmā mūrcchatāś caikatriṃśatiḥ / tānās tv ekonapaūcāśat tisro mātrā layās trayaḥ // 5.52	na kiṃcid adhyavasitam
sthāna-trayaṃ yatīnāṃ ca ṣaḍ-asyāni rasā nava / rāgā ṣaṭ-triṃśatir bhāvāś catvāriṃśat tataḥ smṛtāḥ // 5.53	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
pañcāśīty-adhikaṃ hy etad gītāṅgānāṃ śataṃ smṛtam / svayam eva purā proktaṃ bharatena śruteḥ param // 5.54	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
nānyad gītāt priyaṃ loke devānām api dṛśyate / śuṣka-snāyu-svarāhlādāt try-akṣaṃ jagrāha rāvaṇaḥ // 5.55	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sārameyasya cāśvasya rāsabhasya viśeṣataḥ / muhūrtāt paratau na syāt prahāra-janitā vyathā // 5.56	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
sādhu mātula gītena mayā prokto 'pi na sthitaḥ / apūrvo 'pi maṇir baddhaḥ sāmprataṃ gīta-lakṣaṇam // 5.57	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yasya nāsti svayaṃ prajñā mitroktaṃ na karoti yaḥ / sa eva nidhanaṃ yāti yathā manthara-kolikaḥ // 5.58	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
rājā dāna-paro nityam iha kīrtim avāpya ca / tat prabhāvāt punaḥ svargaṃ spardhate tridaśaiḥ saha // 5.59	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
bhojanācchādane dadyād ṛtu-kāle ca saṅgamam / bhūṣaṇādyaṃ ca nārīṇāṃ na tābhir mantrayet sudhīḥ // 5.60	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yatra strī yatra kitavo bālo yatra praśāsitā / tad gṛhaṃ kṣayam āyāti bhārgavo hīdam abravīt // 5.61	anuṣṭubh (1,2: na-vipulā, 3,4: pathyā)
tāvat syāt suprasannāsyas tāvad guru-jane rataḥ / puruṣo yoṣitāṃ yāvan na śṛṇoti vaco rahaḥ // 5.62	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
etāḥ svārtha-parā nāryaḥ kevalaṃ sva-sukhe ratāḥ / na tāsāṃ vallabhaḥ ko 'pi suto 'pi sva-sukhaṃ vinā // 5.63	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
cāraṇair vandibhir nīcair nāpitair bālakair api / na mantraṃ maitmān kuryāt sārdhaṃ bhikṣubhir eva ca // 5.64	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
yadaiva rājye kriyate'bhiṣekas tadaiva yāti vyasaneṣu buddhiḥ / ghaṭā nṛpāṇām abhiṣeka-kāle sahāmbhasaivāpadam udgiranti // 5.65	upendravajrā [11: jtjgg]
rāmasya vrajanaṃ vane nivasanaṃ pāṇḍoḥ sutānāṃ vane vṛṣṇīnāṃ nidhanaṃ nalasya nṛpate rājyāt paribhraṃśanam / saudāsaṃ tad-avastham arjuna-vadhaṃ sañcintya laṅkeśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā rājya-kṛte viḍambana-gataṃ tasmān na tad vāñchayet // 5.66	śārdūlavikrīḍitā [19: msjsttg]
yad-arthaṃ bhrātaraḥ putrā api vāñchanti ye nijāḥ / vadhaḥ rājya-kṛtāṃ rājñāṃ tad rājyaṃ dūratas tyajet // 5.67	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
anāgatavatīṃ cintām asambhāvyāṃ karoti yaḥ / sa eva pāṇḍuraḥ śete soma-śarma-pitā yathā // 5.68	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yo laulyāt kurute naivodarkam avekṣate / viḍambanām avāpnoti sa yathā candra-bhūpatiḥ // 5.69	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
meṣeṇa sūpakārāṇāṃ kalaho yatra jāyate / sa bhaviṣyaty asandigdhaṃ vānarāṇāṃ kṣayāvahaḥ // 5.70	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tasmāt syāt kalaho yatra gṛhe nityam akāraṇaḥ / tad-gṛhaṃ jīvitaṃ vāñchan dūrataḥ parivarjayet // 5.71	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kalahāntāni harmyāṇi kuvākyāntaṃ ca sauhṛdam / kurājāntāni rāṣṭrāṇi kukarmāntaṃ yaśo nṛṇām // 5.72	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
vadanaṃ daśanair hīnaṃ lālā sravati nityaśaḥ / na matiḥ sphurati kvāpi bāle vṛddhe viśeṣataḥ // 5.73	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
mitraṃ vyasana-samprāptaṃ sva-sthānaṃ para-pīḍanam / dhanyās te ye na paśyanti deśa-bhaṅgaṃ kula-kṣayam // 5.74	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kapīnāṃ medasā doṣo vahni-dāha-samudbhavā / aśvānāṃ nāśam abhyeti tamaḥ sūryodaye yathā // 5.75	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
marṣayed dharṣaṇāṃ yo 'tra vaṃśajāṃ para-nirmitām / bhayād vā yadi vā kāmāt sa jñeyaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ // 5.76	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tṛṣṇe devi namas tubhyaṃ yayā vittānvitā api / akṛtyeṣu niyojyante bhrāmante durgameṣv api // 5.77	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
tathā ca- icchati śatī sahasraṃ sahasrī lakṣam īhate / lakṣādhipas tathā rājyaṃ rājyasthaḥ svargam īhate // 5.78	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
jīryante jīryataḥ keśāḥ dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ / jīryataś cakṣuṣī śrotre tṛṣṇaikā taruṇāyate // 5.79	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
kṛte pratikṛtaṃ kuryād dhiṃsite pratihiṃsitam / na tatra doṣaṃ paśyāmi yo duṣṭe duṣṭam ācaret // 5.80	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
hataḥ śatruḥ kṛtaṃ mitraṃ ratna-mālā na hāritā / nālena pibatā toyaṃ bhavatā sādhu vānara // 5.81	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yas tyaktvā sāpadaṃ mitraṃ yāti niṣṭhuratāṃ vahan / kṛtaghnas tena pāpena narake yāty asaṃśayam // 5.82	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yādṛśī vadana-cchāyā dṛśyate tava vānara / vikālena gṛhīto 'si yaḥ paraiti sa jīvati // 5.83	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yādṛśī vacana-cchāyā dṛśyate tava vānara / vikālena gṛhīto 'si yaḥ paraiti sa jīvati // 5.84	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
durgas trikūṭaḥ parikhā samudro rakṣāṃsi yodhā dhanadāc ca vittam / śāstraṃ ca yasyośanasā praṇītaṃ sa rāvaṇo daiva-vaśād vipannaḥ // 5.85	upajāti : upendravajrā [11: jtjgg], indravajrā [11: ttjgg]
tathā ca- andhakaḥ kubjakaś caiva tristanī rāja-kanyakā / trayo 'py anyāyataḥ siddhāḥ saṃmukhe karmaṇi sthite // 5.86	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
yaḥ satataṃ paripṛcchati śṛṇoti sandhārayaty aniśam / tasya divākara-kiraṇair nalinīva vivardhate buddhiḥ // 5.87	upagīti (12, 15, 12, 15)
tathā ca- pṛcchakena sadā bhāvyaṃ puruṣeṇa vijānatā / rākṣasendra-gṛhīto 'pi praśnān mukto dvijaḥ purā // 5.88	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
hīnāṅgī vādhikāṅgī vā yā bhavet kanyakā nṛṇām / bhartuḥ syāt sā vināśāya sva-śīla-nidhanāya ca // 5.89	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yā punas tristanī kanyā yāti locana-gocaram / pitaraṃ nāśaty eva sā drutaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ // 5.90	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: asamīcīna)
lajjā snehaḥ svara-madhuratā buddhayo yauvana-śrīḥ kāntāsaṅgaḥ svajana-mamatā duḥkha-hānir vilāsaḥ / dharmaḥ śāstraṃ sura-guru-matiḥ śaucam ācāra-cintā pūrṇe sarve jaṭhara-piṭhare prāṇināṃ sambhavanti // 5.91	mandākrāntā [17: mBnttgg]
andho vā vadhiro vātha kuṣṭī vāpy antyajo 'pi vā / parigṛhṇātu tāṃ kanyāṃ sa-lakṣāṃ syād videśagaḥ // 5.92	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
yadi syāc chrī-talo vahniś candramā dahanātmakaḥ / susvādaḥ sāgaraḥ strīṇāṃ tat-satīs tvaṃ prajāyate // 5.93	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekodarāḥ pṛthag grīvā anyānya-phala-bhakṣiṇaḥ / asaṃhatā vinaśyanti bhāruṇḍā iva pakṣiṇaḥ // 5.94	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
ekaḥ svādu na bhuñjīta ekaś cārthān na cintayet / eko na gacched adhvānaṃ naikaḥ supteṣu jāgṛyāt // 5.95	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: ma-vipulā)
api ca- api kāpuruṣo mārge dvitīyaḥ kṣema-kārakaḥ / karkaṭena dvitīyena jīvitaṃ parirakṣitam // 5.96	anuṣṭubh (1,2: asamīcīna, 3,4: pathyā)
kṣīṇaḥ śrayati śaśī ravim ṛddho vardhayati payasāṃ nātham / anye vipadi sahāyā dhanināṃ śriyam anubhavanty anye // 5.97	āryā (12, 18, 12, 15)
mantre tīrthe dvije deve daivajñe bheṣaje gurau / yādṛśī bhāvanā yasya siddhir bhavati tādṛśī // 5.98	anuṣṭubh (1,2: pathyā, 3,4: pathyā)
